# astro-ph.HE [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [The Life and Death of Stars That Capture Primordial Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02700)
*Ore Gottlieb,Matteo Cantiello,Cameron Norton,Ken Van Tilburg,Matthew Kleban*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究首次建立了恒星捕获小行星质量段原初黑洞（PBH）后演化的全局框架，发现系统命运分岔为“爆炸性瓦解”与“安静吞噬”两类，并预测了可观测的瞬变信号及残余黑洞特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小行星质量段（$10^{17}-10^{23}\,{\rm g}$）的原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）仍是可行的暗物质候选体，它们可以被恒星捕获。然而，恒星捕获PBH后的演化过程此前缺乏全局理论框架，该研究旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 结合解析计算（analytic calculations）、恒星演化模型（stellar evolution models）、三维广义相对论磁流体力学模拟（3D general-relativistic magnetohydrodynamic simulations）以及蒙特卡洛星族合成（Monte Carlo population synthesis），建立了首个恒星捕获PBH后演化的全局框架。

Result: 系统命运分岔为两类：形成吸积盘（accretion disk）并在吞噬宿主前驱动爆炸性瓦解（explosive disruption），或捕获过晚/增长过慢而安静吞噬（quiet consumption）。捕获主要通过与行星或恒星伴星的三体相互作用（three-body interactions）实现。对类太阳宿主与类木星伴星，在主序寿命内旋入（inspiral）需要$M_{\rm BH}^{\rm crit}\gtrsim 10^{22}\,{\rm g}$。盘形成是不可逆节点：盘风与相对论性喷流（relativistic jets）$\sim10^{45}-10^{50}\,{\rm erg\,s^{-1}}$可在数分钟内瓦解恒星。瞬变信号包括持续约一天的紫外/蓝光信号、射电余晖，以及可能的X射线闪/低光度伽马射线暴（XRF/llGRB）。若PBH暗物质占比$O(1)$且捕获假设乐观，事件率可达llGRB水平。残余黑洞质量$M_{\rm BH}\sim0.01-1\,M_\odot$，高自旋$a_\ast\approx0.8$。

Conclusion: 该框架揭示了恒星捕获PBH后演化的双分支行为，预测了可观测的瞬变电磁信号，并指出低质量高自旋的残余黑洞可作为PBH的互补探针，以及亚太阳质量黑洞并合（subsolar BH mergers）的可能来源。

Abstract: Primordial black holes (PBHs) in the asteroid mass window ($10^{17}-10^{23}\,{\rm g}$) remain viable dark matter candidates and can be captured by stars. We develop the first global framework for the evolution of stars that capture PBHs, combining analytic calculations, stellar evolution models, 3D general-relativistic magnetohydrodynamic simulations, and Monte Carlo population synthesis. We find that the fate of these systems bifurcates: PBHs that form an accretion disk before consuming the host drive explosive disruption, whereas PBHs captured too late or growing too slowly consume the star quietly. Capture is dominated by three-body interactions with planetary or stellar companions. For a solar-type host with a Jupiter analog, inspiral within a main-sequence lifetime requires $M_{\rm BH}^{\rm crit}\gtrsim 10^{22}\,{\rm g}$, while lighter PBHs generally require tighter companions. Once deposited at the center, the PBH grows through inefficient quasi-spherical Bondi accretion; if it reaches the angular-momentum threshold before consuming the host, the inflow circularizes into a disk. Our Monte Carlo calculations yield sizable quiet-consumption and explosive-disruption populations, with final PBH masses $M_{\rm BH}\sim0.01-1\,M_\odot$ and disk-forming PBH spins $a_\ast\approx0.8$. Disk formation is the point of no return: disk winds and relativistic jets of $\sim10^{45}-10^{50}\,{\rm erg\,s^{-1}}$ disrupt the star within minutes. The resulting transients may include a $\sim$day-long UV/blue signal, radio afterglow, and, if the jet escapes, an X-ray-flash/low-luminosity gamma-ray-burst (XRF/llGRB) signal. For an $O(1)$ PBH dark matter fraction and optimistic capture assumptions, the event rate can reach that of llGRBs. The low-mass, high-spin remnants offer a complementary PBH probe and possible source for subsolar BH mergers.

</details>


### [2] [Targeting black holes from metal-poor progenitors with next-generation gravitational-wave detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03776)
*Federico Leto di Priolo,Martyna Chruślińska,Davide Gerosa*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文针对下一代引力波探测器（如爱因斯坦望远镜和宇宙探测器）如何探测宇宙黎明时期双黑洞并合的问题，引入“目标红移”（target redshift, $z_t$）概念，用于分离低金属丰度环境形成的并合事件，并建立统计框架以检验天体物理预测与观测数据之间的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 下一代引力波探测器能探测到宇宙黎明时期的双黑洞并合事件，但近邻宇宙观测到的并合事件混杂了不同宇宙历史时期和不同天体物理环境的系统。铁族元素（iron-group elements）通过金属丰度（metallicity）显著影响恒星演化并在黑洞种群中留下印记，因此需要一种方法将这些来自不同金属丰度环境的并合事件区分开来。

Method: 引入“目标红移”（target redshift, $z_t$）概念，定义为超过90%的恒星形成发生在金属丰度 $Z < 0.1\,Z_\odot$ 的宇宙纪元。$z_t$ 的确定依赖于对宇宙恒星形成率密度（cosmic star-formation rate density）作为铁丰度函数的重建，该重建因采用不同经验标度关系（empirical scaling relations）而存在非唯一性。进一步构建统计框架，用于快速检验天体物理预测与下一代引力波探测器预期观测数据之间的匹配程度。

Result: 目标红移 $z_t$ 的取值范围因模型变化而广泛分布，从 $z_t \sim 4$ 到 $z_t > 10$。通过量化目标红移与近邻宇宙之间双黑洞并合率密度（binary black-hole merger-rate density）的差异，该统计方法能够描绘参数空间中的演化趋势，并估算区分真实天体物理变化与统计涨落所需的探测统计量。

Conclusion: 该统计框架能够系统地将低金属丰度环境产生的双黑洞并合事件从近邻宇宙的混合样本中分离出来，并评估不同天体物理模型在下一代引力波探测器数据中的可区分性，为未来的引力波天文学观测提供了理论分析工具。

Abstract: Next-generation gravitational-wave detectors such as the Einstein Telescope and Cosmic Explorer will be able to detect binary black-hole mergers out to the cosmic dawn. Mergers observed in the local Universe represent a mixture of systems formed across the entire cosmic history, spanning a wide range of astrophysical environments. Iron-group elements govern metallicity effects on stellar evolution, making metallicity a key tracer that leaves a strong imprint on the black-hole population. We introduce the concept of a "target" redshift, $z_t$, defined as the epoch at which more than 90% of stars form with metallicity $Z < 0.1\,Z_\odot$. This provides a straightforward way to isolate mergers originating from metal-poor environments. The determination of $z_t$ relies on the reconstruction of the cosmic star-formation rate density as a function of iron abundance. This reconstruction is not unique, as it depends on the combination of different empirical scaling relations. Consequently, $z_t$ spans a broad range, from $z_t \sim 4$ to $z_t > 10$, depending on the adopted model variation. We present a statistical framework that enables rapid tests of astrophysical predictions against forecasted observations from next-generation gravitational-wave detectors. By quantifying variations in the binary black-hole merger-rate density between the target redshift and the local Universe, our approach maps evolutionary trends across parameter space and estimates the detection statistics required to distinguish genuine astrophysical variations from statistical fluctuations.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.dis-nn'></div>

# cond-mat.dis-nn [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [High-Dimensional Latents Should Be Diagnosed Through Phase Structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02600)
*Alejandro Ascarate,Leo Lebrat,Rodrigo Santa Cruz,Clinton Fookes,Olivier Salvado*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过自旋玻璃理论（spin-glass theory）的视角分析自编码器（AE）和变分自编码器（VAE）的潜空间（latent space），形式化了潜空间-自旋玻璃字典，并展示了将潜系统驱动至拓扑平凡化（topological trivialization）的临界边界能够改善生成和异常检测性能，从而提出一种相位感知（phase-aware）的评估范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自编码器评估多依赖标准机器学习指标（如重构损失），缺乏对潜空间全局几何结构及其物理相态（ordered/disordered/edge-of-stability）的系统理解，而不同相态可能直接影响下游任务（生成和异常检测）的成败。

Method: 首先，形式化潜空间-自旋玻璃字典：在固定解码器（decoder）条件下，重构项与超球坐标先验（hyperspherical coordinates prior）共同在潜球面上诱导出一个哈密顿量（Hamiltonian），其中潜坐标扮演连续自旋（continuous spins）角色，先验充当外磁场（external magnetic field）。据此引入自旋玻璃诊断工具——重叠分布（overlap distributions）、磁化率（susceptibility）和块自旋粗粒化（block-spin coarse-graining）——来检测潜表示中不同相态。其次，通过调整先验迫使潜系统进入拓扑平凡化临界边界，并在CIFAR-10、CelebA64等数据集上验证其对生成和异常检测的影响。

Result: 在生成任务中，超球压缩（hyperspherical compression）改善了重构-生成权衡，在CIFAR-10和CelebA64上获得更低的自FID（self-FID）同时保持或提升重构质量。在异常检测中，半有序潜几何（semi-ordered latent geometry）提升了全无监督和条件式分布外检测（OOD detection）性能，涵盖真实世界数据集（Mars Rover、Galaxy Zoo）以及CIFAR-10/100和Imagenette基准。

Conclusion: 主张对AE/VAE采用相位感知的评估范式，让自旋玻璃可观测量（spin-glass observables）作为标准机器学习指标的补充，揭示潜空间相态对下游任务成功或失败的根本影响。

Abstract: We study autoencoder and variational-autoencoder latent spaces through the lens of spin-glass theory. The paper has two components. First, we formalize a latent-space spin-glass dictionary: for a fixed decoder, the reconstruction term together with a hyperspherical coordinates prior induces a Hamiltonian on the latent sphere, where latent coordinates play the role of continuous spins and the prior acts as an external magnetic field. This allows us to import operational spin-glass diagnostics -- overlap distributions, susceptibility, and block-spin coarse-graining -- to detect ordered, disordered, and edge-of-stability phases in trained latent representations. Second, we show that deliberately driving the latent system toward the edge-of-stability of the topological trivialization regime has concrete downstream consequences. In generation, hyperspherical compression improves the reconstruction-generation trade-off on CIFAR-10 and CelebA64, yielding lower self-FID while preserving or improving reconstruction. In anomaly detection, the same semi-ordered latent geometry improves both fully unsupervised and conditional OOD detection, including real-world Mars Rover and Galaxy Zoo datasets, as well as CIFAR-10/100 and Imagenette-based OOD benchmarks. We therefore advocate a phase-aware evaluation paradigm for AEs/VAEs, in which spin-glass observables complement standard ML metrics and expose the latent regimes that underlie downstream success or failure in many cases.

</details>


### [4] [Coexistence of topologically nontrivial and trivial insulating states in topological Anderson Chern insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02733)
*Bo Yin,Yan Zhang,Anqi Wang,Jie Shen,Zhijun Wang,Quansheng Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算（DFT）和非平衡格林函数（NEGF）方法，研究了无序（disorder）对铁磁单层MnBi4Te7的拓扑性质的影响，发现无序可以驱动原本具有时间反演对称性破缺（T-broken）的量子自旋霍尔态转变为量子反常霍尔相，即拓扑安德森陈绝缘体（TACI）。结合自洽玻恩近似（SCBA）计算态密度，构建了包含多种无序诱导相的完整相图，并发现强无序下存在与TACI共存的零霍尔平台绝缘态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无序（disorder）与拓扑（topology）之间的相互作用已成为凝聚态物理的核心课题。无序不仅可以破坏拓扑相，还能诱导拓扑相，例如拓扑安德森绝缘体（TAI）。本文旨在探索在时间反演对称性破缺（T-broken）体系中，无序是否能够驱动类似的新奇量子反常霍尔态。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（DFT）和非平衡格林函数（NEGF）方法在存在无序的条件下进行计算，识别无序诱导的多种相（包括T-broken TAI、TACI、正常绝缘体等），并构建完整相图。进一步利用自洽玻恩近似（SCBA）计算态密度（DOS），以区分强无序区域中的有能隙（gapped）与无能隙（ungapped）拓扑相。

Result: 发现两个有效能带反转（band inversions）在不同的临界无序强度下被抑制；单个能带反转在有限无序窗口内的存续稳定了TACI相。在强无序条件下，进一步发现了一种零霍尔平台绝缘态（zero Hall plateau insulating state），其特征为体态绝缘且边缘通道受到扩散散射，该态可与TACI共存。

Conclusion: 零霍尔平台绝缘态的行为区别于传统的能隙陈绝缘体（band-gap Chern insulator），提供了清晰的实验可观测特征。

Abstract: The interplay between disorder and topology has become a central theme in condensed matter physics. Disorder can not only destroy topological phases but also induce them, as exemplified by the topological Anderson insulator (TAI). Here we show that, in close analogy, disorder can drive the clean-limit, time-reversal-broken(T-broken) quantum spin Hall state of ferromagnetic(FM) monolayer MnBi4Te7 into a quantum anomalous Hall phase, which was called topological Anderson Chern insulator (TACI). Using density functional theory (DFT) and nonequilibrium Green's func tion (NEGF) calculations in the presence of disorder, we identify disorder induced phases-including T-broken TAI, TACI, Normal insulator, etc., then construct a comprehensive phase diagram. To discriminate multiple phases in the strong disorder regime, we further use the density of states computed within the self-consistent Born approximation (SCBA), which in particular distinguishes gapped and ungapped topological phases. We find that the two effective band inversions of Hamiltonian are suppressed at distinct critical disorder strengths; the survival of a single inversion over a finite disorder window stabilizes the TACI. Remarkably, at strong disorder, we further propose a zero Hall plateau insulating state characterized by an insulating bulk and edge channels subject to diffusive scattering that can coexist with the TACI. This behavior is distinct from a conventional band-gap Chern insulator and provides a clear experimental signature.

</details>


### [5] [Scaling Laws for Neural-Network Quantum States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02794)
*Riccardo Rende,Alessandro Sinibaldi,Luciano Loris Viteritti,Roeland Wiersema,Antoine Georges,Giuseppe Carleo*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本研究将神经网络的缩放律（scaling laws）推广至物理问题，发现基于Transformer波函数的神经网络量子态（Neural-Network Quantum States）在训练计算量下的V-score呈幂律衰减，且该指数随阻挫（frustration）程度系统性地减小，可作为基态表示难度的定量指标，从而建立了缩放律作为变分拟设（variational Ansatz）基准测试的通用框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代神经网络中观察到的缩放律（scaling laws）——即损失（loss）与架构规模、计算量之间的幂律关系（power-law relations）——提供了一种定量描述学习问题复杂性的方式，其中损失衰减的指数反映了额外资源转化为精度提升的速率，从而衡量目标的难学程度。然而，是否存在类似的框架来刻画物理问题的复杂性，仍是一个开放问题。本文旨在回答这一疑问。

Method: 采用Transformer波函数（transformer wave functions）逼近三角晶格和方晶格上$J_1$-$J_2$海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）的基态（ground states），晶格规模最大达$20\times 20$个格点。通过训练计算量（training compute）与变分态精度度量V-score之间的幂律关系进行分析，并对计算量进行适当的无量纲化缩放（rescaling）。

Result: 研究发现V-score随训练计算量呈幂律衰减。对计算量进行适当缩放后，不同系统尺寸的结果坍缩到同一条曲线上，类似于临界现象（critical phenomena）中的标度坍缩（scaling collapse）。该幂律的指数在良好近似下与格点数无关，表明Transformer拟设（Ansatz）对所考虑的系统具有尺寸一致性（size-consistent）。指数随阻挫（frustration）程度系统性地减小。

Conclusion: 该指数可作为基态表示难度的定量度量，从而将缩放律确立为一种对变分拟设（variational Ansätze）进行基准测试的通用框架。

Abstract: Scaling laws, the power-law relations between loss, architecture size, and compute observed in modern neural networks, offer a quantitative way to characterize the complexity of a learning problem, with the exponent governing the decay of the loss reflecting how rapidly additional resources translate into improved accuracy, and thus how hard the target is to learn. Whether an analogous framework can characterize the complexity of physical problems remains open. We address this question for Neural-Network Quantum States, a leading variational approach for strongly correlated quantum many-body systems. Using transformer wave functions to approximate ground states of the $J_1$-$J_2$ Heisenberg model on triangular and square lattices with up to $20\times 20$ sites, we find that the $V$-score, a measure of accuracy of a variational state, decays as a power law in training compute. Under an appropriate rescaling of compute, results for different system sizes collapse onto a single curve, analogous to scaling collapse in critical phenomena. The resulting power law is, to a good approximation, independent of the number of sites, showing that the transformer Ansatz is size-consistent for the systems considered. The exponent decreases systematically with frustration, identifying it as a quantitative measure of representational difficulty of the ground state and establishing scaling laws as a general framework for benchmarking variational ansätze.

</details>


### [6] [Structural glasses model using disorder fields: the boson peak from local ground states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02808)
*M. M. Balbino,I. P. de Freitas,A. M. S. Macedo,G. Krein,N. F. Svaiter*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过引入乘性淬火无序（multiplicative quenched disorder）与静态密度涨落场耦合的模型，证明了结构玻璃（structural glasses）谱密度中玻色峰（boson peak）贡献的出现。通过对所有无序实现进行系综平均，作者在平均自由能（average free energy）的函数空间表示中识别出大量亚稳态和基态，并自然导出了随机一级相变（random first-order transition）理论。同时建立了具有随机系数的双曲型微分方程（hyperbolic differential equations）与平均自由能中多个基态之间的联系，从而为研究非晶材料中的涌现激发（emergent excitations）提供了途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解结构玻璃中玻色峰（boson peak）这一普遍存在的谱密度异常特征的微观起源，并在理论层面建立从过冷液体（supercooled liquid）到玻璃态（glassy state）转变的统一形式化描述。

Method: 将静态密度涨落场（static density-fluctuation fields）与乘性淬火无序（multiplicative quenched disorder）耦合来建模玻璃态；对所有无序实现进行系综平均（ensemble average），得到平均自由能（average free energy）的函数级数表示，并从中识别出有效作用量（effective actions）。

Result: 在函数空间中识别出的有效作用量呈现出大量亚稳态（metastable states）和基态（ground states）；随机一级相变（random first-order transition）作为该形式体系的自然涌现结果；建立了具有随机系数的双曲型微分方程与平均自由能中多个基态之间的形式化联系。

Conclusion: 该形式化框架不仅自然产生了随机一级相变理论，还通过随机微分方程与多基态结构的联系，为研究非晶材料（amorphous materials）中的涌现激发（emergent excitations）提供了新的理论途径。

Abstract: We show the emergence of a contribution characteristic of the boson peak in the spectral density of structural glasses. To model the vitreous state, we consider static density-fluctuation fields coupled to a multiplicative quenched disorder. Performing an ensemble average over all disorder realizations, a functional series representation of the average free energy is obtained. In this series representation of the average free energy for the glassy state of matter, we identify in the function space effective actions. These effective actions present a large number of metastable states and ground states. Random first-order transition, widely discussed in the literature as a description of the transition from the supercooled liquid to the glassy state of matter, emerges naturally in our formalism. We establish the connection between the use of hyperbolic differential equations with random coefficients and the presence of many ground states in the average free energy. This connection allows us to study emergent excitations in such amorphous materials.

</details>


### [7] [Relaxation of the Random Site Coulomb glass Model in Two Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02999)
*Preeti Bhandari,Vikas Malik*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过二维随机位点库仑玻璃模型（random site Coulomb glass model）的平均场近似（mean-field approximation）研究材料密度、位点能量无序（disorder in onsite energies）及局域化长度（localization length）对弛豫动力学（relaxation dynamics）的影响。系统先经历快速弛豫，随后因费米能级附近单粒子态密度（density of states, DOS）耗尽而进入幂律（power law）缓慢弛豫，最终遵循指数衰减律（exponential decay law），弛豫时间（relaxation time）与动力学矩阵最小本征值成反比。密度降低或无序增强均导致弛豫时间延长；局域化长度缩短与无序增加的协同效应可能是慢动力学（slow dynamics）的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索材料密度、位点能量无序及局域化长度这三个关键参数对二维随机位点库仑玻璃模型中弛豫动力学的影响机制，以理解无序系统中慢弛豫行为的物理根源。

Method: 基于半满填充（half-filling）的二维随机位点库仑玻璃模型，采用平均场近似计算线性动力学矩阵（linear dynamical matrix）的本征值分布，进而分析系统的弛豫规律。

Result: 系统经历三个弛豫阶段：初始快速能量降低跃迁；随后因费米能级附近单粒子态密度耗尽而呈现幂律衰减的缓慢弛豫；最终在弛豫时间后遵循指数衰减律。弛豫时间与动力学矩阵的最小本征值成反比。密度降低或位点能量无序增强均导致弛豫时间延长。本征值谱的相当部分不受影响。

Conclusion: 密度降低与无序增加均会减缓弛豫速率；局域化长度缩短与无序增加的共同作用可能在慢动力学中扮演与无序本身同等重要的角色。

Abstract: This study investigates the influence of material density, disorder in onsite energies, and localization length on relaxation dynamics within a two-dimensional random site Coulomb glass model at half-filling. To explore relaxation laws, we calculate the eigenvalue distribution of the linear dynamical matrix using mean-field approximations. Our findings indicate that the system initially undergoes rapid relaxation through energy-lowering transitions. The depletion of the single-particle density of states (DOS) near the Fermi level leads to slow relaxation, with fluctuations diminishing according to a power law. Subsequently, the system adheres to an exponential decay law after a specific period, defined as the relaxation time, which is inversely related to the minimum eigenvalue of the dynamical matrix. As the density of the system decreases, the relaxation rate slows down, resulting in an increase in the relaxation time. For a constant density and localization length, an increase in the disorder of onsite energies results in a longer relaxation time. A significant portion of the eigenvalue spectrum remains unaffected, suggesting that a reduction in localization length concurrent with increased disorder may play an equally vital role in the slow dynamics observed.

</details>

### [8] [Scattering and Bound States of Two Heteronuclear Ultracold Atoms in a Quasi-Two-Dimensional Confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02987)
*B. Wang,F. Yang,P. Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文精确求解了准二维（quasi-2D）几何中超冷异核原子的两体问题，推导出二维散射长度 $a_{\rm 2D}$、二维有效力程参数 $R_{\rm 2D}$ 以及束缚态能量作为三维（3D）$s$ 波散射参数（scattering length 和 effective range）的函数，发现纵向质心运动与相对运动的耦合可诱导多个二维散射共振，并对有效相互作用提供调控手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前许多超冷异核气体实验中采用了沿纵向（$z$ 方向）谐波势阱（harmonic trap）的准二维约束，且两原子的阱频不同，导致纵向质心运动与相对运动耦合，使两体问题显著复杂化。此前缺乏对该问题的精确求解，因此需要发展解析方法以准确描述其二维散射性质。

Method: 作者对纵向质心（center-of-mass, CoM）运动与相对运动存在耦合的准二维异核原子两体问题进行了精确求解，从三维自由空间的 $s$ 波散射长度和有效力程出发，推导出二维散射长度 $a_{\rm 2D}$、二维有效力程参数 $R_{\rm 2D}$ 以及束缚态能量的解析表达式。

Result: 研究发现，纵向质心运动与相对运动的耦合可在准二维系统中诱导出多个二维散射共振（scattering resonances）。在这些共振附近，$a_{\rm 2D}$ 随三维散射参数急剧变化，而 $R_{\rm 2D}$ 显著增强。

Conclusion: 由于准二维超冷气体中的有效两体相互作用由两体散射振幅和束缚态能量决定，本文结果可用于通过调节约束阱频和三维散射参数来操控准二维超冷异核气体中的有效二维原子间相互作用。

Abstract: We solve the two-body problem of ultracold heteronuclear atoms in a quasi-two-dimensional (quasi-2D) geometry. The quasi-2D confinement is realized by a harmonic trap along the longitudinal ($z$-) direction, with different trap frequencies for the two atoms, as in many current experiments on ultracold heteronuclear gases. As a consequence, the longitudinal center-of-mass (CoM) motion is coupled to the relative motion, which significantly complicates the two-body problem. We solve this problem exactly and derive the 2D scattering length $a_{\rm 2D}$, the 2D effective range parameter $R_{\rm 2D}$, and the bound-state energies, as functions of the $s$-wave scattering length and effective range of the two atoms in free three-dimensional (3D) space. We show that multiple 2D scattering resonances can be induced by the coupling between the longitudinal CoM and relative motion. Around these resonances, $a_{\rm 2D}$ varies rapidly with the 3D scattering parameters, while $R_{\rm 2D}$ is strongly enhanced. Since the effective pairwise interaction in quasi-2D ultracold gases is determined by i.e., the two-body scattering amplitudes and bound-state energies, our results can be used for manipulating the effective 2D interatomic interaction in quasi-2D ultracold heteronuclear gases by tuning the confinement frequencies and the 3D scattering parameters.

</details>


### [9] [Observation of interaction-induced fast Thouless pumping of solitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03044)
*Yuqing Li,Jinxiong Jia,Yunfei Wang,Huiying Du,Zhong An,Zhenhua Qiao,Liantuan Xiao,Suotang Jia,Qian Niu,Jie Ma*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文在动量空间周期性调制的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中，实验研究了相互作用与调制频率在Thouless泵浦（Thouless pumping）中的协同效应。发现中等相互作用下的物质波孤子（matterwave solitons）可实现快速Thouless泵浦，并在高调制频率下观察到相互作用诱导的非绝热量子化泵浦，而低频绝热泵浦区孤子则被束缚。该工作为加速驱动量子系统中的拓扑输运及设计快速拓扑器件开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Thouless泵浦研究多受限于绝热条件（adiabatic conditions），无法在高驱动频率下探索相互作用驱动的新型拓扑态（topological states）。作者旨在实验上突破这一限制，研究相互作用与调制频率的耦合效应。

Method: 在动量空间中的周期性调制晶格（periodically modulated lattice）内，利用原子玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（atomic Bose-Einstein condensate）实现Thouless泵浦。通过调节相互作用强度和调制频率，观测物质波孤子的输运行为，并与理论计算进行对比。

Result: 在中等相互作用区间观察到无弱相互作用或强相互作用对应物的快速物质波孤子Thouless泵浦；在相互作用诱导的拓扑相变（topological phase transition）边界之外，高调制频率下出现非绝热量子化孤子泵浦，而低频绝热泵浦区孤子被束缚。

Conclusion: 实验揭示了相互作用可突破绝热泵浦的局限性，实现高频率下的快速拓扑输运。该结果为加速驱动量子系统中的拓扑输运以及开发快速拓扑器件（fast topological devices）提供了新方向。

Abstract: Thouless pumping provides a paradigmatic platform for studying the effects of interactions on topological transport in periodically driven systems. However, most studies have been constrained by adiabatic conditions, which preclude exploration of interaction-driven novel topological states at high driving frequencies. Here, we experimentally investigate the interplay between interaction and modulation frequency in Thouless pumping realized in a periodically modulated lattice in momentum space of atomic Bose-Einstein condensate. We observe fast Thouless pumping of matterwave solitons at intermediate interactions, with no counterpart in the non- or weakly interacting regimes. Beyond the boundary of topological phase transition induced by interaction, nonadiabatic quantized pumping of solitons emerges at high modulation frequencies over a broad interaction range, in good agreement with theoretical calculations, while the solitons remain trapped in the low-frequency adiabatic pumping regime. Our work opens new avenues for accelerating topological transport in driven quantum systems and engineering fast topological devices.

### [10] [Drag-induced skin effect in a Bose-Fermi mixture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03403)
*Wenjie Liu,Ching Hua Lee,Yi Qin*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文发现了一种新的拖曳诱导非厄米趋肤效应（drag-induced NHSE）机制，存在于相互作用的玻色-费米混合物中。其中，仅玻色子经历非对称跳跃，而费米子通过强相互作用与玻色子形成关联束缚态（correlated bound states），从而继承边界积累；在少体情况下，相互作用、量子统计与非厄米动力学的耦合还导致了不对称的费米子输运。该机制在超冷原子体系中具有动态稳定性与可实验实现性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米趋肤效应（NHSE）是非厄米物理学中最具标志性的现象之一。现有研究主要集中在单一组分体系中，对于在混合量子物质中是否能够通过相互作用实现不同组分间的NHSE传递尚不清楚，尤其是当某些组分本身保持厄米性（Hermitian）时。

Method: 通过分析玻色-费米混合体系中仅玻色子具有非对称跳跃（asymmetric hopping）而费米子保持厄米性的设定，利用强相互作用诱导的关联束缚态以及相互作用阻塞机制（interaction-induced blockade mechanism），研究费米子如何继承玻色子的边界积累。

Result: 强玻色-费米相互作用使本身不支持独立NHSE的费米子通过关联束缚态继承边界积累。在少体情况下，相互作用、量子统计与非厄米动力学的耦合导致高度不对称的费米子输运。该拖曳诱导NHSE具有动态稳定性。

Conclusion: 研究建立了一种通过相互作用介导实现混合量子物质中新兴非厄米定域化（emergent non-Hermitian localization）的一般机制，并提出了利用Floquet调控非对称隧穿在超冷玻色-费米混合物中实现该效应的可行方案。

Abstract: The non-Hermitian skin effect (NHSE) represents one of the most distinctive phenomena in non-Hermitian physics. Here, we uncover a new drag-induced NHSE mechanism in interacting Bose--Fermi mixtures where only bosons and not fermions experience asymmetric hoppings. %While bosons exhibit intrinsic skin localization due to asymmetric hopping, fermions remain Hermitian in isolation and do not independently support NHSE. We show that strong Bose--Fermi interactions enable fermions to inherit boundary accumulation through correlated bound states. %In the few-body regime, The interplay of interactions, quantum statistics, and non-Hermitian dynamics gives rise to an interaction-induced blockade mechanism, leading to highly asymmetric fermionic transport. We demonstrate that the drag-induced NHSE is dynamically stable and propose a feasible realization in ultracold Bose--Fermi mixtures with Floquet-engineered asymmetric tunneling. Our results establish a general interaction-mediated mechanism for emergent non-Hermitian localization in hybrid quantum matter.

</details>


### [11] [Populating topologically protected edge states of a Chern insulator with the cold-atom elevator scheme and measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03438)
*Toke Marstrand Pontoppidan Lindhard,Anne E. B. Nielsen*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文数值研究了在Chern绝缘体边缘态制备过程中，对粒子库进行瞬时投影测量（projective measurement）的影响，发现测量后的后选择（postselection）可提高手征边缘态中的粒子数或占比，并提出一种计算复杂度仅随格点数量线性增长的解析方法，适用于非相互作用费米子模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前已知可以通过从粒子库（reservoir）转移粒子来填充Chern绝缘体（Chern insulator）的某一组边缘态，但丢弃粒子库前对其进行瞬时投影测量会如何影响最终系统的纯态特性及手征边缘态（chiral edge states）的布居尚不清楚，因此需要数值研究这一测量步骤的物理效应及其可计算性。

Method: 采用数值方法模拟对粒子库实施瞬时投影测量的过程，并对测量结果进行后选择以筛选高概率事件；通过适当改写解析表达式，将测量概率、期望值及其平均值和纯度（purity）的计算转化为仅依赖于测量前状态的形式，且计算复杂度对于固定粒子数仅随格点数量线性增长。

Result: 测量后的后选择有助于提高最终系统中手征边缘态中的粒子数或百分比；所提出的计算方法能够在14个粒子和198个格点的体系中进行数值模拟，且该方法普遍适用于粒子数守恒的非相互作用费米子模型（noninteracting fermionic models）。

Conclusion: 瞬时投影测量步骤虽使物理描述复杂化（从单粒子物理变为多体问题），但通过恰当的解析重写仍可高效计算关键物理量；测量及后选择可作为一种调控手征边缘态布居的有效手段。

Abstract: Two-dimensional Chern insulators support topologically protected, chiral edge currents, and these can be detected in experiments with ultracold atoms in optical lattices. It has previously been shown that one can populate a selected group of edge states of a Chern insulator by transferring particles from a reservoir. Here, we numerically investigate the effect of performing an instantaneous, projective measurement on the reservoir before the reservoir is discarded. In this way, the final state of the system is pure and described by a wavefunction. We also show that quite likely measurement outcomes can help to increase the final number or percentage of particles in the chiral edge states through postselection. Without the measurement step, the physics can be described in terms of single-particle physics. The measurement significantly complicates the description. By appropriately rewriting the analytical expressions, we show that measurement probabilities, expectation values, averages of expectation values, and purity can nevertheless be computed from the state before the measurement in a way that scales only linearly with the number of lattice sites for a fixed number of particles. This enables us to investigate a setup with, for instance, 14 particles and 198 lattice sites numerically. The approach applies generally to noninteracting, fermionic models that conserve the number of particles.

</details>

### [12] [Geometric Bounds on the Finite-Time Performance of Active Machines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03205)
*Geng Li,Z. C. Tu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个统一的热力学框架，用于描述相互作用主动机器（active machines）的有限时间性能。通过几何方法将循环功分解为反对称热力学曲率（antisymmetric thermodynamic curvature）和对称度量（symmetric metric），分别控制功提取与耗散。最优协议由参数空间中的测地线（geodesics）决定，而最优功提取则因曲率诱导的类洛伦兹效应（Lorentz-like effect）偏离测地线。该几何结构建立了与昂萨格型准线性流-力关系（Onsager-type quasi-linear current–force relations）的映射，并用不对称参数（asymmetry parameter）和优值（figure of merit）揭示了主动热机与热电装置的形式对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非平衡物理学（nonequilibrium physics）中，优化主动物质（active matter）的能量转换效率是一个核心挑战。现有理论缺乏统一框架来描述相互作用主动机器在有限时间内的热力学性能。

Method: 发展了一个统一的热力学几何框架，将循环功分解为反对称曲率（控制功提取）和对称度量（控制耗散）；识别出参数空间中的测地线对应最小耗散协议；利用曲率诱导的类洛伦兹效应描述最优功提取的偏离行为。

Result: 建立了几何结构与有限时间标度律（finite-time scaling）的关系，并映射到昂萨格型准线性流-力关系。最大效率与最大功率效率均由不对称参数和优值决定，揭示了主动机器与时间反演对称性破缺热电装置（thermoelectric devices with broken time-reversal symmetry）的形式对应关系。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了能量转换性能的几何起源，为主动机器的优化设计提供了一个通用框架。

Abstract: Optimizing energy conversion in active matter remains a central challenge in nonequilibrium physics. Here, we develop a unified thermodynamic framework that characterizes the finite-time performance of interacting active machines. We show that cyclic work admits a geometric decomposition into an antisymmetric thermodynamic curvature, governing work extraction, and a symmetric metric, controlling dissipation. Minimal-dissipation protocols follow geodesics in parameter space, while optimal work extraction deviates from them due to a curvature-induced, Lorentz-like effect. This geometric structure directly determines the finite-time scaling of work and dissipation, enabling a mapping onto Onsager-type quasi-linear current--force relations. We show that both the maximal efficiency and the efficiency at maximum power are governed by an asymmetry parameter and a figure of merit, establishing a formal correspondence between active machines and thermoelectric devices with broken time-reversal symmetry. Our results reveal a fundamental geometric origin of energy-conversion performance and provide a general framework for optimizing active machines.

</details>


### [13] [Predicting the conditions for observing the Mpemba effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03445)
*Yue Liu,Tan Van Vu,Raphaël Chétrite,Frédéric van Wijland,Hisao Hayakawa*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究通过一维过阻尼朗之万动力学，对能量景观（energy landscape）中的姆潘巴效应（Mpemba effect）进行了系统分类和分析，发现边界条件（boundary conditions）而非内部结构（如亚稳态或势阱数目）是该效应产生的主要驱动因素，并揭示了其背后的动力学机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管姆潘巴效应已在多种非平衡系统中被广泛观测到，但其产生所需能量景观的基本结构特征（structural features）仍存在争议。本研究旨在明确该效应存在的核心条件。

Method: 采用一维过阻尼朗之万动力学（overdamped Langevin dynamics），根据势阱（单阱/双阱）、对称性及壁（wall）的存在性对势能景观进行分类；使用福克-普朗克算符（Fokker-Planck operator）的谱分解（spectral decomposition）分析第一非平凡本征模（first nontrivial eigenmode）的行为。

Result: 姆潘巴效应的存在主要由边界（硬边界或软边界）驱动，而非势能景观的内部具体结构（如亚稳态（metastability）或极小值数量）。第一非平凡本征模的导数在低温区域表现为狄拉克δ峰（Dirac delta peak），该行为与初始布居动力学（initial population dynamics）之间的相互作用——由壁的存在以非平凡方式诱导——构成了效应的机制。

Conclusion: 该分析在单阱与双阱势能之间提供了统一分类，强调了边界条件与不对称性（asymmetry）的关键作用。该框架还可用于设计能够产生多级姆潘巴跃迁（multistage Mpemba transitions）的势能景观。

Abstract: The Mpemba effect, a counterintuitive phenomenon where a hotter system relaxes faster than a colder one, has been widely observed in various nonequilibrium systems. Despite this progress, the fundamental structural features of the energy landscape required for its emergence remain a subject of debate. In this study, we investigate the conditions for the Mpemba effect within one-dimensional overdamped Langevin dynamics. We classify the potential landscapes based on the presence of single or double wells, their symmetry properties, and the existence of walls. We establish that the existence of the effect is primarily driven by the presence of boundaries, either hard or soft, rather than the specific internal structure of the potential landscape, such as metastability or the number of minima. By employing a spectral decomposition of the Fokker-Planck operator, we analyze the behavior of the first nontrivial eigenmode and demonstrate that its derivative acts as a Dirac delta peak in the low-temperature regime. This helps us elucidate the mechanism underlying the Mpemba effect: it appears as the interplay between this behavior and the initial population dynamics in a non-trivial way induced by the presence of the wall. Our analysis provides a unified classification across single- and double-well potentials, highlighting the crucial role of boundary conditions and asymmetry. Furthermore, we demonstrate that this framework allows for the engineering of potential landscapes capable of producing multistage Mpemba transitions.

</details>


### [14] [Constraint-Enhanced Physical Search through Correlation Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03554)
*Song-Ju Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 提出约束增强型物理搜索（constraint-enhanced physical search）原则：将探索的时间相关性与更新动力学中约束诱导的空间相关性相匹配。通过最小化 tug-of-war bandit 模型（TOW）证明，守恒律可将局部观测转化为不同选项的差分证据，时间相关驱动控制探索顺序；搜索效率的提升依赖于时间相关性与物理更新尺度的匹配，而非更强的随机性或最大反相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理系统在搜索过程中不仅引入噪声，还施加约束而产生结构化相关性。已有研究未系统阐明这种约束如何被利用来提升搜索效率，因此需要建立一种组织原则来理解约束与涨落（fluctuations）在物理搜索中的协同作用。

Method: 采用最小化 tug-of-war bandit 模型（TOW）作为理论框架，通过守恒律（conservation law）将局部观测转化为跨选项的差分证据（differential evidence），并引入时间相关驱动（temporally correlated drive）控制探索顺序。通过标度估计（scaling estimate）识别更新噪声与对比度之比（update-noise-to-contrast ratio）作为限制时间反相关（temporal anti-correlation）强度的主导参数。

Result: 搜索效率的提升并非来源于更强的随机性或最大反相关性，而是来自将时间相关性与物理更新尺度（physical update scale）相匹配——即该尺度决定了反馈如何转化为证据。标度分析表明，更新噪声与对比度之比是限制时间反相关性可被利用程度的关键参数。

Conclusion: 约束与涨落能够产生结构化的时空相关性（structured spatiotemporal correlations），当这些相关性与更新动力学（update dynamics）相匹配时，高效的探索即可涌现。该结果为物理搜索提供了一个通用组织原则。

Abstract: Physical systems do not merely add noise to search processes; they impose constraints that generate structured correlations. We propose a principle of constraint-enhanced physical search in which temporal correlations in exploration are matched to constraint-induced spatial correlations in the update dynamics. Using a minimal tug-of-war bandit model (TOW), we show that a conservation law converts local observations into differential evidence across alternatives, while a temporally correlated drive controls the order of exploration. Search efficiency is improved not by stronger randomness or by maximal anti-correlation, but by matching the temporal correlation to the physical update scale that converts feedback into evidence. A scaling estimate identifies the update-noise-to-contrast ratio as the leading parameter that limits how strongly temporal anti-correlation can be used. The results suggest a general organizing principle for physical search: constraints and fluctuations can generate structured spatiotemporal correlations, and efficient exploration emerges when these correlations are matched to the update dynamics.

</details>

### [15] [A family of variational principles of minima for the plasticity, the friction contact and the fracture mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02590)
*Géry de Saxcé*

TL;DR: 本文基于Brezis、Ekeland和Nayroles的原创思想，综合多个关于变分原理（variational principles）在力学和物理学中应用的工作，构建了一个用于动态耗散系统（dynamic dissipative systems）的统一框架，导出一个基于凸分析（convex analysis）和辛几何（symplectic geometry）的时空最小变分原理，并通过理论和数值示例加以说明。

Result: 成功构建了适用于动态耗散系统的统一变分框架，并提供了多种理论和数值示例以展示该框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 基于Brezis、Ekeland和Nayroles思想的变分原理推广，为动态耗散系统的力学与物理学分析提供了一种统一的、基于时空最小化原理的框架。

Abstract: The paper is a synthesis of several works on the variational principles for application to the mechanics and the physics, inspired from original ideas of Brezis, Ekeland and Nayroles. On this basis, we developed an unified framework for dynamic dissipative systems that leads to a space-time variational principle of minimum constructed with tools of convex analysis and symplectic geometry. We stress the essential ideas and concepts. They are illustrated with various theoretical and numerical examples.

### [16] [Logarithmic regularity of spectral measures on infinite graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03006)
*Charles Bordenave*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在单模（unimodular）框架下研究无穷加权图上自伴算子的谱测度正则性，证明在特定几何条件下期望谱度满足对数 Hölder 正则估计，并将经典 Craig–Simon 定理推广到欧几里得晶格（Euclidean lattice）之外。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展谱测度正则性理论，特别是 Craig–Simon 定理，从欧几里得晶格到更一般的无穷加权图结构，涵盖群代数中的算子、随机算子以及 Benjamini–Schramm 极限等广泛情形。

Method: 基于之前与 Sen 和 Virág 共同提出的单调标记方法（monotone labelling method）的强化版本，以控制谱测度的纯点部分（pure point part）；同时施加图上的自然几何条件。

Result: 证明了期望谱度满足对数 Hölder 正则估计（logarithmic Hölder regularity estimate）；结果适用于可指示群（indicable groups）的群代数、Cayley 图上具有任意紧支撑势的 Anderson 型模型、各向异性渗流算子（anisotropic percolation operators）以及准传递图（quasi-transitive graphs）上的算子。

Conclusion: 将经典 Craig–Simon 定理推广到欧几里得晶格之外，为一大类无穷图上的自伴算子的谱测度正则性提供了统一的分析框架。

Abstract: We study the regularity of spectral measures of self-adjoint operators on infinite weighted graphs in the unimodular setting. This framework encompasses operators in the group algebra of a finitely generated group, random operators whose distribution is quasi-invariant under a group action, and Benjamini--Schramm limits of operators on finite graphs. Under a natural geometric condition on the underlying graph, we prove that the expected spectral measure satisfies a logarithmic Hölder regularity estimate. The proof relies on a strengthened version of the monotone labelling method previously introduced with Sen and Virág to control the pure point part of the spectal measure. Applications include operators in group algebras of indicable groups, Anderson-type models with arbitrary compactly supported potentials on Cayley graphs, anisotropic percolation operators, and operators on quasi-transitive graphs. In particular, our results extend the classical Craig--Simon theorem beyond the Euclidean lattice.

</details>


### [17] [Logarithmic Sobolev inequality and hypercontractivity for the Navier-Stokes Fokker-Planck operator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03182)
*Zhi-Wei Wang,Samuel L. Braunstein*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，带有涨落-耗散噪声（fluctuation-dissipation noise）的随机不可压Navier-Stokes方程在$\TT^3$上的Fokker-Planck生成元，其对数Sobolev不等式（logarithmic Sobolev inequality）和超收缩性（hypercontractivity）均保持与纯Ornstein-Uhlenbeck算子相同的常数和速率，且这一结果源于对流生成元在平衡Gibbs测度下的反对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解随机Navier-Stokes方程的Fokker-Planck生成元的结构性质，特别是其耗散部分与对流部分的相互作用对泛函不等式（如对数Sobolev不等式）的影响。

Method: 将Fokker-Planck生成元分解为自伴的Ornstein-Uhlenbeck（耗散）部分和反对称的（对流）部分；证明对流生成元在$L^2(P_\mathrm{eq})$中为反对称算子，从而对Dirichlet形式和$L^q$范数演化无贡献；利用这一结构性质推导泛函不等式。

Result: 对数Sobolev不等式成立，最优常数为$c_\mathrm{LSI} = νλ_1$，与纯Ornstein-Uhlenbeck算子相同，且与保留的Fourier模数无关；全半群（full semigroup）的超收缩速率与Ornstein-Uhlenbeck半群相同。

Conclusion: 对流生成元的反对称性——源于不可压Navier-Stokes非线性的能量守恒和相空间体积守恒（Liouville性质）——保证了泛函不等式不受对流项影响，这也正是涨落-耗散定理（fluctuation-dissipation theorem）的数学基础。

Abstract: The stochastic incompressible Navier-Stokes equations on $\TT^3$, completed by the fluctuation-dissipation noise, have a Fokker-Planck generator that decomposes into a self-adjoint Ornstein-Uhlenbeck (dissipative) part and an antisymmetric (convective) part. We prove two results about this generator. First, the logarithmic Sobolev inequality holds with the same optimal constant as the pure Ornstein-Uhlenbeck operator, $c_\mathrm{LSI} = νλ_1$ (where $ν$ is the viscosity and $λ_1$ is the smallest nonzero eigenvalue of the Laplacian on $\TT^3$), independent of the number of retained Fourier modes. Second, the full semigroup is hypercontractive with the same rate as the Ornstein-Uhlenbeck semigroup. Both results follow from a single structural property: the convective generator is antisymmetric in $L^2(P_\mathrm{eq})$ (where $P_\mathrm{eq}$ is the Gibbs measure), and therefore contributes nothing to the Dirichlet form or the $L^q$ norm evolution. The antisymmetry is a consequence of two properties of the incompressible Navier-Stokes nonlinearity: energy conservation and phase-space volume preservation (the Liouville property). These are the same properties that underpin the fluctuation-dissipation theorem for the nonlinear Navier-Stokes equations.

</details>

*Christian Hainzl,Fabian Saxler,Robert Seiringer*

Method: 通过计算排斥短程相互作用下稀薄二维费米气体的基态能量上界，构建与三维Huang-Yang公式类似的二维表达式，并捕捉小参数$\varrho a^2$（密度$\varrho$与散射长度$a$的乘积）渐近展开的前三项。

Result: 获得了二维费米气体基态能量的上界，该上界在小密度-散射长度参数$\varrho a^2$的渐近展开中包含了前三项。

Conclusion: 本文结果可视为三维Huang-Yang公式在二维情形的直接类比，为二维稀薄费米气体的基态能量提供了可计算的严格上界约束。

Abstract: We compute an upper bound on the ground state energy of a dilute two-dimensional Fermi gas with repulsive short-range interactions. Our bound can be viewed as the two-dimensional analogue of a formula derived by Huang and Yang in the three-dimensional case. It captures the first three terms in an asymptotic expansion for small $\varrho a^2$, where $\varrho$ denotes the density and $a$ the scattering length of the interaction potential.

### [19] [Classical Symmetry TFTs for Continuous Symmetries via Higher Symplectic Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03368)
*Hao Xu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种经典连续对称TFT范式的平移辛（shifted-symplectic）表述，将群G的拓扑缺陷作用与AKSZ构造中的移位余切叠T*[n](BG)联系，建立了(n+1)维BF理论作为体态理论，并讨论了边界条件、规范对称性、约化以及预量子化细化，包括't Hooft反常和三维中的因子化双与r-矩阵的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对称TFT（symmetry TFT）范式是研究量子场论中全局对称性和反常的重要工具，但其经典连续类比尚缺乏系统性的几何表述。本文旨在建立一种基于平移辛几何（shifted symplectic geometry）的严格理论框架，将AKSZ构造与群作用的拓扑缺陷相结合，为经典连续对称TFT提供统一的数学基础。

Method: 利用AKSZ（Alexandrov–Kontsevich–Schwarz–Zaboronsky）构造，提出了一种平移辛表述，将作用在n维经典拓扑sigma模型上的群G的拓扑缺陷与目标为(n-1)-平移辛导出叠（shifted symplectic derived stack）的理论相关联；论证了对应的(n+1)维体态理论应为以移位余切叠T*[n](BG)为目标的AKSZ理论（等价于n+1维BF理论）；通过移位拉格朗日子流形（shifted Lagrangians）刻画Dirichlet和Neumann边界条件及更一般的拓扑边界；通过在BF体态中插入拓扑畴壁（topological domain wall）实现规范对称性；引入平移辛框架下的哈密顿约化（Hamiltonian reduction）、辛约化（symplectic reduction）和拉格朗日约化（Lagrangian reduction）；通过高位丛（higher gerbes）编码't Hooft反常数据；在三维情形比较了无穷小BF模型B(g ⋉ g^∨)与因子化双B(g ⊕ g)。

Result: 建立了连续经典对称TFT的平移辛形式体系；将体态理论识别为n+1维BF理论；给出了边界条件与移位拉格朗日的对应关系；引入了平移辛框架下的多种约化概念；构建了预量子化细化中高位丛与't Hooft反常的联系；在三维中揭示了无穷小BF模型与因子化双之间的差异，指出因子化情形下的拓扑边界由拉格朗日李子代数（Lagrangian Lie subalgebras）描述，并将SymTFT字典与r-矩阵（r-matrices）和Belavin–Drinfeld数据关联起来。

Conclusion: 本文提出的平移辛表述为经典连续对称TFT提供了严格的几何框架，统一了AKSZ构造、BF理论和群作用下的拓扑缺陷。该框架不仅系统地刻画了边界条件和对称性规范化的实现方式，还通过预量子化细化为理解't Hooft反常提供了新的几何视角。三维情形的分析进一步揭示了SymTFT字典与可积系统理论中r-矩阵和Belavin–Drinfeld分类之间的深层联系，预示了该形式体系的广阔应用前景。

Abstract: We propose a shifted-symplectic formulation of a classical continuous analogue of the symmetry TFT paradigm. Let $G$ be an algebraic or Lie group acting by topological defects on an $n$-dimensional classical topological sigma model with target an $(n-1)$-shifted symplectic derived stack $(X,ω)$ via the AKSZ construction. We argue that the corresponding $(n+1)$-dimensional bulk theory should be the AKSZ theory with target the shifted cotangent stack $T^*[n] (\mathrm B G)$, equivalently the $(n+1)$-dimensional BF theory for $G$. We characterize the Dirichlet and Neumann boundary conditions, and more general topological boundaries, in terms of shifted Lagrangians in $T^*[n] (\mathrm B G)$. We realize the gauging of the $G$-symmetry in the original theory as inserting a topological domain wall between the corresponding topological boundaries in the BF bulk, and introduce the notion of Hamiltonian reduction, syplectic reduction, and Lagrangian reduction in the shifted symplectic setting. We also discuss prequantum refinements of continuous SymTFTs. In this refinement, higher gerbes on $\mathrm B G$ encode classical analogues of 't Hooft anomaly data by decorating the shifted cotangent bulk and its Lagrangian boundary conditions. Finally, in dimension three we compare the infinitesimal BF model $\mathrm B(\mathfrak g\ltimes\mathfrak g^\vee)$ with the factorizable double $\mathrm B(\mathfrak g\oplus \mathfrak g)$. The resulting topological boundaries are described by Lagrangian Lie subalgebras, and the factorizable case relates the SymTFT dictionary to $r$-matrices and Belavin--Drinfeld data.

</details>


### [20] [Interpolating non-Hermitian universality classes A and AI$^\dagger$: eigenvalue density and transition regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03447)
*Mark J. Crumpton,Francesco Mezzadri*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用Kac-Rice形式化方法，研究了在复Ginibre矩阵（Class A）与复对称矩阵（Class AI†）之间插值的高斯系综中特征值与其归一化右特征向量的联合分布，推导了有限N和渐近极限下的特征值密度，并发现了一种新的边缘标度过渡区间（σ = 1 - κN^{-1/2}），其中特征值密度平滑插值两个已知结果，且该过渡被认为具有普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展Kac-Rice形式化方法（Kac-Rice formalism）至非厄米随机矩阵（non-Hermitian random matrices），用于研究不同对称类之间插值系综的特征值与特征向量统计性质，尤其是边缘特征值在有限尺寸下的新过渡行为。

Method: 采用Kac-Rice形式化方法，推导高斯插值系综中特征值与其归一化右特征向量的联合分布；该分布适用于任意有限矩阵尺寸N和插值参数σ∈[0,1]。进一步对特征值密度进行有限N推导及N→∞渐近分析。

Result: 对体态特征值，所有σ均恢复标准圆形律（circular law）。对边缘特征值，固定σ时服从Class A的边缘密度；但当σ以σ = 1 - κN^{-1/2}标度时，发现新的过渡区间，特征值密度平滑插值两个已知结果。此过渡行为被推测为对非高斯矩阵具有普适性，并提供了数值证据支持。

Conclusion: 特征值的边缘密度在特定标度下展现出新的过渡行为，该行为可能具有普适性，为理解非厄米随机矩阵不同对称类之间的连续过渡提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We employ the recently developed Kac-Rice formalism for non-Hermitian random matrices to derive the joint distribution of an eigenvalue and its associated normalised right eigenvector in a Gaussian ensemble that interpolates between complex Ginibre (Class A) and complex symmetric matrices (Class AI$^\dagger$). This distribution is valid at finite matrix size, $N$, for any value of the interpolation parameter $σ\in [0,1]$, with $0$ and $1$ corresponding to classes A and AI$^\dagger$ respectively. The marginal distribution for the density of the eigenvalues is derived at finite $N$ and then considered asymptotically as $N \to \infty$. When considering bulk eigenvalues, we recover the standard circular law for all $σ$. Furthermore, for edge eigenvalues we find that for fixed $σ$, the eigenvalues follow the edge density associated with matrices in Class A. However, a transitional regime is discovered for the interpolation parameter being scaled as $σ= 1 - κN^{-1/2}$, where new edge behaviour is observed for the density of eigenvalues - smoothly interpolating two previously known results. This transitional regime and the associated density of eigenvalues is conjectured to be universal for non-Gaussian matrices and we provide numerical evidence in support of this.

</details>


### [21] [Asymptotics of complex $b$-$6j$ symbols](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03653)
*Yunpeng Meng,Tian Yang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了复指数b的b-6j符号（b-6j symbols），即量子群U_q𝔰𝔩(2;ℝ)模对偶主序列上6j符号的解析延拓，并将其在双曲四面体（hyperbolic tetrahedron）六参数按二面角缩放时的渐近行为与四面体的体积及Gram矩阵行列式建立联系，并在arg b = ±π/4情形下认为该工作与复刘维尔弦论（complex Liouville string）密切相关。

Method: 通过引入复指数b构造b-6j符号作为标准6j符号的解析延拓；分析当六个参数按超理想双曲四面体（hyperideal hyperbolic tetrahedron）的二面角（dihedral angles）缩放时该符号的渐近行为。

Abstract: We study the $b$-$6j$ symbols -- an analytic extension of the $6j$-symbols for the principal series of the modular double of $\mathrm U_q\mathfrak{sl}(2;\mathbb R)$ -- with complex index $b,$ refereed to as the \emph{complex $b$-$6j$ symbols}. ### [22] [Two-orbital $e_g$ model with bond-dependent spin-orbit coupling: A playground for emergent band topology, Kitaev magnetism, and magnetoelectricity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02716)
*YuZheng Xie,Manoj Gupta,Arun Paramekanti,Tanusri Saha-Dasgupta*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一个低能双轨道e_g模型，模型中包含由配体X上原子自旋轨道耦合驱动的键依赖自旋轨道项；基于对称性分析和微观计算探索磁电效应（magnetoelectric effect），超越了广义Katsura-Nagaosa-Balatsky理论对单轨道情形的描述。

Result: 在非相互作用能带极限下，自旋轨道衍生的自旋依赖和自旋翻转跳跃项产生了具有自旋陈数（spin-Chern numbers）C_s=±2, ±4的拓扑能带，以及具有分数角落电荷（fractional corner charges）的高阶拓扑态（higher order topological states）；在半填充莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator）极限下，恢复了具有键依赖Kitaev交换相互作用的自旋-1哈密顿量。

Conclusion: 该工作可能与NiX₂及关联材料的掺杂、应变或压力研究相关，为理解此类体系中的拓扑和磁电性质提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Inspired by the electronic structure of compounds like nickel dihalides Ni$X_2$ ($X$=Cl, Br, I), we propose a low-energy two-orbital $e_g$ model featuring bond-dependent spin-orbit terms, driven by atomic spin-orbit coupling on the ligand $X$. We demonstrate that this model hosts a rich array of phenomena. In the non-interacting band limit, spin-orbit-derived spin-dependent and spin-flip hopping terms produce topological bands with spin-Chern numbers $C_s=\pm 2, \pm 4$, and higher order topological states with fractional corner charges, respectively. In the half-filled Mott insulator limit, we recover a spin-$1$ Hamiltonian with bond-dependent Kitaev exchange interactions. We explore the magnetoelectric effect in this two-orbital model using symmetry-based perspective and microscopic calculations, going beyond the generalized Katsura-Nagaosa-Balatsky theory for the single-orbital case. Our work may be relevant to study of doping, strain, or pressure on Ni$X_2$ and related materials.

</details>

Abstract: We investigate the ground state properties, magnetization, and low-temperature thermodynamics of the ferromagnetic-antiferromagnetic spin-$s$ model on diamond-decorated lattices with ideal diamond units, incorporating bilinear Heisenberg and higher-order exchange interactions between diagonal spins-$σ$. Local conservation of the composite spin on each diamond diagonal enables exact analysis. For the pure Heisenberg case, the system undergoes a series of $2σ$ transitions between monomer-dimer (MD), ferrimagnetic (Ferri) and ferromagnetic (F) phases with different optimal composite spin values as the coupling ratio varies. In the presence of higher-order interactions, a multicritical point exists where the states with all possible values of composite spin are degenerate, leading to maximal ground state degeneracy. The case $s=σ=1$ with bilinear and biquadratic interactions is studied in detail. Its phase diagram comprises three phases - F, Ferri and MD, which meet at a triple point. On the phase boundaries, the ground state becomes macroscopically degenerate. For the diamond chain, we calculate the ground state degeneracy exactly; for higher dimensions, the problem maps onto a bond percolation framework, solved numerically. The residual entropy per spin reaches up to $60\%$ of the maximal value, peaking at the triple point. Low-temperature magnetization curves in external magnetic fields exhibit plateaus and jumps. The excitation spectrum is gapped in the MD phase, gapless in the F phase, and resembles that of the Lieb-Mattis ferrimagnet in the Ferri phase. The high residual entropy suggests potential applications in ultra-low-temperature cooling and quantum thermal machines.

### [24] [Skyrmion and meron phases induced by spin-phonon coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02793)
*E. Iroulart,F. A. Gómez Albarracín,H. Diego Rosales*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用蒙特卡罗模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）方法，在正方晶格（square lattice）上的二维斯格明子模型中，对比两种简化的自旋-声子耦合模型：爱因斯坦位点声子模型（Einstein site-phonon model, ESP）和键-声子模型（bond-phonon model, BP）。

Conclusion: 晶格效应为调控拓扑磁性相（topological magnetic phases）提供了一种简洁的机制。

Abstract: In chiral magnets, magnetic skyrmions are typically stabilized by the competition between exchange and Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interactions under an external magnetic field, while the role of lattice degrees of freedom has received comparatively less attention. Here we study how spin-phonon (SP) coupling modifies magnetic interactions and the resulting spin textures in a two-dimensional skyrmion model in the square lattice. Using Monte Carlo simulations, we compare two simplified models describing the SP coupling: the Einstein site-phonon (ESP) and bond-phonon (BP) models. We find that ESP coupling stabilizes skyrmion crystals in field regimes that are topologically trivial in the uncoupled model and also induces additional textures, including meron-antimeron (M-aM) crystals and mixed skyrmion-bimeron (SkX-Bm) phases. Furthermore, for sufficiently strong phonon coupling, the conventional triple-$\textbf{q}$ hexagonal skyrmion lattice is distorted into a double-$\textbf{q}$ square skyrmion lattice. Overall, our results show that lattice effects provide a simple mechanism to tune topological magnetic phases.

### [25] [Phase transitions through excited-state level crossings and topological indicators: the case of the XXZ chain with staggered Ising interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02845)
*B. F. Márquez,K. Hallberg,A. A. Aligia*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文结合精确对角化（exact diagonalization）、拓扑指标（topological indicators）和能级交叉方法，确定了自旋-1/2 XXZ链在交错Ising相互作用和均匀横向交换作用下的相图，并分析了两种方法的适用性与局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋-1/2 XXZ链在交错Ising相互作用下呈现Néel序（Néel order）与键二聚化相（bond-dimerized phases）之间的竞争，但精确确定相边界（尤其在小能隙或大关联长度区域）存在困难。本文旨在结合拓扑指标和能级交叉两种方法，提高相图计算的效率与准确性。

Method: 本文采用两种方法确定相边界。第一种基于广义位置算符（generalized position operators）构造拓扑指标（topological indicators），并将其与玻色化（bosonization）结果进行对比。第二种基于激发态能级交叉（crossings of excited energy levels），并用共形场论（conformal-field theory）进行解释。两种方法均以精确对角化（exact diagonalization）为数值基础。

Result: 对于拓扑指标，玻色化与数值结果总体上一致，但当场论分析表明某一侧能隙极小（或关联长度极大）时，拓扑指标跳跃的准确性受到影响，仅能给出定性正确的相图。能级交叉方法尽管部分平移对称性（translational symmetry）因交错Ising相互作用而丧失，仍能精确确定Néel相与二聚化相之间的边界。两者结合比传统方法更高效。

Conclusion: 拓扑指标与能级交叉两种方法的结合，为关联一维模型（correlated one-dimensional models）提供了一种比传统方法更高效的相图计算方案。

Abstract: We combine two ways of determining the phase diagram of the spin-$1/2$ XXZ chain with a staggered Ising interaction and uniform transverse exchange, based on exact diagonalization. The model realizes a competition between Néel order and bond-dimerized phases generated by the alternating Ising interaction. The simplest approach to determine the phase boundaries is to use topological indicators based on generalized position operators. We show that in general, the bosonized and numerical results for the topological indicators agree. The second is based on crossings of excited energy levels and justified by conformal-field theory. In spite of the partial loss of translational symmetry caused by the alternating Ising interaction, we find that the latter method provides an accurate determination of the boundary between Néel and dimerized phases. Instead, while the jumps of a topological indicator provide a qualitatively correct phase diagram, its accuracy is affected when the gap is very small (or the correlation length very large) at one side of the transition, as we show using field-theoretical arguments. The combination of both methods provides a more efficient way of calculating phase diagrams for correlated one-dimensional models than other widely used conventional approaches.

TL;DR: 本文提出一种降维理论框架，通过将玻色子（boson）与费米子（fermion）置于不同空间维度来研究有限密度下的量子场论（quantum field theory），显著简化了重整化群（renormalization group）分析并改善了非费米液体（non-Fermi liquid）行为的微扰收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子场论在有限密度下处理非费米液体行为时，玻色子-费米子耦合的重整化群分析复杂，且微扰展开中存在严重的对数发散（logarithmic divergence）问题，需要更可控的理论工具。

Method: 提出降维框架，将玻色场（bosonic fields）置于$(d+1)$维体（bulk），费米场（fermionic fields）限制在$d$维边界（boundary），实现空间维度的分离。

Result: 树图级（tree-level）玻色子交换贡献在降维方案中变为有限；传统1-loop四费米子相互作用中的$\log^2$和$\log^3$发散被简化为对数发散。

Conclusion: 该框架显著改善了微扰展开的收敛性（convergence property），为非费米液体物理提供了可控的理论分析途径。

Abstract: We present a reduced dimension theoretical framework for studying quantum field theories at finite density, providing a tractable model for investigating non-Fermi liquid (NFL) behavior near quantum phase transitions. Our approach departs from the standard paradigm by placing bosons and fermions in different spatial dimensions: bosonic fields reside in a $(d+1)$-dimensional bulk, while fermionic fields are confined on a $d$-dimensional boundary. This dimensional separation significantly simplifies the renormalization group (RG) analysis of gapless boson-fermion coupling. We demonstrate that the tree-level boson exchange contributions, which typically exhibit logarithmic divergences, become finite in our reduced-dimension scheme. Furthermore, the $\log^2$ and $\log^3$ divergences that characterize 1-loop four-fermion interactions in conventional treatments are reduced to logarithmic divergences within this framework, substantially improving the convergence properties of the perturbative expansion and allowing controlled theoretical analysis of NFL physics.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准虚时间演化方法（如均匀时间步长的时间相关变分原理）在量子多体系统中步数过多、计算开销大，需要更高效的传播方案。

Method: 首先证明对数时间网格（logarithmic time grids）足以解析长虚时间动力学，从而将时间步数指数级缩减；其次利用常微分方程的A-稳定隐式时间步进法（A-stable implicit time-stepping methods），使传播在任意步长下保持稳定。整个方案仅需矩阵-向量乘积与线性求解，属于MPS标准操作。

Result: 在Heisenberg自旋链上，该方法相比均匀步长的时间相关变分原理实现数个数量级的加速；在单杂质安德森模型中，传播至大虚时间可观测到Kondo温度对相互作用强度的指数依赖关系。

Conclusion: 所提出的对数网格与隐式步进相结合的策略，能显著提升MPS虚时间演化的计算效率，并适用于长时尺度物理现象的模拟。

Abstract: We present a new method for the efficient imaginary time evolution of quantum many-body wavefunctions represented by matrix product states (MPS). We first show that logarithmic time grids are sufficient to resolve long imaginary time dynamics, yielding an exponential reduction in the number of time steps compared with standard approaches. We then show that A-stable implicit time-stepping methods for ordinary differential equations allow stable propagation for any time step size. The resulting scheme requires only matrix-vector products and linear solves, standard operations in the MPS toolbox. We validate our approach with two examples: a Heisenberg spin chain, which we use to demonstrate a speedup of several orders of magnitude over the standard time-dependent variational principle method with uniform time steps, and a single-site Anderson impurity model with a metallic bath, for which propagation to large imaginary times allows one to observe the exponential dependence of the Kondo temperature on the interaction strength.

Abstract: The breakdown of conventional bulk-boundary correspondence (BBC) in
  non-Hermitian system can be resolved by the generalized Brillouin
  zone (GBZ) theory. However, extending the GBZ theory to interacting
  many-body systems remains an open problem. Here, we consider an
  interacting non-Hermitian model characterized by a circular GBZ. We
  show that, based on a GBZ transformation, a quasi-reciprocal
  many-body Hamiltonian can be constructed which, under periodic
  boundary conditions (PBC), captures the physics of the original
  non-Hermitian model under open boundary conditions (OBC). Using
  exact diagonalization (ED), we determine the phase diagram for the
  quasi-reciprocal many-body Hamiltonian by computing the Zak phase
  and the structure factor of the charge-density-wave (CDW) phase. We

  degeneracy of the low-lying entanglement spectrum characterizes each
  phase in the phase diagram. These findings demonstrate that the
  topological properties in interacting non-Hermitian system is encoded in
  the entanglement spectrum of the quasi-reciprocal model. Our work
  establishes a route to studying many-body non-Hermitian physics
  within the GBZ formalism.

Method: 通过数值计算分析强无序陈绝缘体中拓扑相与平庸安德森绝缘体（Anderson insulator）之间的相变，提取关联长度临界指数（correlation-length critical exponent）和动力学临界指数（dynamical critical exponent）；并通过对无序强度进行淬火（quench），研究激发密度和局域陈标记相关的非平衡长度标度随时间的演化。

Result: 该相变具有非零电导，局域陈标记实空间分布中出现临界长度标度；提取的临界指数与整数量子霍尔效应非相互作用模型的结果一致。非平衡动力学中，激发密度不遵循Kibble-Zurek标度；局域陈标记相关的非平衡长度在拓扑到平庸的淬火方向接近Kibble-Zurek预测，但在反方向存在偏离。

Abstract: We study the critical properties of the topological Anderson phase transition in a strongly disordered Chern insulator, separating the topological phase from a trivial Anderson insulator. We show that the transition is characterized by a non-zero electrical conductance and by the emergence of a critical length scale in the real-space profile of the local Chern marker. From this, we extract the correlation-length and the dynamical critical exponents, which are consistent with those of non-interacting models of the integer quantum Hall effect. We then ramp the disorder strength across the transition and study the ensuing dynamics. In contrast to clean topological systems, we find that the excitation density does not follow the Kibble-Zurek scaling. The non-equilibrium length scale associated with the local Chern marker is decoupled from the generation of excitations. For studied system sizes, we find it to be close to the Kibble-Zurek prediction for the topological-to-trivial quench, while it deviates from it for the reverse direction.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交错磁体（altermagnet）和完全补偿铁磁体（fully compensated ferrimagnet）中，电子能带和磁子能带在无净磁化（net magnetization）下仍存在自旋分裂（spin splitting），可热激活磁子自旋电流。本文旨在理论探索弱易轴各向异性下磁场对这类反铁磁体中磁子性质的影响机制。

Method: 针对交错磁体，在方格子（square lattice）$J_1$-$J_2$-$J_2^\prime$ 模型上分析2-子格序（2-sublattice order）；针对完全补偿铁磁体，在kagome格点$J_1$-$J_3$模型上分析三重${\bf Q}$12-子格序（triple-$\bf Q$ 12-sublattice order），两者在零场下分别伴随$d$-波和$s$-波自旋分裂。理论框架考虑弱易轴各向异性（easy-axis anisotropy）使共线态（collinear states）对磁场具有鲁棒性。

Result: 当磁场能量尺度小于各向异性能隙（anisotropy gap）时，正（负）磁场使上自旋和下自旋磁子能带分别向低（高）能量和高（低）能量偏移，类似电子系统中的塞曼耦合（Zeeman coupling）。交错磁体中，随磁场增强，$d$-波分裂趋于变形为$s$-波分裂，表现为热梯度驱动自旋电流（spin current）方向的变化。完全补偿铁磁体中，$s$-波特性（零场时上、下自旋磁子布居不平衡）导致纵向自旋和热导率（spin and thermal conductivities）呈现不对称场依赖性。

Conclusion: 磁场可有效调控交错磁体和完全补偿铁磁体中的磁子能带分裂模式及自旋输运性质，为基于反铁磁体的自旋热电子学（spin caloritronics）器件设计提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In altermagnets and fully compensated ferrimagnets, not only the electron band but also the magnon band exhibits spin splitting without net magnetization, which enables thermal activation of the magnon spin current. Here, we theoretically investigate magnetic field effects on the magnon properties of these antiferromagnets in the presence of a weak easy-axis anisotropy which makes the collinear states robust against the magnetic field. For the altermagnet and compensated ferrimagnet, we analyze a 2 sublattice order in the $J_1$-$J_2$-$J_2^\prime$ model on the square lattice and a triple-${\bf Q}$ 12-sublattice order in the $J_1$-$J_3$ model on the kagome lattice, respectively, each accompanied by $d$-wave and $s$-wave spin splitting at zero field. It is shown that for positive (negative) magnetic field $H$ whose energy scale is smaller than the anisotropy gap, the up- and down-spin magnon bands are shifted to lower (higher) and higher (lower) energies, respectively, similarly to the Zeeman coupling in electron systems. In the altermagnet, with increasing field, the $d$-wave splitting tends to be deformed into the $s$-wave one, which is reflected as the change in the direction of the spin current generated by thermal gradient. In the compensated ferrimagnet, the $s$-wave nature, i.e., the population imbalance between the up- and down-spin magnons at $H=0$, results in an asymmetric field dependence of the longitudinal spin and thermal conductivities.

</details>


### [31] [Mott transition of photons: quantum Monte Carlo study of Gross-Neveu criticality in a cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03733)
*João C. Inácio,Natanael C. Costa,Fakher F. Assaad*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文研究了蜂窝状晶格上的哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）与单一线极化腔光子模式的耦合，发现光-物质耦合在临界点（criticality）处是无关的（irrelevant），但光子谱函数（photon spectral function）通过耦合电子系统的光导率（optical conductivity）经历莫特转变（Mott transition），可作为非接触式探测莫特临界性（Mott criticality）的手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蜂窝状晶格上的哈伯德模型是实现属于Gross-Neveu O(3)普适类（universality class）的半金属-绝缘体莫特转变（semimetal-to-insulator Mott transition）的理想体系。作者希望将这一电子系统耦合到腔光子模式，以探讨光-物质相互作用对莫特临界行为的影响，并开发一种新的探测手段。

Method: 作者将该电子系统与一个单一线极化的腔光子模式（cavity photon mode）耦合，使得光子数保持为强度量（intensive quantity）。针对该相互作用的光-物质模型，作者提出了一个无负符号问题（negative-sign-free）的费米子量子蒙特卡洛算法（fermion quantum Monte Carlo algorithm），可在有限系统尺寸上获得无偏结果（bias-free results）。

Result: 数值结果表明，即使在强电子-光子耦合下，光-物质耦合在临界点处是无关的。另一方面，数值与解析分析均显示，光子谱函数与电子系统的光导率耦合，腔光子因此经历莫特转变。

Conclusion: 光子谱函数可作为无需接触的非侵入式探针（contact-free non-invasive probe），用于探测莫特临界性。

Abstract: The Hubbard model on the honeycomb lattice is a pristine realisation of a semimetal-to-insulator Mott transition belonging to the Gross-Neveu O(3) universality class. We couple this system to a single linearly polarised cavity photon mode. The light-matter coupling is such that the photon number remains an intensive quantity as is the case for an empty cavity. For this interacting light-matter model, we formulate a negative-sign-free fermion quantum Monte Carlo algorithm that allows for bias-free results on finite system sizes. Our numerical results show that the coupling to the cavity is irrelevant at criticality, even at strong electron-photon coupling. On the other hand, we observe, and show analytically, that the photon spectral function couples to the optical conductivity of the electronic system. The cavity photons thereby undergo a Mott transition, and the photon spectral function acts as a contact-free non-invasive probe for Mott criticality.

</details>


### [32] [Spin-chiral electron-phonon coupling in metallic strontium titanate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03908)
*N. Somun,L. Rogić,I. Khayr,E. Tafra,M. Basletić,A. Kundu,J. Dzian,F. Le Mardele,M. Orlita,M. Greven,B. Büchner,A. Alfonsov,M. N. Gastiasoro,A. Klein,D. Pelc*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过远红外光吸收实验，在SrTiO₃中发现了一种由电子自旋介导的电子-声子耦合新机制，该机制能产生具有大有效磁矩的手性声子模式，其耦合强度足以解释SrTiO₃的超导电性，并有望普遍存在于所有具有极性声子的金属中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling, EPC）仅由离子静电背景诱导，电子自旋不起作用。本文旨在挑战这一传统认识，揭示一种由自旋直接介导的电子与横向极性声子之间的耦合机制。

Method: 以SrTiO₃为模型体系，在磁场中进行远红外光吸收测量（far-infrared light absorption measurements），观测自旋介导的电子-声子耦合信号，并将其与理论预测和第一性原理（ab initio）估算进行定量比较。

Result: 实验观测到强自旋介导的电子-声子耦合，与理论预测定量一致；该耦合产生了具有大有效磁矩的手性声子模式（chiral phonon modes），提取的耦合强度与第一性原理估算吻合，且高到足以解释SrTiO₃的超导电性。

Conclusion: 自旋-手性电子-声子耦合（spin-chiral EPC）应普遍存在于所有具有极性声子的金属中。该工作对自旋电子学（spintronics）应用、以及揭示层状材料、具有狄拉克点（Dirac points）的金属和近铁电超导体中超导电性的起源具有重要意义。

Abstract: Electron-phonon coupling (EPC) - the interaction between conduction electrons and quantized atomic vibrations - plays a central role in condensed matter physics and determines some of the most important properties of materials, such as electrical resistivity and superconductivity. Conventionally, EPC is assumed to be induced by the ionic electrostatic background, and electronic spin plays no role in the process. In stark contrast with this view, here we uncover a direct spin-mediated coupling mechanism between electrons and transverse polar phonons in a metal. Using far-infrared light absorption measurements of the model system SrTiO$_3$ in a magnetic field, we observe a strong spin-mediated EPC that is quantitatively consistent with recent theoretical predictions, and that generates chiral phonon modes with large effective magnetic moments. The extracted coupling strength is in good agreement with ab initio estimates and sufficiently high to explain superconductivity in SrTiO$_3$, thereby resolving a long-standing conundrum. Spin-chiral EPC should generically appear in all metals with polar phonons, and the present work could be of relevance to spintronics applications and to uncovering the origins of superconductivity in layered materials, metals with Dirac points in their electronic dispersions, and nearly ferroelectric superconductors.

</details>

### [33] [On-Shell Bootstrap of Loop Inflation Correlators with Spectral Dispersion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02686)
*Haoyuan Liu,Zhehan Qin,Jiayi Wu,Zhong-Zhi Xianyu,Hongyu Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为“谱色散（spectral dispersion）”的新自举（bootstrap）策略，用于计算圈图层次的宇宙学关联函数。该方法基于两个概念性观察：关联函数可通过解析性从壳上数据（on-shell data）恢复至局域抵消项（local counterterms），以及圈过程的壳上数据表现为准正规模式（quasinormal modes）的离散求和。技术上，该方法结合了德西特谱分解（dS spectral decomposition）与色散关系（dispersion relations），并成功自举出标量和矢量玻色子单圈质量交换的三点及四点关联函数的新结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 圈图层次的宇宙学关联函数计算复杂，传统方法往往繁琐且缺乏系统性。本文旨在开发一种新的自举策略，简化此类计算过程，并能够以简洁直观的形式获得新结果。

Method: 该方法的核心理念是通过解析性从壳上数据恢复关联函数，直至局域抵消项；同时利用圈过程壳上数据表现为准正规模式离散求和的特点。技术上，该方法将德西特谱分解与色散关系相结合。

Result: 利用该技术，本文以简洁直观的形式自举出标量和矢量玻色子单圈质量交换的三点及四点关联函数的新结果。该方法还可直接推广到更高自旋以及具有德西特协变色散（dS covariant dispersions）但非协变耦合的高圈香蕉图（banana graphs）。

Conclusion: 谱色散自举策略为圈图宇宙学关联函数的计算提供了一种系统且高效的新工具，其适用性可拓展至更高自旋和更复杂的圈图结构。

Abstract: We develop a new bootstrap strategy for cosmological correlators at loop level, which we call spectral dispersion. It is based on two conceptual observations that a correlator can be recovered from its on-shell data, also known as nonlocal signals, by analyticity up to local counterterms, and that the on-shell data for a loop process take the form of a discrete sum over quasinormal modes. Technically, our method combines the dS spectral decomposition with dispersion relations. Using this technique, we bootstrap new results in a simple and intuitive form for 3-point and 4-point correlators with 1-loop massive exchanges of scalar and vector bosons, either directly or derivatively coupled. Applications of this bootstrap technique to higher spins and higher-loop banana graphs with dS covariant dispersions but noncovariant couplings are also straightforward.

### [34] [Quintessential $α$-attractors fit DESI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02701)
*Alessandro Borys,Joaquin Masias,Marco Scalisi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究 α-吸引子模型（α-attractor models）中的精质场（quintessence），以回应 DESI 近期对动态暗能量（dynamical dark energy）的观测指示。研究发现吸引子势的“膝点”（knee）可很好地近似 DESI 基准模型中使用的类轴子精质场（axion-like quintessence model），从而在轴子衰变常数 f_a 与吸引子参数 α 之间建立简单关系，并导出 α=O(1) 的偏好。数值求解背景动力学后，结果与 DESI 偏好的 w(z) 演化在 z∼O(1) 范围内吻合良好。文章还指出两类势的吻合反映了数据的共同要求：当前势能与斜率在普朗克单位下均处于哈勃尺度量级，并讨论了多场吸引子场景中初始条件的自然起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期 DESI 观测给出了动态暗能量的迹象，需要对精质场模型进行理论检验。本文旨在将 α-吸引子模型与 DESI 基准类轴子精质场模型建立联系，以解释观测结果并探索弦理论启发的参数偏好。

Method: 通过解析分析建立吸引子势“膝点”与类轴子势的对应关系，导出 f_a 与 α 之间的简单公式；并对背景动力学方程进行数值求解，计算 w(z) 的演化并与 DESI 偏好做比较。

Result: 吸引子势的“膝点”可精确近似类轴子精质场模型；实验约束转化为对 α=O(1) 的偏好，与弦理论预期一致；数值求解得到的 w(z) 演化在 z∼O(1) 范围内与 DESI 偏好吻合良好。

Conclusion: 类轴子势与吸引子势的吻合源于数据对当前势能与斜率均处于哈勃尺度量级的共同要求；多场吸引子场景可自然提供所需的初始条件。

Abstract: We study quintessence in $α$-attractor models in light of recent DESI indications for dynamical dark energy. We show that the \emph{knee} of the attractor potential provides an excellent approximation to the axion-like quintessence model used as a DESI benchmark. This leads to a simple relation between the axion decay constant $f_a$ and the attractor parameter $α$, allowing the experimental constraints to be translated into a preference for $α=\mathcal{O}(1)$, in agreement with string-motivated expectations. We solve the background dynamics numerically and find good agreement with the DESI-preferred evolution of $w(z)$ up to $z\sim\mathcal{O}(1)$. More generally, we point out that the agreement between axion-like and attractor potentials reflects a common requirement imposed by the data: today's potential energy and slope are both of order the Hubble scale in Planck units. We finally comment on the origin of the required initial conditions, which can naturally arise in multifield attractor scenarios.

### [35] [Perturbative construction of amplitudes from on-shell trees with vacuum pairs: the all-plus four-gluon amplitude through order $\boldsymbol{g}^{\boldsymbol{6}}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02702)
*M. Maniatis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种固定阶微扰壳上构建振幅（fixed-order perturbative on-shell construction of amplitudes）的方法，以树图振幅、真空对（vacuum pairs）和包含-排除符号（inclusion-exclusion signs）为基础，通过对色序四胶子全加振幅（color-ordered four-gluon all-plus amplitude）在g⁴和g⁶阶的检验，成功重现了单圈和双圈已知结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统圈图振幅计算在微扰论框架下复杂度随阶数急剧增加，需要一种系统性的壳上方法（on-shell method）来构建固定阶振幅，避免显式圈积分，并统一处理树图振幅与圈图贡献。

Method: 方法以粒子谱（particle spectrum）和允许的壳上三点振幅（on-shell three-point amplitudes）为基本输入，利用BCFW递推（BCFW recursion）生成树图振幅，并引入不可观测的状态-共轭壳上对（state-conjugate on-shell pairs），即真空对（vacuum pairs），对这些对在洛伦兹不变相空间（Lorentz-invariant phase space）上积分。相对符号通过重复相空间区域的包含-排除符号（inclusion-exclusion signs）分配。固定阶树图振幅的簿记以多边形（polygons）形式组织。

Result: 在g⁴阶，该构建重现了有限的有理单圈结果（finite rational one-loop result）。在g⁶阶，非零多边形扇区包括八边形（octagon）、六边形-四边形（hexagon-quadrilateral）、双五边形（two-pentagon）和三四边形（three-quadrilateral）扇区，它们共同重现了已知的平面（planar）、非平面（non-planar）和蝶形结（bow-tie）表达式。

Conclusion: 该固定阶壳上构建方法能有效将树图振幅与真空对相空间积分相结合，通过包含-排除符号处理重复区域，从而在g⁴和g⁶阶成功再现标准单圈和双圈贡献，为振幅计算提供了一种新的非传统框架。

Abstract: We formulate a fixed-order perturbative on-shell construction of amplitudes. The basic input is the particle spectrum together with the allowed on-shell three-point amplitudes. The construction is formulated in terms of tree amplitudes generated by BCFW recursion, supplemented by additional unobservable state-conjugate on-shell pairs, called vacuum pairs, and integrated over the Lorentz-invariant phase space of these pairs. The relative signs are assigned as inclusion-exclusion signs for repeated phase-space ranges in the on-shell construction.
  As a test case, we study the color-ordered four-gluon all-plus amplitude through orders $g^4$ and $g^6$, and compare the resulting signed phase-space sums with the standard one- and two-loop contributions. The fixed-order bookkeeping of the tree amplitudes is organized in terms of polygons. At order $g^4$ the construction reproduces the finite rational one-loop result. At order $g^6$ the non-vanishing polygon sectors are the octagon, hexagon-quadrilateral, two-pentagon, and three-quadrilateral sectors. Taken together, they reproduce the known planar, non-planar, and bow-tie expressions.

</details>


### [36] [Gravitational index, black hole saddle degeneracy, and one-form symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02707)
*Davide Cassani,Gianmarco Esposto*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文指出超对称黑洞对四维超共形场论指标中鞍点贡献是简并的，这种简并源于理论的一型对称性（one-form symmetry），并表现为鞍点作用量的对数修正。作者在不同全息（holographic）框架下探讨了一型对称性及其导致的鞍点简并的引力实现；为说明无限体积下一型对称性的自发破缺，他们采用小化学势的Cardy-like极限的引力实现，此时黑体退紧致化为黑膜（black brane）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知超对称黑洞在超共形场论指标中的鞍点是简并的，但简并的引力机制和一型对称性的角色尚未充分阐明。本文旨在通过全息对偶（holographic duality）建立一型对称性与鞍点简并之间的引力对应，并解释无限体积下单型对称性的自发破缺。

Method: 采用全息引力实现方法，在不同全息框架下分析一型对称性及其导致的指标鞍点简并；通过Cardy-like极限（小化学势极限）的引力实现，将黑体退紧致化为黑膜，从而展示一型对称性在无限体积下的自发破缺过程。

Result: 一型对称性导致的鞍点简并可以视为鞍点作用量的一种特定对数修正（logarithmic correction）；在无限体积下，一型对称性发生自发破缺，这一破缺过程通过黑体到黑膜的退紧致化转变得以在引力中实现。

Conclusion: 论文建立了一型对称性、鞍点简并和对数修正之间的全息联系，为超对称黑洞熵的简并性提供了引力解释，并揭示了无限体积下一型对称性自发破缺的几何机制。

Abstract: It is known that the saddle describing the contribution of supersymmetric black holes to the index of four-dimensional superconformal field theories is degenerate. This degeneracy is a consequence of the one-form symmetry of the theory, and can also be seen as a specific logarithmic correction to the saddle-point action. We discuss the gravitational realization of the one-form symmetry and of the index saddle degeneracy in different holographic setups. In order to illustrate the spontaneous breaking of the one-form symmetry at infinite volume, we employ a gravitational realization of the Cardy-like limit of small chemical potentials where the black hole decompactifies into a black brane.

### [37] [Supersymmetry, Large Extra Dimensions and the Gravitino Conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02708)
*Leonardo Bersigotti,Dieter Lust,Marco Scalisi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于引力子猜想（Gravitino Conjecture），通过引入各向异性指数（anisotropy exponent）α来参数化大额外维度的体积缩放关系，研究了超对称与额外维度信号缺失的关联性。结果表明，线性标度关系n=1仅与一或两个大额外维度兼容，且对应的超对称破缺机制取决于紧致化尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨超对称（supersymmetry）和额外维度（extra dimensions）实验信号缺失是否可被理解为一种关联现象，从而为缺乏相关实验证据提供理论解释。

Method: 基于引力子猜想，在四维N=1超引力（supergravity）框架下，通过各向异性指数α参数化内禀体积相对于大p-循环（large p-cycle）体积的缩放行为，推导相应的Kähler势体积贡献，并得到关于标度指数n和有效大维度数αp的约束条件。

Result: 线性关系n=1仅与一个或两个大额外维度兼容，这正是仍可在微米尺度（micron distances）被探测的情形。在此类场景中，微米大小的额外维度意味着轻引力子（gravitino）和规范中介超对称破缺（gauge-mediated supersymmetry breaking），而引力中介（gravity mediation）对应的紧致化尺度超出当前实验可及范围。

Conclusion: 超对称与额外维度信号的共同缺失可能源于内在的理论关联：仅当额外维度数为1或2时线性标度关系成立，这为当前实验未发现相关信号提供了一种自洽的理论解释，并区分了不同超对称破缺机制的可探测性。

Abstract: We investigate whether the absence of experimental signals for supersymmetry and extra dimensions can be understood as a correlated phenomenon. Assuming the Gravitino Conjecture, we study the relation between the gravitino mass and the Kaluza-Klein scale in four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=1$ supergravity from Type II compactifications with large extra dimensions. We parametrize the scaling of the full internal volume with respect to that of a large $p$-cycle through an anisotropy exponent $α$, and derive the corresponding volume contributions to the Kähler potential. This leads to constraints on the scaling exponent $n$, linking the gravitino mass to the KK scale, and on the effective number $αp$ of large dimensions. We find that the linear relation $n=1$ is compatible only with one or two large extra dimensions, precisely the cases that can still be probed at micron distances. In such scenarios, micron-sized extra dimensions imply a light gravitino and gauge-mediated supersymmetry breaking, whereas gravity mediation corresponds to compactification scales beyond current experimental reach.

A uniformly convergent functional perturbation series developed around universal, surprisingly simple, analytic non-perturbative background profiles corresponding to a partial resummation of the Borel-plane expansions suggested there, is constructed; a perfect match to what is known about the full solutions' local behaviour at zero and infinite radii is achieved, along with simple analytic prescriptions for the locally inaccessible numerical parameters therein.

### [39] [Kinematical correlations via $κ$-Poincaré coproducts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03004)
*Mohammad Ali Gorji,Babak Vakili*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了κ-Minkowski时空中Hopf代数动量合成律的运动学后果，揭示了不同坐标基下有序平面波标签与平移生成元本征值之间的非线性多支映射关系，以及由此产生的支依赖的κ-变形背对背动量关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在κ-Minkowski弯曲动量空间中，不同坐标基（如bicrossproduct基与classical基）对平移生成元本征值P_μ与有序平面波标签p_μ的映射关系不同，后者可能在高动量区域失去全局一一对应性。作者旨在厘清这种多支映射（multibranch mapping）结构的运动学含义及其对两粒子态动量关联的影响。

Method: 在bicrossproduct基下，有序平面波标签即为平移生成元本征值，映射一一对应；在classical基下，P_μ与p_μ通过非线性关系联系，部分区域可存在多个实数辅助原像。当出现多支情况时，支敏感量P_+≡P_0+P_4=κ e^{p_0/κ}进入余积（coproduct）并在两粒子态中分辨支。通过施加总动量为零的约束，得到支依赖的κ-变形背对背动量关联。作者还将该结构与标准自伴非相对论最小长度模型进行了对比。

Result: 在单支区域，两粒子的约束关联呈现为变形了的关联乘积（deformed correlated product）；在多支区域，仅由P_μ指定的态可展开为不同辅助支的叠加。若将P_μ视为物理动量，则物理内容是变形的关联模式；若将辅助变量p_μ赋予操作意义，同一约束态可被解释为不同辅助支上的叠加态。与标准非相对论最小长度模型对比，未发现类似的光滑局部两实支反转结构。

Conclusion: κ-Minkowski时空中classical基下的多支映射结构导致了两粒子态中支依赖的变形背对背关联，且该结构的物理解释依赖于P_μ和p_μ何者被赋予操作意义。这种多支行为是κ-变形动量空间特有的运动学效应，在标准最小长度模型中不存在类似结构。

Abstract: We study a kinematical consequence of the Hopf-algebraic momentum composition law in $κ$-Minkowski spacetime. The same curved momentum space can be described in different coordinates. In the bicrossproduct basis the ordered-plane-wave labels are the translation-generator eigenvalues, so the relevant map is one-to-one. In the classical basis, instead, the translation eigenvalues $P_μ$ are nonlinearly related to the ordered-plane-wave labels $p_μ$. This relation can fail to be globally one-to-one in a high-momentum region. When a given classical-basis four-momentum admits more than one real auxiliary preimage, the branch-sensitive quantity $P_+\equiv P_0+P_4=κe^{p_0/κ}$ enters the coproduct and resolves the branches in two-particle states. Imposing the vanishing total-momentum constraint therefore gives branch-dependent $κ$-deformed back-to-back momentum correlations. In a single-branch regime this is just a deformed correlated product, while in a multibranch regime a state specified only by $P_μ$ can be expanded into distinct auxiliary branches. If $P_μ$ are taken as the directly meaningful momenta, the physical content is the resulting deformed correlation pattern. If the auxiliary variables $p_μ$ are assigned operational meaning, the same constrained state can be interpreted as a superposition over different auxiliary branches. We also compare this structure with standard regular self-adjoint nonrelativistic minimal-length models and find no analogous smooth local two-real-branch inversion on their physical domains.

### [40] [Holographic complexity of de-Sitter black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03049)
*Chaoxi Fang,Jiayue Yang,Shao-Wen Wei,Ming Zhang,Robert B. Mann*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本论文在 Schwarzschild-de Sitter (SdS) 黑洞时空背景下，研究了静态片方案和 dS/CFT 对应方案两种 de Sitter 全息学框架下的复杂度行为，发现 CV 和 CV2.0 猜想在线性增长上一致，而 CA 猜想增长率为零，且两种方案的复杂度增长率完全等价。
