Method: 在 Schwarzschild-de Sitter (SdS) 黑洞时空下，分别采用静态片方案（static patch scheme）和 de Sitter/共形场论对应（dS/CFT correspondence）方案，评估 Complexity equals Volume (CV) 猜想，并扩展至余维零（codimension-zero）提议，包括 Complexity equals Spacetime Volume (CV2.0) 和 Complexity equals Action (CA)，通过构建 Wheeler-DeWitt (WDW) 片进行计算。

Result: 在 CV 和 CV2.0 猜想下，静态片全息复杂度与 dS/CFT 全息复杂度均呈现线性增长；在 CA 猜想下，两种方案的复杂度增长率均为零，归因于受限 WDW 区域内（正则化）作用的有限性。此外，静态片方案与 dS/CFT 方案的复杂度增长率完全相同。

Abstract: We investigate holographic complexity within the Schwarzschild-de Sitter (SdS) black hole spacetime. Two distinct de Sitter holography prescriptions are examined: the static patch scheme restricted to the stretched horizon and the de Sitter/Conformal Field Theory (dS/CFT) correspondence scheme defined at asymptotic future and past infinities. We evaluate the Complexity equals Volume (CV) conjecture and extend the analysis to codimension-zero proposals, specifically Complexity equals Spacetime Volume (CV2.0) and Complexity equals Action (CA), through the Wheeler-DeWitt (WDW) patch we construct. The behaviors of the complexity in the static patch holography at late time and in the dS/CFT at infinite spacelike boundary coordinate are studied, respectively. We find that under both the CV and CV2.0 conjectures, the static patch holographic complexity and the dS/CFT holographic complexity consistently exhibit linear growth. Conversely, regarding the CA conjecture, the holographic complexity growth rates for both the static patch and the dS/CFT correspondence vanish. This behavior is attributed to the finiteness of the (regularized) action within the restricted WDW region. Furthermore, it is demonstrated that the complexity growth rate of the static patch scheme is identical to that in the dS/CFT scheme. This equivalence implies the existence of a unified description for bulk dynamics within de Sitter holography.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究通常依赖具体模型或微扰展开（perturbative expansions）来处理外磁场中的量子场论，缺乏一个普适的、基于对称性的统一理解。本文旨在从磁平移与磁旋转对称性出发，以模型无关的方式揭示这些对称性对关联函数的一般性约束。

Result: 发现磁平移对称性约束带电算符关联函数必须包含施温格相位，并可分解为一个规范协变相位因子（gauge-covariant phase factor）与一个仅依赖相对坐标的约化关联函数（reduced correlator）。进一步推导了两点函数基于磁平移代数表示的谱表示，并指出朗道规范（Landau gauge）与对称规范（symmetric gauge）的描述对应于该表示中不同基的选择。

Conclusion: 本文为外磁场中的量子场论提供了一个统一的、基于对称性的理论框架，该框架不依赖于特定模型或规范选择，能够系统地处理关联函数的对称性约束问题。

Abstract: Quantum field theories in the presence of a static and uniform external magnetic field possess two characteristic spatial symmetries: magnetic translations and magnetic rotation. We investigate general consequences of these symmetries on correlation functions from a model-independent perspective, without relying on specific models or perturbative expansions. The projective structure of magnetic translation symmetry constrains correlation functions of charged operators to acquire the Schwinger phase and leads to a factorized form into a gauge-covariant phase factor and a reduced correlator depending only on relative coordinates. We further derive the spectral representation of two-point functions in terms of representations of the magnetic translation algebra, in which the Landau- and symmetric-gauge descriptions arise as different choices of basis. Our results provide a unified symmetry-based framework for quantum field theories in external magnetic fields.

Motivation: NUT荷（NUT charge）在黑洞热力学中引入额外的热力学自由度，但如何将其一致地纳入热力学态空间（thermodynamic state space）尚未完全明确。本文旨在为Kerr-Newman-NUT-AdS₄时空建立一个包含多个次级毛（secondary hairs）的自洽热力学框架。

Method: 将NUT荷通过两个次级毛——转动类毛发$J_n=mn/K^2$和电荷类毛发$N=n/\sqrt K$——引入均匀热力学态空间，结合电荷、压力、角动量和弦张力（string tensions），推导出紧致形式的Christodoulou-Ruffini型平方质量公式。对该状态方程求导，得到视界温度、角速度、电势、NUT势（NUT potential）、热力学体积和热力学长度，并代数验证第一定律（first law）和Smarr关系（Smarr relation）。

Result: 得到了包含NUT相关次级毛的平方质量公式及其对应的第一定律与Smarr关系；论证了NUT荷参数并非额外的度量参数，而是热力学响应变量（thermodynamic response variables）；讨论了其他一致的NUT参数化方案（包括基于对偶质量（dual mass）的方案），并阐明了热力学体积的选择与NUT扇区（NUT sector）的关联。

Conclusion: 该构造提供了一个受控实例，展示了当仅凭第一定律一致性不足以唯一确定态空间时，如何为AdS黑洞（AdS black hole）选取合适的态空间。

Abstract: We formulate multihair thermodynamics for Kerr-Newman-NUT-AdS$_4$ spacetimes with symmetric Misner strings and conical deficits. The NUT charge parameter enters the homogeneous thermodynamic state space through two secondary hairs: a rotation-like hair $J_n=mn/K^2$ and a charge-like hair $N=n/\sqrt K$. They are not additional metric parameters, but thermodynamic response variables in the enlarged state space. Together with the electric charge, pressure, angular momentum, and string tensions, these variables yield a compact Christodoulou-Ruffini-type squared-mass formula. Differentiating this equation of state gives the horizon temperature, angular velocities, electric potential, NUT potential, thermodynamic volume, and thermodynamic lengths, and the resulting first law and Smarr relation are verified algebraically. We also discuss alternative consistent NUT parametrizations, including one based on the dual mass, and clarify how the choice of thermodynamic volume is tied to the chosen NUT sector. The construction gives a controlled example of how an AdS black hole state space can be selected when first law consistency alone is not unique.

</details>


### [47] [Flowing with Displacements and Tilts: Surface Operators in $O(N)$ Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03974)
*Jake Belton,Nadav Drukker,Biswajit Sahoo*

TL;DR: 本文利用共形微扰论（conformal perturbation theory）系统研究了缺陷共形场论（defect conformal field theory）中的位移算子（displacement）和倾斜算子（tilt）及其重整化群（renormalization group）流，在4-ε维Wilson-Fisher O(N)模型及其他多标量场理论中构建了新解，并发现了缺陷共形流形非单连通时可能存在涡旋（vortex）等新特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用共形微扰论（conformal perturbation theory）构建分析框架，该方法能够简洁地再现临界Wilson-Fisher O(N)模型在4-ε维中的已知结果，并可推广至其他多标量场理论。通过该方法系统计算位移和倾斜算子的归一化系数在流过程中的变化。

Result: 在所有研究的系统中，算子流动过程均为短程且完全可控，位移和倾斜归一化系数的变化可被精确追踪。此外，论文指出当缺陷共形流形非单连通（not simply connected）时，可能存在涡旋（vortex）等新颖结构。

Conclusion: 共形微扰论为研究缺陷共形场论中的位移和倾斜算子及其流动提供了一种有效且可推广的框架，不仅复现了已有结果，还构建了新的解，并揭示了缺陷流形拓扑性质相关的非平凡特征。该工作部分依赖生成式人工智能辅助。

Abstract: Defect conformal field theories have special operators of protected dimension known as displacements and tilts. They arise due to the breaking of global symmetries by the defect and the normalisations of their two-point functions are characteristics of the defect. In the case of surface defects, these normalisations are related to some of the anomaly coefficients in the surface effective action. To study these operators and their flows between different defect renormalization group fixed points we present an elegant approach using conformal perturbation theory that easily reproduces the known examples from the critical Wilson-Fisher $O(N)$ model in $4-\varepsilon$ dimensions and allows us to construct new ones in other multiscalar theories. In all the systems that we study the flows are short and under full control, as is the change of the displacement and tilt normalizations. We point out some novel features like the existence of vortices when the defect conformal manifold is not simply connected. In addition to regular human labour, this work relied heavily on generative AI; see full disclosure in methodology section.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Recent observations, particularly from DESI, have provided intriguing hints of dynamical behaviour in late-time dark energy. A central challenge in these models, however, lies in determining the precise functional form of $f(R)$. Nevertheless, several viable models have been proposed that successfully reproduce the standard $Λ$CDM cosmology at high red shifts while generating late-time cosmic acceleration without an explicit dark energy component. Within this framework, the evolution of the linear matter density contrast becomes scale dependent, leading to a growth index that varies with both scale and redshift. In this work, we explore the capability of forthcoming 21 cm observations to constrain the growth index, as well as the combined neutral hydrogen (HI) bias and growth-rate parameter. Our results indicate that future 21 cm surveys can provide meaningful, though moderate, support for these modified gravity scenarios.

### [49] [Modeling Discrete Data with High-Order Vector Potts Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03429)
*Aaron De Clercq,Merijn Moody,Clélia de Mulatier*

Main category: stat.ME

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类完整的最大熵模型——q态自旋模型（q-state spin models），将矢量Potts模型（vector Potts model）推广至包含任意高阶相互作用（high-order interactions）的离散数据场景，并利用配分函数的圈展开（loop expansion）揭示了相互作用代数结构与统计性质之间的内在联系，同时定义了规范变换（gauge transformations）以实现不同阶相互作用模型间的统一表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维数据建模对理解复杂系统至关重要，但现有最大熵模型（如伊辛模型Ising model和Potts模型）主要局限于捕捉两两相互作用（pairwise interactions）。近期对三体及以上高阶关联模式（higher-order correlation patterns）的关注日益增加，但已有工作多局限于二值数据（binary data）的高阶伊辛模型，缺乏适用于更一般离散数据（discrete data）的统一理论框架。

Method: 引入q态自旋模型族，作为最大熵模型（maximum entropy models）的完整推广，将矢量Potts模型扩展至包含长程（long-range）和任意高阶相互作用。通过配分函数的圈展开证明，自旋模型的统计性质完全由其相互作用的代数结构决定；定义规范变换，在该变换下相互作用结构及配分函数保持不变。针对实际数据分析，将二值情形下的最小复杂模型（Minimally Complex Models）推广至离散数据，并推导出其边际似然（marginal likelihood）的闭式表达式。

Result: 在只考虑两两相互作用的情况下，所提模型比标准矢量Potts模型支持更多样化的相互作用类型。规范等价的模型可视为同一抽象统计模型的不同表示，尽管它们通常具有不同阶数的相互作用，从而将二值情形的结果推广至一般离散数据。最小复杂模型的边际似然具有闭式解，实现了快速的模型选择（model selection）。

Conclusion: 本文建立的q态自旋模型框架为离散数据中的高阶相互作用建模提供了统一的理论工具，并通过简单真实世界示例展示了其实用价值。

Abstract: Modeling high-dimensional data is challenging, yet essential to understanding many complex systems. Maximum entropy models such as Ising and Potts models have been used extensively to capture pairwise interactions from correlation patterns in data, allowing to infer graphical representations of complex systems from observations (e.g., from protein sequences or neural population activity). Recently, there has been growing interest in modeling higher-order correlation patterns involving simultaneously three or more variables. While progress has been made in binary data with high-order Ising models, we extend this framework to the more general case of discrete data.
  We introduce q-state spin models, a complete family of maximum entropy models that generalize the vector Potts model to include long-range and arbitrary high-order interactions. In the pairwise case, our models allow for more diverse interaction types compared to the standard vector Potts model. We discuss their statistical interpretation with examples and relate them to discrete Fourier analysis. Using a loop expansion of the partition function, we show that the statistical properties of spin models are fully captured by the algebraic structure of their interactions. We define gauge transformations under which this structure, and thus the partition function, remains invariant. Models equivalent under gauge transformations can be seen as different representations of the same abstract statistical model, despite generally having interactions of different orders, extending results from the binary case. For practical application to data analysis, we focus on a subset of models known in the binary case as Minimally Complex Models, generalizing them to discrete data. We obtain a closed-form expression for the marginal likelihood of these models, enabling fast model selection. We illustrate their use with simple real-world examples.

</details>

### [50] [An Asymptotic Theory of Chain-of-Thought in In-Context Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03217)
*Kaito Takanami,Cengiz Pehlevan*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文通过一个理论可解的链式思维（chain-of-thought, CoT）推理模型，结合随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）在高维渐近条件下的解析工具，推导了泛化误差随推理深度、预训练数据量和上下文长度变化的精确公式，揭示了指数与多项式改进、饱和及过度思考之间的相变（phase transition）行为，并验证了深层推理在充足预训练和上下文条件下最有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管链式思维（chain-of-thought, CoT）推理已被广泛用于激发大语言模型（large language models）的多步推理能力，但CoT深度（即推理步骤数量）对泛化（generalization）的标度行为（scaling behavior）尚不明确。本文旨在从理论上系统理解测试时CoT深度如何影响泛化性能。

Method: 研究线性回归（linear regression）上下文内权重预测（in-context weight prediction）场景，将测试时推理建模为权重参数估计的迭代精炼过程。利用高维渐近条件下的随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）工具，推导泛化误差（generalization error）作为推理深度、预训练数据量和上下文长度函数的精确公式。

Result: 分析揭示了指数与多项式改进、饱和及过度思考（overthinking）之间的尖锐相变（phase transition），并刻画了最优推理深度（optimal reasoning depth）的标度行为。更深层推理在预训练信息与上下文信息充分时最有效，而有限的预训练或上下文会导致长推理易出现误差放大或饱和。

Conclusion: 通过在完全学习的线性注意力（linear attention）和软最大注意力（softmax attention）模型上的实验验证了理论预测。该结果为测试时CoT深度如何影响泛化提供了统一的理论解释。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning has become a widely used mechanism for eliciting multi-step reasoning in large language models by generating intermediate reasoning steps at inference time. Yet the scaling behavior of generalization with CoT depth remains poorly understood. To address this question, we study a theoretically solvable model of CoT for in-context weight prediction in linear regression, where test-time reasoning is represented as an iterative refinement of the weight-parameter estimate. Using tools from random matrix theory under high-dimensional asymptotics, we derive an exact formula for the generalization error as a function of reasoning depth, pretraining data amount, and context length. Our analysis reveals a sharp phase transition separating exponential and polynomial improvement, saturation, and overthinking, and characterizes how the optimal reasoning depth scales. We further show that deeper reasoning is most effective with sufficiently rich pretraining and in-context information, whereas limited pretraining or context makes longer reasoning prone to error amplification or saturation. We also validate these predictions through experiments on fully learned linear attention and softmax attention models. Our results provide a unified theoretical account of how test-time CoT depth affects generalization.

### [51] [Data-Driven Forecasting of three-Component Seismograms Using Transformer Architectures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02912)
*Waleed Esmail,Stuart Russell,Jana Klinge,Alexander Kappes,Christine Thomas*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出 SeismoGPT——一种基于Transformer的自回归模型（autoregressive model），直接在地震波形时域（time domain）中预测三分量波形。该方法将预测形式化为受物理约束的延拓问题，在合成地震图上中位归一化互相关（median normalized cross correlation）超过0.93，成功保留了相位一致性与频谱能量分布，展示了Transformer基础模型在物理驱动时间序列预测中的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于地震波传播具有非线性（nonlinear）、色散（dispersive）和多尺度（multi-scale）特性，超出观测数据范围的地震波形预测仍然极具挑战。现有方法难以同时捕获波场的相位与能量演化规律。

Method: 采用Transformer架构的自回归模型 SeismoGPT，直接在时域中预测三分量（three-component）地震波形。预测被视为一个物理约束的延拓问题：模型接收从P波到时起并延伸至S波过后一段时间的波形上下文，之后递归生成未来运动，不再依赖真实样本。评估采用三种配置，以距离归一化上下文比（distance-normalized context ratio）和固定预测时窗（120 s和240 s）区分上下文长度与预测范围的影响。

Result: 在所有评估配置下，模型的中位归一化互相关（median normalized cross correlation）超过0.93。成功预测保留了相位相干性（phase coherence）与频谱能量分布（spectral energy distribution）。失败案例主要源于自回归递推过程中的相位逐渐漂移（phase drift），而非产生非物理信号。

Conclusion: 基于Transformer的序列模型能够学习地震波场的稳定动力学延拓（stable dynamical continuation），表明基础模型方法（foundation-model approaches）在物理驱动时间序列预测方面潜力巨大。该技术在地震预警与减灾中具有潜在应用前景，特别是针对下一代引力波观测站（如爱因斯坦望远镜 Einstein Telescope）。

Abstract: Forecasting seismic waveforms beyond observed data remains challenging due to the nonlinear, dispersive, and multi-scale nature of seismic wave propagation. In this work, we introduce \textsc{SeismoGPT}, a transformer-based autoregressive model designed to forecast three-component seismic waveforms directly in the time domain. Forecasting is formulated as a physically constrained continuation problem in which the model receives waveform context beginning at the P-wave arrival and extending a defined time beyond the S-wave arrival, after which future motion is generated recursively without access to ground-truth samples. Evaluation is performed on synthetic seismograms spanning source depths of 5--100\,km, epicentral distances of 10--90$^\circ$, and magnitudes $3 \leq M_w \leq 7$. To disentangle the effects of context length and prediction horizon, we define three evaluation configurations using a distance-normalized context ratio and fixed prediction horizons of 120 and 240\,s. Across all configurations, the model achieves median normalized cross correlation above 0.93. Analysis of representative forecasts shows that successful predictions preserve both phase coherence and spectral energy distribution. Where failure cases arise, this is primarily due to gradual phase drift during autoregressive rollout rather than unphysical signal generation. These results demonstrate that transformer-based sequence models can learn stable dynamical continuation of seismic wavefields, highlighting the potential of foundation-model approaches for physics-driven time-series forecasting. There are potential applications of this methodology in seismic warning and hazard mitigation, particularly for next-generation gravitational-wave observatories, such as the Einstein Telescope.

### [52] [Turbulence: An Entropic Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03139)
*Christian Beck,Constantino Tsallis*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过最大化广义熵泛函 $S_{q,δ}$，在标准动能约束下导出广义正则分布，该分布与泰勒-库埃特高湍流中速度差的实验概率密度完美吻合。湍流级联的终点由参数 $δ=3/2$ 描述，该值在黑洞物理中同样扮演重要角色。在 Kolmogorov 尺度 $r=η$ 处，所有可观测涡旋结构消失，与黑洞视界现象类比。研究将统计力学推广至非可加熵泛函，使其适用于湍流，并建立了 $δ$ 与 $q$ 之间的理论关系（$δ^{-1}(r)=2-q(r)$），经高精度实验数据验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统统计力学基于可加（additive）熵泛函，难以直接描述湍流这类强非平衡、非可加系统。本文旨在将统计力学推广至更一般的非可加熵泛函 $S_{q,δ}$，使其能够统一描述湍流现象，并揭示湍流与黑洞物理之间的深层类比。

Method: 在标准动能约束下最大化广义熵泛函 $S_{q,δ}$，得到广义正则分布（generalized canonical distributions），即拉伸 $q$-指数（stretched $q$-exponentials）分布。利用非广延统计力学（nonextensive statistical mechanics）中的伴随形式体系（escort formalism），导出 $δ^{-1}(r)=2-q(r)$ 这一理论关系，并将实验结果与理论预测进行对比验证。

Result: 理论导出的广义正则分布与高湍流泰勒-库埃特流（Taylor-Couette flow）中速度差概率密度的实测数据高度吻合。在 Kolmogorov 长度尺度 $r=η$ 处，参数 $δ=3/2$，此时速度差的三阶矩（third moment）不复存在，所有涡旋结构消失。实验数据很好地验证了 $δ^{-1}(r)=2-q(r)$ 这一理论关系。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入广义非可加熵泛函 $S_{q,δ}$，成功将统计力学框架拓展至湍流系统，并与黑洞物理中的熵方法建立了有趣的类比。该工作为湍流的统计力学描述提供了新视角，同时揭示了湍流级联终点与黑洞视界之间的概念相似性。

Abstract: We show that maximizing the generalized entropic functional $S_{q,δ}$ subject to standard kinetic energy constraints provides generalized canonical distributions that agree perfectly with measured probability densities of velocity differences at distance $r$ in highly-turbulent Taylor-Couette flow. The end point of the turbulent cascade is described by $δ=\frac{3}{2}$, a parameter value that also plays an important role in black-hole physics. At this point the Kolmogorov length scale $r=η$ is reached and all observable eddy structures of the turbulent flow disappear, in certain analogy to what is observed for black holes at the event horizon. Our approach generalizes statistical mechanics to more general nonadditive entropic functionals $S_{q,δ}$ such that it is applicable to turbulent flows. This approach asymptotically generates stretched $q$-exponentials as generalized canonical distributions relevant for turbulent flow, with a particular dependence of the stretching exponent $δ^{-1}$ on $q$ that follows from the well-known escort formalism in nonextensive statistical mechanics. Along this particular line in the parameter space, the physics can be described by $S_q$ on its own with suitable escort constraints, leading to the prediction $δ^{-1} (r) =2-q(r)$, thus allowing for a consistent thermodynamic description since $S_q$ is both trace-form and composable. We show that the above theoretically derived relation is well satisfied by measured high-precision experimental data for Taylor-Couette flow. At the Kolmogorov length scale $r=η$, the endpoint of our scenario, one has $δ=\frac{3}{2}$ and at this point the third moment of velocity differences ceases to exist and all eddies disappear. We point out various analogies with thermodynamic entropic approaches to black hole physics.

</details>

# hep-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [53] [Chiral Quark Soliton Model And Nucleon Parton Distribution Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03042)
*Masashi Wakamatsu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文阐述手征夸克孤子模型（CQSM）作为重子有效夸克模型，如何凭借其对非定域夸克-夸克关联的处理能力，成功预测了核子内多种夸克分布函数，特别是非极化与纵向极化海夸克（反夸克）分布函数中的味不对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手征夸克孤子模型（CQSM）虽在重子观测量预测上优于Skyrme模型，但其对核子内夸克分布函数（quark distribution functions）的预测机制尚未得到系统阐明，因此需要深入解析其成功的原因与方式。

Method: 基于CQSM框架，通过处理双线性夸克算符（bilinear quark operators）在光锥分离（light-cone separation）下的核子矩阵元（nucleon matrix elements），计算各类夸克分布函数，并特别分析非极化与纵向极化海夸克分布中的味不对称性（flavor asymmetry）。

Result: CQSM能够成功预测核子内多种类型的夸克分布函数，尤其是非极化与纵向极化海夸克（反夸克）分布函数中的味不对称性。

Conclusion: CQSM相较于有效介子理论框架的核心优势在于其能够处理非定域夸克-夸克关联（non-local quark–quark correlations），这一能力对于从理论上预测核子夸克分布函数具有决定性意义。

Abstract: The chiral quark soliton model (CQSM) is an effective quark model of baryons maximally taking account of the most important feature of low-energy QCD, i.e., the spontaneous chiral symmetry breaking of the QCD vacuum and the associated appearance of Nambu--Goldstone pions. It shares many common features with the famous Skyrme model in that the baryons are viewed as rotating hedgehog objects in both models. Despite many similarities, it turned out that the CQSM can give more realistic predictions on most baryon observables. Above all, a decisive advantage of the CQSM over the Skyrme-like models is that it can handle non-local quark--quark correlations in baryons, which is absolutely impossible within the framework of effective meson theories. This feature is decisively important for making theoretical predictions on the quark distribution functions inside the nucleon, which are defined as nucleon matrix elements of bilinear quark operators with light-cone separation. In the present paper, we try to elucidate why and how the CQSM can give successful predictions for a variety of types of nucleon quark distribution functions, especially for the flavor asymmetry of the unpolarized and longitudinally polarized sea-quark (anti-quark) distribution functions in the nucleon.

</details>

We discuss selected results obtained with Dyson-Schwinger equations (DSE) and the functional renormalisation group (fRG) in the context of a general physics perspective on the QCD phase diagram. This article is specifically aimed at students and non-practitioners of functional methods alike and may serve as a short guide to further literature.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Determining the neutrino mass ordering remains a central open problem in particle physics. While next-generation long-baseline experiments are expected to resolve this question, current data provide limited sensitivity because the spectral differences between normal and inverted ordering are subtle and entangled with parameter degeneracies. We investigate a machine-learning strategy for mass-ordering determination using a feed-forward neural-network classifier trained on synthetic long-baseline datasets generated with three-flavour oscillation probabilities, matter effects, and statistical fluctuations. We evaluate the classifier against standard $χ^2$ and $\log\mathcal{L}$ approaches using common discrimination metrics, including receiver-operating-characteristic curves, to quantify sensitivity and to illustrate how operating points can be selected to prioritise purity or efficiency. We find that the neural network achieves performance comparable to conventional fits for the scenarios studied, providing a flexible, independent cross-check of established analyses. The framework can be extended to incorporate systematic uncertainties and to explore joint inference of oscillation parameters, and it may also serve as a pedagogical tool for introducing machine-learning methods in neutrino physics.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PTA实验报道的纳赫兹随机引力波背景需要宇宙学解释；亚稳宇宙弦是一种有前景的机制，但以往研究多假设零温下通过单极子成核（monopole nucleation）衰变，未充分考虑热等离子体环境中有限温度效应的影响。

Result: 热等离子体中弦形成后，主导衰变通道是弦世界面上的热诱导成核而非零温单极子成核；同时满足可行的一阶相变（first-order transition）和PTA兼容的引力波信号的条件将模型参数空间限制在(sin²θ_w, √β)平面内的狭窄区域，其中θ_w为暗扇区弱混合角（weak mixing angle），β≡M_Φ²/M_Z²为希格斯-玻色子与Z玻色子的质量平方比；热效应显著改变零温图像，将PTA兼容区域移向更小的暗精细结构常数（dark fine-structure constant）α'和更大的单极子-弦张力比（monopole-to-string-tension ratio）κ。

Conclusion: 热效应对亚稳宇宙弦的衰变动力学至关重要，忽略有限温度效应会导致对PTA兼容参数空间的错误估计；该研究为纳赫兹引力波背景的宇宙弦起源提供了更完整的理论框架。

Abstract: Metastable cosmic strings provide a cosmological interpretation of the nanohertz stochastic gravitational wave background reported by Pulsar Timing Array (PTA) experiments. We revisit this scenario in a minimal dark-sector gauge theory, in which a complex Higgs doublet breaks $\mathrm{SU}(2)\times\mathrm{U}(1)\to\mathrm{U}(1)$ at a single symmetry-breaking scale. This one-scale setup predicts metastable $Z$-strings whose endpoints are monopole-like defects, and whose zero-temperature decay rate is controlled by the gauge couplings and mass ratios. We show that, once the string-forming transition occurs in a thermal plasma, the dominant decay channel is not the zero-temperature monopole nucleation but thermally induced nucleation on the string worldsheet. We determine the nucleation temperature, $T_{\rm nuc}$, from the one-loop finite-temperature effective potential with daisy resummation, and use it to compute the string formation temperature throughout the model parameter space. Requiring both a viable first-order transition and a PTA-compatible gravitational wave signal selects a narrow region in the model parameter space, in the $(\sin^2θ_w,\sqrtβ)$ plane, where $θ_w$ is the dark-sector weak mixing angle and $β\equiv M_Φ^2/M_{Z}^2$ is the squared Higgs-to-$Z$ mass ratio. Thermal effects modify the zero-temperature picture significantly, shifting the PTA-compatible region towards lower values of the dark fine-structure constant $α'$ and larger values of the monopole-to-string-tension ratio $κ$.

Abstract: We present a four-dimensional deconstruction of the extra-dimensional axion arising from a $U(1)$ gauge theory in a five-dimensional orbifold, where the axion is identified with the Wilson line of the $U(1)$ gauge field and its coupling to QCD is generated by a 5D Chern-Simons (CS) term. We construct the corresponding 4D moose (quiver) gauge theory with link scalar fields, in which the axion emerges as a collective pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson. The axion-gluon coupling is described by a gauged Wess-Zumino-Witten term, providing the 4D counterpart of the 5D CS term. We further analyze non-perturbative effects from zero-mode and ``fractional'' instanton configurations. While the latter is exponentially suppressed in the regime corresponding to the 5D description, ensuring consistency with the higher-dimensional picture, we point out that this suppression can break down for smaller instantons whose inverse size exceeds the 5D cutoff scale, leading to a potentially significant effect. We also study axion potentials induced by bulk matter fields and boundary-localized symmetry-breaking operators, reproducing the characteristic nonlocal suppression associated with propagation in the extra dimension. Our construction provides a renormalizable 4D framework with a transparent understanding of the axion shift symmetry and its quality.

  <summary>Details</summary>

As a consequence, the reheating temperature consistent with the observed dark matter abundance exhibits a maximum value, $T_{\rm reh}^{\rm reak}$, which decreases as $M_{1/2}$ increases. This behavior gives rise to a tension between prospective lower bounds on the gluino mass from future collider searches and the high reheating temperatures required for successful thermal leptogenesis. In this work, we investigate a nonstandard cosmological scenario in which the thermal bath is supplemented by an additional scalar field. We show that, for a matter-like equation of state, this component can induce a substantial dilution of the gravitino abundance, thereby allowing significantly larger values of the reheating temperature. In contrast, for a kination-like equation of state, the gravitino abundance is enhanced rather than diluted, leading to a reduction of the maximum allowed reheating temperature.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最近的研究提出夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）中开放粲强子（open-charm hadrons）的顺序强子化（sequential hadronization）机制——束缚更紧的Dₛ⁺在约1.2 T_c附近先形成，D⁰在T_c处后形成——并发现该机制相对于常规同步强子化基线，可反转D⁰与Dₛ⁺之间椭圆流劈裂（elliptic-flow splitting）的符号。本文旨在验证事件形状工程（ESE）能否比仅依赖包容测量（inclusive measurements）更清晰地区分这两种图像。

Method: 在Pb-Pb对撞（√s_NN = 5.02 TeV）的0–10%和30–50%中心度类中，选取大q₂事件和小q₂事件，通过分离粲介子v₂的几何驱动增强与强子化时间响应，对比顺序强子化与同步强子化基线下的D⁰与Dₛ⁺椭圆流劈裂Δv₂及其随q₂的系统性变化，并分析响应斜率χ的物种依赖性层次。

Result: 顺序强子化场景中，正值的Δv₂(D⁰ – Dₛ⁺)随q₂系统性增大，响应斜率χ呈现χ(D⁰) > χ(Dₛ⁺)的物种依赖性层次，且该层次对整体流归一化具有鲁棒性；同步基线中，劈裂接近零或负值且不遵循相同的几何标度（geometry scaling）。30–50%半中心类因QGP寿命与初始离心率（initial eccentricity）的非单调相互作用，成为最优观测窗口。q₂分档下的Dₛ⁺/D⁰产额比接近1，证实劈裂源于动力学流效应而非化学产额修正。

Conclusion: Δv₂(D⁰ – Dₛ⁺)与ESE下的响应斜率χ可作为互补的微分探针（differential probes），用于探测QCD相变温度附近粲强子化的时空结构。

Abstract: Recent work has proposed sequential hadronization of open-charm hadrons in the quark-gluon plasma, wherein more tightly bound species such as $D_s^+$ form earlier near $1.2 T_c$ and $D^0$ forms later at $T_c$. That work showed that this mechanism naturally reverses the sign of the $D^0-D_s^+$ elliptic-flow splitting relative to the conventional simultaneous baseline. In this work, we demonstrate that event-shape engineering (ESE) provides a sharper discrimination between the two pictures than inclusive measurements alone. By selecting large-$q_2$ and small-$q_2$ events in 0--10\% and 30--50\% centrality classes in Pb-Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\mathrm{NN}}}=5.02$ TeV, we show that the geometry-driven enhancement of charm-meson $v_2$ can be separated from the hadronization-time response: the positive $Δv_2(D^0-D_s^+)$ in the sequential scenario grows systematically with $q_2$, while the corresponding response slope $χ$ reveals a species-dependent hierarchy $χ(D^0) > χ(D_s^+)$ that is robust against the overall flow normalization and absent in the simultaneous baseline. In the simultaneous case, the splitting is near zero or negative and does not follow the same geometry scaling. Notably, the semi-central 30--50\% class emerges as the optimal window, because the non-monotonic interplay between QGP lifetime and initial eccentricity maximizes the late-stage flow conversion. The $q_2$ ratios of the $D_s^+/D^0$ yield ratio remain close to unity, confirming that the splitting is a dynamical flow effect rather than a chemical yield modification. These results establish $Δv_2(D^0-D_s^+)$ and the response slope $χ$ under ESE as complementary differential probes of the space-time structure of charm hadronization near the QCD transition temperature.

</details>


### [62] [The Polymorphic Chiral Anomaly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03619)
*Christopher Smith*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种完全通用的手征反常（chiral anomaly）统一表达式，涵盖了阿贝尔型（abelian）、单态型（singlet）、一致型（consistent）和协变型（covariant）等多种实现形式。该表达式通过包含三角图（triangle）、箱图（box）和五边形图（pentagon）来描述有质量或无质量费米子情形下的反常。论文同时提供了基于FeynCalc的实现代码，并利用斯托克斯定理（Stokes' theorem）绕开微分几何语言对各形式的拓扑方面进行了阐述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手征反常以阿贝尔型、单态型、一致型、协变型等多种形式呈现，表现形式多样且缺乏统一描述。本文旨在提供一种完全通用的反常表达式，并在此基础上清晰推导出各种传统形式，从而在技术和概念上提供一种统一理解手征反常各形式的强大工具。

Method: 首先推导出一个完全通用的手征反常表达式，该表达式适用于有质量或无质量费米子，不仅包括标准三角图，还纳入了箱图和五边形图。随后，从这一主表达式出发透明地推导出各种传统形式的反常。在拓扑方面，完全绕过微分几何语言（仅借助斯托克斯定理）对各形式的拓扑性质进行描述。此外，提供了基于FeynCalc的计算实现代码以便读者复现所有结果。

Result: 得到了一个完全通用的手征反常主表达式，能够统一描述阿贝尔型、单态型、一致型和协变型等多种反常形式。通过该表达式可以透明地推导出各种传统反常形式。在不使用微分几何语言（仅用斯托克斯定理）的条件下，对各形式的拓扑方面进行了描述。提供了可复现的FeynCalc实现代码。

Conclusion: 通过简化并统一描述手征反常的所有形式，本文凸显了其背后潜在的概念之美，并为全面理解相关物理提供了综合性视角。该工作无论在技术计算还是概念理解层面均具有重要价值。

Abstract: The chiral anomaly famously manifests in a rich variety of forms, from abelian and singlet to consistent or covariant. In this paper, all these realizations are described in detail, along with their properties and phenomenological applications. Central to this presentation is a novel expression for the fully generic chiral anomaly, derived with either massive or massless fermions, that incorporates not only the standard triangle but also the box and pentagon diagrams. From this master expression, the various traditional forms of the anomaly are then transparently derived. This provides a powerful tool, technically and conceptually, driving two further objectives. First, the topological aspects of each form are dutifully described while bypassing the differential language entirely, save for Stokes' theorem. Second, to make sure anyone interested can truly reproduce all the results in a reasonable amount of time, a FeynCalc implementation of the relevant calculations is provided. Ultimately, this simplified and unified description of all the forms of the chiral anomaly highlights the underlying conceptual beauty, and offers a comprehensive grasp of the physics at play.

</details>

### [63] [QUIVER: Quantum-Informed Views for Enhanced Representations in Large ML Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02785)
*Aritra Bal,Michael Binder,Markus Klute,Benedikt Maier,Michael Spannowsky*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出QUIVER（量子信息视图增强表示）范式，通过从变分量子电路（VQC）中提取量子Fisher信息矩阵作为几何驱动的特征视图，为经典机器学习模型提供互补模态输入。该方法在QM9分子性质预测和JetClass喷注味识别两个基准数据集上提升了标准性能指标，表明量子几何特征在容错量子硬件到来之前即可为经典任务带来可衡量的价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型机器学习模型受益于多模态输入提供的互补视角，但经典特征增强方法难以捕获高阶统计结构。量子Fisher信息矩阵（quantum Fisher information matrix）编码了学习到的量子态流形（quantum state manifold）的内在几何结构，这种由量子信息论（quantum information theory）启发的特征映射通常难以用经典方式建模，却能揭示经典数据和模型容量难以学习的统计结构，因此作者旨在将其作为一种真正互补而非冗余的模态引入经典学习框架。

Method: QUIVER范式通过训练一个与主任务相同的变分量子电路（variational quantum circuit, VQC），从中提取量子Fisher信息矩阵作为几何驱动的、与基无关的高阶相关性摘要，并将其融合到经典数据驱动特征中。这种融合通过对基础架构进行定向修改来实现，使量子几何信息能够被整合到广泛的模型架构中。

Result: 在QM9分子性质预测和JetClass喷注味（jet flavor）识别两个来自不同领域的基准数据集上，QUIVER提升了标准性能指标。实验从模拟变分电路中提取的量子几何特征（quantum-geometric features）即可产生可测量的性能增益，无需依赖容错量子硬件（fault-tolerant quantum hardware）。

Conclusion: QUIVER的核心贡献是领域无关的：量子Fisher视图能够通过架构层面的定向修改融入多种模型，为经典机器学习任务提供基于量子几何信息的互补模态。研究结果表明，即使在使用模拟量子电路的条件下，量子信息理论驱动的特征增强也能为当前经典机器学习带来切实收益。

Abstract: Large machine learning models benefit substantially from multimodal inputs that provide a complementary view of the same example. We introduce QUIVER (QUantum-Informed Views for Enhanced Representations, a paradigm that enriches classical data-driven features with a quantum Fisher view: a geometrically motivated, basis-independent summary of higher-order correlations captured by a variational quantum circuit (VQC) trained to perform the same task. Unlike classical feature augmentation, the quantum Fisher information matrix encodes the intrinsic geometry of the learned quantum state manifold. While this feature map, motivated by quantum information theory, is ordinarily non-trivial to model classically, it can surface statistical structure that additional classical data or model capacity finds difficult to learn. This makes the quantum Fisher view a genuinely complementary modality rather than a redundant one. We demonstrate that QUIVER improves standard performance metrics on two benchmark datasets from very different fields: QM9 for predicting molecule properties, and JetClass for predicting jet flavor at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC). The core contribution, however, is domain-agnostic: the quantum Fisher view can be fused into a broad class of model architectures via targeted modifications to the base architecture, to incorporate information about the quantum geometry of the problem. These results demonstrate that quantum-geometric features, extracted from simulated variational circuits, can deliver measurable value for standard machine learning tasks, well before the advent of fault-tolerant quantum hardware.

### [64] [Optoelectronics and Magnetic properties calculation of RE$_2$MnNiO$_6$ (RE=La-Lu,Y) using Density Functional Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02760)
*Debidutta Pradhan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过DFT+U框架对RE₂MnNiO₆（RE=La-Lu）有序双钙钛矿氧化物的电子结构、晶格动力学和光学性质进行了系统第一性原理研究，揭示了镧系收缩通过A位离子半径调控体系磁性基态和光电响应的统一机制，并明确了4f电子占据与八面体畸变的协同作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RE₂MnNiO₆体系中RE 4f电子的强局域性对密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）处理构成根本性挑战，但4f与相邻5d（RE）或3d（Ni, Mn）态的杂化是交换相互作用和光电响应的起源，因此亟需系统揭示该杂化如何影响体系的电子和磁性基态。

Method: 在DFT+U框架内对代表性RE₂NiMnO₆化合物进行第一性原理计算；通过将RE 4f电子分别处理为冻结芯态（frozen core states）和显式价态（valence manifold），直接评估Kondo型4f-d杂化对能带结构、介电函数和声子色散（phonon dispersion）的贡献。

Result: 自旋极化计算揭示了显著的自旋通道不对称性（spin-channel asymmetry），部分体系成员的单位分子式磁矩高达30 μB；计算结果表明4f占据数和八面体畸变共同决定了该双钙钛矿家族的磁性和光电势能。

Conclusion: 该系列体系形成一个统一的图像：镧系收缩通过A位离子半径系统地调控NiO₆和MnO₆八面体网络的电子和磁性基态，4f电子占据与八面体畸变的协同作用是理解其磁性和光电响应的关键。

Abstract: RE$_2$MnNiO$_6$ (RE = La-Lu) family of ordered double-perovskite oxides hosts a corner-sharing network of alternating NiO$_6$ and MnO$_6$ octahedra whose electronic and magnetic ground states are systematically governed by the A-site ionic radius through the lanthanide contraction. The strong localisation of RE 4f electrons poses a fundamental challenge to density-functional treatments, yet the hybridisation between 4f and neighbouring 5d (RE) or 3d (Ni, Mn) states is central to the origin of exchange interactions and optoelectronic response across the series. We present a comprehensive first-principles study of the electronic structure, lattice dynamics, and optical properties of representative RE2NiMnO6 compounds within the DFT+U framework. To disentangle the role of Kondo-type 4f-d hybridisation, calculations are performed with the RE 4f electrons treated both as frozen core states and explicitly in the valence manifold, enabling a direct assessment of their contribution to the band structure, dielectric function, and phonon dispersion. Spin-polarised calculations reveal significant spin-channel asymmetry, with magnetic moments reaching up to 30 $μ$B per formula unit for select members of the series. The results establish a unified picture of how 4f occupancy and octahedral distortion collectively determine the magnetic and optoelectronic potential of this double-perovskite family.

### [65] [Shift current conductivity in monolayer SnS: a tight-binding analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02851)
*Yuki Kusunoki,Tomoaki Kameda,Katsunori Wakabayashi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用第一性原理推导的有效紧束缚模型研究单层SnS中的体光伏效应（bulk photovoltaic effect），通过比较短程与长程跃迁模型，揭示了短程模型能捕捉移位电流（shift current）非线性响应的低能特征结构，而长程跃迁则定量修正峰位与幅值，并为理解和设计二维材料体光伏效应提供了清晰框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解并设计二维材料中的体光伏效应（bulk photovoltaic effect），特别是揭示不同跃迁过程（短程 vs 长程）对移位电流（shift current）非线性响应的贡献机制。

Method: 基于第一性原理（first-principles）计算推导出有效紧束缚模型（tight-binding model），通过对比短程（short-range）与长程（long-range）跃迁模型，将移位电流分解为跃迁强度（transition intensity）和移位矢量（shift vector），以识别主导的带间跃迁（interband transitions）。

Result: 短程模型保留了非线性响应（nonlinear response）的特征低能结构，而长程跃迁过程定量修正了移位电流的峰位和幅值。

Conclusion: 为理解和设计二维材料中的体光伏效应提供了透明的理论框架，表明最小模型可捕获移位电流导电性的核心特征。

Abstract: We investigate the bulk photovoltaic effect in monolayer SnS using an effective tight-binding model derived from first-principles calculations. By comparing short-range and long-range hopping models, we show that the essential features of the shift current conductivity are captured by a minimal model. The shift current is decomposed into transition intensity and shift vector, enabling identification of dominant interband transitions. The comparison reveals that long-range hopping processes quantitatively modify the peak positions and magnitudes, while the short-range model retains the characteristic low-energy structure of the nonlinear response. Our findings provide a transparent framework for understanding and designing bulk photovoltaic effects in two-dimensional materials.

### [66] [Multiferroicity in the two-dimensional limit in hexagonal LuFeO3 films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03053)
*Huilin Lai,Junyu Tan,Jinfeng Zhai,Yang Shi,Lili Feng,Huanyu Zhang,Chuanrui Huo,Chuhang Liu,Lijun Wu,Lifeng Yin,Hangwen Guo,Jun Chen,Xiaoshan Xu,Jun Zhao,Yimei Zhu,Shiqing Deng,Wenbin Wang,Jian Shen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究证明六方相LuFeO3 (h-LuFeO3) 在仅1.5个单胞厚度的二维极限下，仍能同时保留铁电性与磁性，并维持磁电耦合，成为首个展现真正二维极限多铁性（2D-limit multiferroicity）的氧化物体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多铁性氧化物（multiferroic oxides）是理解关联量子现象（correlated quantum phenomena）的核心材料。然而，当厚度逼近二维极限时，传统理论预期铁电性会因退极化场（depolarization fields）消失，磁性会因有限尺寸效应（finite-size effects）消失。因此，探索能否在原子尺度突破这一限制，成为关键科学问题。

Method: 研究选取六方相LuFeO3 (h-LuFeO3) 作为研究对象，将其减薄至仅一个半单胞（one and a half unit cells）的二维极限厚度，并测量其铁电极化、长程磁性（long-range magnetism）、磁电耦合（magnetoelectric coupling）以及K3声子模（K3 phonon mode）的行为。

Result: 在室温下，二维极限h-LuFeO3的铁电极化与体材料相当；在低温下，长程磁性和磁电耦合得以保持。此外，介导极化-磁性耦合的K3声子模在二维极限下保持稳定。

Conclusion: h-LuFeO3被确立为首个展现真正二维极限多铁性的氧化物体系，这是在原子尺度理解和控制耦合铁性序（coupled ferroic orders）的长期探索中取得的基础性突破。

Abstract: Multiferroic oxides, which combine coupled ferroelectric and magnetic orders, are central to understanding correlated quantum phenomena. Yet, as thickness approaches the two-dimensional (2D) limit, both ferroelectricity and magnetism are conventionally expected to vanish due to depolarization fields and finite-size effects, respectively. Here, we demonstrate that hexagonal LuFeO3 (h-LuFeO3) retains coupled ferroelectricity and magnetism at the 2D limit, with a thickness of just one and a half unit cells. Remarkably, the ferroelectric polarization remains comparable to bulk values at room temperature, while long-range magnetism and magnetoelectric coupling persist at low temperatures. We further show that the K3 phonon mode, which mediates the polarization-magnetism coupling, is stable down to the 2D limit. Our results establish h-LuFeO3 as the first oxide system to exhibit genuine 2D-limit multiferroicity, providing a fundamental breakthrough in the long-standing quest to understand and control coupled ferroic orders at the atomic scale.

### [67] [High-Throughput Discovery of Semimetallic Borophenes with Diverse Dirac States Via Transferable Tight-Binding Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03060)
*Yuke Song,Shifang Li,Tao Ouyang,Chao Tang,Jin Li,Chaoyu He*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过开发可转移的紧束缚框架（transferable tight-binding framework）并结合图论与群论的随机生成策略，对522个硼烯（borophene）同素异形体进行高通量筛选，发现了八种新型半金属硼烯，首次预测了其中的二次型节点半金属（quadratic nodal-point semimetals），并验证了其狄拉克态（Dirac states）由晶体对称性保护且具有动力学与热力学稳定性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了一个可转移的紧束缚框架（transferable tight-binding framework）用于平面硼烯，并结合基于图论（graph theory）和群论（group theory）的随机生成策略，对522个硼烯候选同素异形体进行了高通量筛选（high-throughput screening）。

Result: 识别出八种此前未报道的半金属硼烯，展现出多种拓扑能带交叉（topological band crossings），包括I型与III型狄拉克锥（type-I and type-III Dirac cones）、狄拉克节线（Dirac nodal lines）以及二次型节点（quadratic nodal points）。首次在硼烯中预测了二次型节点半金属（quadratic nodal-point semimetals）。对称性分析表明这些狄拉克态受晶体对称性保护，第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）证实了其动力学与热力学稳定性。

Conclusion: 这些发现确立了硼烯作为在二维体系中工程化涌现狄拉克物理（emergent Dirac physics）的一个多功能平台。

Abstract: Borophene has attracted extensive interest due to its structural flexibility and emergent topological electronic states. However, semimetallic borophenes hosting robust Dirac states remain rare among the large number of predicted allotropes. Here, we develop a transferable tight-binding framework for planar borophenes and combine it with a graph- and group-theory-based random generation strategy to perform high-throughput screening of 522 borophene candidates. Eight previously unreported semimetallic borophenes are identified, hosting diverse topological band crossings, including type-I and type-III Dirac cones, Dirac nodal lines, and quadratic nodal points. Notably, quadratic nodal-point semimetals are predicted in borophene for the first time. Symmetry analysis reveals crystalline-symmetry-protected Dirac states, while first-principles calculations confirm their dynamical and thermal stability. These findings establish borophene as a versatile platform for engineering emergent Dirac physics in two dimensions.

### [68] [Unconventional crystallization pathway bypassing the intermediate cubic phase in phase-change superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03309)
*Bai-Qian Wang,Nian-Ke Chen,Yao-Jie Wang,Jia Sun,Yu-Ting Huang,Ming Xu,Shengbai Zhang,Xian-Bin Li*

TL;DR: 本文通过机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potential）驱动的大规模分子动力学模拟，揭示了Ge-Sb-Te超晶格相变材料在部分非晶化后的再结晶机理：残余晶区可引导非晶区直接再结晶为具有反位缺陷和堆垛层错的有序但化学无序的超晶格相，该缺陷超晶格区更易熔化，可作为器件活性区，从而解决了超晶格相变存储器工作机制的长期争议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ge-Sb-Te (GST) 超晶格（superlattice）相变材料有望克服相变存储器（phase-change memory, PCM）的高功耗问题，但其工作机制尚存争议。特别是部分非晶化（partial amorphization）机制中，部分非晶化的GST如何再结晶为超晶格相而非常规预期的立方相（cubic phase）这一问题亟待澄清。

Method: 采用基于机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potential）的大规模分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，对部分熔化的GST超晶格体系进行再结晶过程的原子尺度计算研究。

Result: 残余晶区可作为晶核，引导非晶GST直接再结晶为超晶格相，而不经过中间立方相。所得再结晶相并非理想超晶格，而是具有反位缺陷（anti-site defects）和堆垛层错（stacking faults）的结构有序但化学无序的缺陷超晶格（defective superlattice）。该缺陷超晶格区比无缺陷超晶格更易熔化，因此可作为PCM器件的活性区（active region）。

Conclusion: 该研究澄清了超晶格相变存储器工作机制中长期存在的争议，为理解部分非晶化条件下的再结晶路径提供了原子尺度的直接证据。

Abstract: The Ge-Sb-Te (GST) superlattice phase-change material is a promising candidate for overcoming the high power-consumption of phase-change memory (PCM). However, the working mechanism of the superlattice PCM remains controversial. Partial amorphization, which is currently considered the most plausible mechanism, remains hotly debated: how does the partially amorphized GST recrystallize into its superlattice phase instead of the conventionally expected cubic phase? Here, we address this issue using large-scale molecular dynamics simulations enabled by a machine-learning interatomic potential. Starting from a partially melted GST superlattice, we demonstrate that the residual crystalline regions serve as nuclei, enabling the amorphous GST to recrystallize directly into the superlattice phase without passing through the intermediate cubic phase. Moreover, the recrystallized phase is not an ideal superlattice, but rather a structurally ordered and chemically disordered defective superlattice characterized by anti-site defects and stacking faults. The defective superlattice region is also more susceptible to melting than the defect-free superlattice, and thereby can act as the active region of the PCM device. These results help to clarify the longstanding debates concerning the mechanism of superlattice-based PCM.

### [69] [Role of Characteristic Length Scale in Interface Graphitization-Induced Wear Resistance of Diamond and Amorphous Carbon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03325)
*WenLiang Shi,YanYu Zhang,WenZheng Liao,Kai Xu,HongYu Wu,ZhiCheng Zhong,KeKe Chang*

Result: 金刚石界面形成横向连续的sp²重构层，特征长度为30–45 Å；非晶碳界面仅形成完全孤立的sp²斑块，尺寸为8–12 Å。该特征长度尺度差异决定了重构层外弱键合界面原子的密度，从而直接决定宏观磨损率。

Conclusion: 通过保护特定晶体学取向（如(111)密排面）可调控金刚石涂层的摩擦诱导石墨化。该工作桥接了原子尺度界面结构与宏观摩擦学性能之间的鸿沟，为耐磨碳基涂层的理性设计提供了机理指导。

Abstract: The evolution of interfacial atomic structures critically influences the friction and wear behavior of carbon-based materials. However, how the characteristic length scale of friction-induced sp\textsuperscript{2} reconstruction governs macroscopic wear remains poorly understood, particularly for diamond and amorphous carbon where the interfacial graphitization modes differ fundamentally. In this work, we develop a machine learning potential for these carbon systems and investigate the structural evolution at interfaces in both diamond/diamond and amorphous/amorphous carbon systems using molecular dynamics simulations. Our results reveal distinct atomic-scale characteristics of graphitization at the two interfaces. Diamond interfaces develop a laterally continuous sp\textsuperscript{2} reconstruction layer with a characteristic length of 30--45~Å, while amorphous carbon interfaces form only fully isolated sp\textsuperscript{2} patches of 8--12~Å. This disparity in characteristic length scale determines the density of weakly bonded interfacial atoms left outside the reconstruction layer, thereby directly dictating the macroscopic wear rate. Based on these insights, we propose a strategy to regulate friction-induced graphitization in diamond coatings by protecting specific crystallographic orientations, such as the (111) close-packed planes. This work bridges the gap between atomic-scale interfacial structure and macroscopic tribological performance, offering mechanistic guidelines for the rational design of wear-resistant carbon-based coatings.

### [70] [Quantum annealing for materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03405)
*Alfredo Fiorentino,Nicola Marzari*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在材料科学中，寻找势能面（potential energy surface）的全局最小值是一个基础性挑战，广泛应用于蛋白质折叠（protein folding）和团簇物理（cluster physics）等领域。随着（亚）稳态构型数量呈指数增长，传统方法面临巨大困难，亟需高效的全局优化策略。

Method: 基于路径积分分子动力学（path-integral molecular dynamics）实现量子退火（quantum annealing）协议。该方法利用量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）替代经典退火中的热涨落（thermal fluctuations），无需显式操控多体波函数（many-body wavefunctions），即可对量子核密度（quantum nuclear density）进行采样。

Result: 该量子退火协议在多种原子系统中表现出色，可通过经验力场（empirical force fields）或机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potentials）进行模拟。方法兼具分子动力学模拟的灵活性与量子退火的强性能。

Conclusion: 该方法可作为势能面的全局优化器（global optimizer），或作为考虑量子核效应的结构搜索策略——这一特性对高压氢化物（high-pressure hydrides）等材料尤为关键。

Abstract: Finding the global minimum of a potential energy surface is a fundamental challenge in materials science, with applications ranging from protein folding to cluster physics and, more broadly, to systems in which the number of (meta)stable configurations grows prohibitively large. In recent decades, quantum annealing (QA) has emerged as a promising global optimization strategy, exploiting quantum fluctuations in contrast to the thermal fluctuations that drive its classical counterpart.
  Here, we introduce a novel implementation of QA based on path-integral molecular dynamics, an efficient and well-established framework for sampling the quantum nuclear density without the need to manipulate many-body wavefunctions explicitly. While retaining the flexibility and simplicity of molecular dynamics simulations, this quantum-annealing protocol delivers strong performance across a wide range of atomic systems, simulated by either empirical force fields or machine-learning interatomic potentials. The method can be used either as a global optimizer of the potential-energy surface, or as a quantum-informed structure-search strategy in which nuclear quantum effects are included directly in the optimization workflow -- a feature particularly relevant for materials such as high-pressure hydrides.

### [72] [Molecular neutron spectroscopy techniques applied to ceramics $α$-SiC and $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03586)
*Adam J. Jackson,Svemir Rudić,Manh Duc Le,Sanghamitra Mukhopadhyay*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过两种具有工业电子应用背景的陶瓷材料（α-SiC 和 β-Ga₂O₃）作为“最坏情况”体系，实证检验了非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering）中一种类声子态密度（DOS-like）的半解析非相干近似模拟方法的有效性。研究发现，对于紧凑型仪器采集的一维粉末谱，该近似方法与实验谱易于比对，且结果与更耗时的相干谱数值采样方法相似，表明该方法适用于多数粉末样品的谐波声子非弹性中子散射模拟；而Q分辨仪器采集二维动态结构因子时仍需数值平均以捕捉声子特征。此外，PBEsol泛函与α-SiC实验吻合良好，RSCAN泛函则对β-Ga₂O₃最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固定几何结构的中子谱仪只能在有限角度范围内测量非弹性散射，生成一维谱S(ω)。此类测量通常采用基于声子态密度（density of states, DOS）的半解析非相干近似进行模拟，该方法在分子晶体弯曲/伸缩模研究中已成熟，但需检验其对于具有相干散射（coherent scattering）、依赖动量转移Q且频率处于分子谱典型“指纹”区以下的陶瓷材料的适用性。

Method: 对α-SiC和β-Ga₂O₃粉末样品进行两种不同对比型谱仪在低温和高温下的非弹性中子散射测量；采用多种密度泛函近似（DFA）进行模拟，包括PBEsol和RSCAN泛函；将一维近似模拟结果与实验谱及更耗时的相干谱数值采样方法进行对比。

Result: 对于紧凑型仪器的一维粉末谱，近似模拟与实验谱易于比对，且与相干谱数值采样给出相似结果。对于Q分辨仪器采集的二维动态结构因子S(Q,ω)，仍需数值平均。PBEsol泛函对α-SiC（6H多型）的模拟与实验良好吻合；RSCAN泛函对β-Ga₂O₃的模拟与实验吻合最佳。

Conclusion: 该近似方法适用于通过该技术对几乎任何粉末样品中谐波声子（harmonic phonon）的非弹性中子散射进行建模。未来对β-Ga₂O₃晶格动力学的研究推荐使用RSCAN泛函。

Abstract: Neutron spectroscopy is a powerful technique for determining the vibrational states of matter. Instruments with fixed geometry may measure inelastic scattering at a limited set of angles, producing a 1-D spectrum $S(ω)$. Such measurements are usually simulated in a DOS-like semi-analytic incoherent approximation, well-established for study of bending/stretching modes in molecular crystals. In this work we empirically test the simulation method for two ceramics with industrial electronic applications that act as "worst-case" systems. The phonon scattering from $α$-SiC and $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ is coherent, depends on momentum transfer $Q$ and sits in frequencies below the typical "fingerprint" range of molecular spectroscopy. Inelastic neutron-scattering measurements of powders were performed with two contrasting spectrometers at cryogenic and elevated temperatures, and simulations performed using a variety of density-functional approximations. We find that for 1-D powder spectra from a compact instrument, the approximate simulations are easily comparable with experimental spectra and give similar results to a more computationally-intensive numerical sampling of the coherent spectrum. Given the success with these systems, the approximate method appears to be suitable for modelling inelastic neutron scattering by harmonic phonons of almost any powder sample with this technique. When a $Q$-resolved instrument is used to collect the 2-D dynamical structure factor $S(Q,ω)$, numerical averaging is still required to capture phonon features. Our simulations of inelastic scattering from $α$-SiC in the 6H polytype using the PBEsol functional gave good agreement with the experiments. By contrast, the RSCAN functional gave the best agreement with the measured spectra of $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ and is recommended for future work on the lattice dynamics of this material.

### [73] [Demonstrating magnetic memory in iron-rhodium structures using a quantum diamond microscope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03738)
*Kristine V. Ung,Gregory M. Stephen,Nicholas A. Blumenschein,Alexander J. Edwards,Samuel W. LaGasse,Steven P. Bennett,Aubrey T. Hanbicki,Ronald L. Walsworth,Adam L. Friedman,Paul V. Petruzzi*

Abstract: Iron-rhodium (FeRh) has a first-order phase transition near room temperature between antiferromagnetic (AFM) and ferromagnetic (FM) phases, making it a promising material for magnetic memory technologies like heat-assisted magnetic recording (HAMR). It has a comparatively sharper phase transition and lower writing temperature than alternative materials, implying less thermal engineering constraints and an increase in write/read head lifetime. Despite great effort, however, AFM-based magnetic memory using FeRh has not yet been realized. Here, we employ both wide-field and scanning nanoscale quantum diamond microscopes (QDMs) to image directly the magnetic field of a patterned FeRh thin film structure under ambient conditions, demonstrating a magnetic recording technique that is reliable and robust. Thus, the magnetic orientation is maintained when the system is cycled between AFM and FM phases, providing the foundation for a practical, AFM-based magnetic memory.

### [74] [Quantitative Detection of Molecular Oxygen in the Gas Phase with Fluorescent Nanodiamonds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03844)
*Nicholas A. Nunn,Antonin Marek,Alex I. Smirnov,Olga A. Shenderova,Marco D. Torelli*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了利用荧光纳米金刚石中带负电的氮-空位（NV-）中心的光探测磁共振（ODMR）技术，定量检测气体混合物中的顺磁分子氧（O2）。研究发现ODMR对比度随氧分压线性降低，检测限约为8 mmHg，并展示了该量子传感器在酶催化反应产氧检测中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现对气体混合物中顺磁分子氧（paramagnetic molecular oxygen, O2）的定量检测，尤其是利用纳米金刚石中氮-空位（NV-）中心的光探测磁共振（ODMR）技术，以开发基于量子传感的高灵敏度氧检测方法。

Method: 将直径约70 nm的荧光纳米金刚石沉积在微流控通道的玻璃表面，通过混合O2和N2气体在环境压力下调节氧浓度为0–100%（对应氧分压0–760 mmHg）。采用双调制（锁相）检测方案，同时对光激发和微波驱动进行调制，测量连续波（CW）ODMR对比度。

Result: ODMR对比度随氧分压线性降低，灵敏度系数k = (-10.1 ± 0.3) × 10⁻⁴ % mmHg⁻¹；氧检测限约为8 mmHg（约1% O2）。在0–5% O2循环测试中观察到轻微迟滞，重复性为0.006（百分比ODMR对比度）。观测到荧光猝灭现象，响应时间从数分钟到数十分钟不等，表明气体分子在纳米金刚石表面的物理吸附（physisorption）主导了平衡动力学。

Conclusion: 基于纳米金刚石的氧量子传感器能够定量检测气体混合物中的分子氧，并成功演示了其在酶催化过氧化氢分解产生瞬时氧爆发检测中的应用。该传感器具有良好的灵敏度、线性响应和可重复性，但响应速度受限于气体物理吸附过程。

Abstract: The quantitative detection of paramagnetic molecular oxygen (O2) in gas mixtures using optically detected magnetic resonance (ODMR) from negatively charged nitrogen-vacancy (NV-) centers in fluorescent nanodiamonds is described. Fluorescent nanodiamonds approximately 70 nm in diameter were deposited on the glass surface of a microfluidic channel, and the oxygen concentration varied from 0 to 100% (0 to 760 mmHg O2 partial pressure) by mixing O2 and N2 gases at ambient pressure. Continuous-wave (CW) ODMR contrast was measured using a double-modulation (lock-in) detection scheme applied to both optical excitation and microwave drives. The ODMR contrast decreases linearly with oxygen partial pressure, with a sensitivity coefficient k of (-10.1 +/- 0.3) x 10^-4 % mmHg^-1. The oxygen detection limit of the experimental setup was estimated to be approximately 8 mmHg O2 partial pressure (corresponding to about 1% O2 in the gas mixture). Cycling of the content of O2 in the gas mixture in the range of 0-5% revealed slight hysteresis and corresponding repeatability of 0.006 in percent ODMR contrast. The observed fluorescence quenching and relatively slow response (ranging from several to tens of minutes) upon changes in oxygen concentration suggest that physisorption of gas molecules on the nanodiamond surfaces contributes to equilibration dynamics. The applicability of the nanodiamond-based oxygen quantum sensor was further demonstrated by detecting transient bursts of molecular oxygen generated by enzyme-catalyzed decomposition of hydrogen peroxide.

### [75] [Predicting core-level X-ray photoemission spectra of oxide surfaces from first principles -- a case study for SnO$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03853)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: XPS是研究氧化物表面化学性质的有力工具，但谱图解释困难，因为真实表面包含多种终止、重构、吸附物和缺陷，这些因素会产生可能重叠的光谱指纹。因此需要一种能从第一性原理出发、直接与实验对比的谱图预测方法。

Method: 基于Z+1方法（Z+1 method）的第一性原理计算，预测氧化物表面XPS谱图。具体计算SnO₂ (110)表面的O 1s芯电子结合能（O 1s core-electron binding energy），包括化学计量比表面、含不同类型空位（vacancy）的表面（其中一种是完全还原表面），以及吸附OH和O₂分子的完全还原表面，进而预测XPS谱。

Result: 完全还原表面（fully reduced surface）产生高度对称的峰形，与近期XPS测量一致；化学计量比表面（stoichiometric surface）在低结合能处出现额外特征峰，由表面桥接氧原子（bridging oxygen atom）引起；吸附OH和O₂的还原表面在高结合能处出现额外特征。预测谱与暴露于氧气后的还原表面实验结果吻合良好。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法具有普适性（general），可直接推广应用于其他表面，为氧化物表面XPS谱的理论预测与实验对比提供了可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: X-ray photoemission spectroscopy (XPS) is a powerful technique to gain insight into the chemical properties of oxide surfaces. However, the interpretation of XPS spectra is notoriously difficult as realistic surfaces contain different terminations, reconstructions, adsorbates and defects all of which leave (potentially overlapping) spectroscopic fingerprints. To address this challenge, we present a first-principles approach based on the Z+1 method that allows us to predict XPS spectra of oxide surfaces which can directly be compared to experimental measurements. We present results for different SnO$_2$ (110) surfaces: the stoichiometric surface, surfaces with different types of vacancies (one of which is the fully reduced surface) and also the fully reduced surface with adsorbed OH and O$_2$ molecules. For these systems, we calculate the O 1s core-electron binding energies of all oxygen atoms and then use this to predict the XPS spectrum. We find that the fully reduced surface gives rise to a highly symmetric peak shape in agreement with recent XPS measurements. In contrast, the spectrum of the stoichiometric surface exhibits an additional feature at low binding energies caused by the bridging oxygen atoms at the surface. For the reduced surface with OH and O$_2$ adsorbates, the spectrum exhibits additional features at higher binding energies. The predicted spectra are in good agreement with experimental results obtained for reduced surfaces that have been exposed to oxygen gas. The presented method is general and can be straightforwardly applied to other surfaces.

</details>


### [76] [Data-driven mapping of borophene growth pathways](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03886)
*Colin Bousige,Jean Furstoss,Julien Lam,Pierre Mignon*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本论文通过结合反应性机器学习原子间势（reactive machine-learned interatomic potential）、巨正则蒙特卡洛模拟（grand-canonical Monte Carlo simulations）和数据驱动的结构分类方法，追踪了硼烯（borophene）在Ag(111)和Ag(100)表面的形成过程，建立了温度-压力基底生长图谱，揭示了空位构型、相混合和种子结构如何控制多晶型选择，并给出了可操作的合成窗口。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用反应性机器学习原子间势（reactive machine-learned interatomic potential）结合巨正则蒙特卡洛模拟（grand-canonical Monte Carlo simulations）以及数据驱动的结构分类（data-driven structural classification），系统追踪硼烯从早期核到Ag(111)和Ag(100)基底上扩展层的形成全过程。

Result: 构建了温度-压力基底生长图谱（temperature-pressure substrate growth maps）；揭示了空位构型（vacancy motifs）、相混合（phase intermixing）和种子结构（seed structure）对多晶型选择（polymorph selection）的控制机制。模拟成功复现了关键实验趋势，包括$β_{12}$/$χ_3$相的普遍存在及其随温度变化的竞争关系，并发现了将亚稳核（metastable nuclei）连接到长程有序（long-range order）的动力学路径（kinetic pathways）。

Conclusion: 识别了抑制竞争构型并促进目标相的条件，提供了可操作的合成窗口（actionable synthesis windows）。这些结果建立了一个用于指导硼烯生长乃至更广泛地控制低维材料（low-dimensional materials）中多晶型的预测性框架（predictive framework），该框架的核心在于将原子尺度模拟与基于机器学习（machine learning）的相识别相结合。

Abstract: Deterministic synthesis of borophene remains challenging because many polymorphs compete during nucleation and growth. Here we combine a reactive machine-learned interatomic potential with grand-canonical Monte Carlo simulations and data-driven structural classification to track borophene formation from early nuclei to extended layers on Ag(111) and Ag(100). We build temperature-pressure substrate growth maps and resolve how vacancy motifs, phase intermixing and seed structure govern polymorph selection. The simulations reproduce key experimental trends, including the prevalence of $β_{12}$/$χ_3$ phases and their temperature-dependent competition, while revealing kinetic pathways that connect metastable nuclei to long-range order. We identify conditions that suppress competing motifs and promote targeted phases, providing actionable synthesis windows. These results establish a predictive framework for directing borophene growth and, more broadly, for controlling polymorphism in low-dimensional materials by coupling atomistic simulation with machine-learning-enabled phase recognition.

</details>


### [77] [Topological Weyl Phase of an Ideal Spin-Gapless Semiconductor KCrSe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03959)
*Subhajit Mandal,Bishal Das,Himanshu Sharma,Satoru Hayami,Aftab Alam*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 基于第一性原理计算，本文识别出半霍伊斯勒化合物KCrSe是一种理想的自旋无隙外尔半金属（spin-gapless Weyl semimetal），它同时具备自旋无隙半导体（SGS）行为和外尔半金属特性，仅含一对靠近费米面的外尔节点，展现出显著的异常输运响应，为拓扑自旋电子学器件提供了理想平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找能够同时展现拓扑电子态与自旋极化电子态的材料体系是当前凝聚态物理的重要目标，但兼具自旋无隙半导体（spin-gapless semiconducting, SGS）行为和外尔半金属（Weyl semimetallicity）特性的材料极为罕见。本文旨在通过理论计算发现并验证这类材料的存在。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）对半霍伊斯勒（half-Heusler）化合物KCrSe的电子结构进行系统研究，并利用输运计算分析其纵向电导率、赛贝克系数（Seebeck coefficients）以及反常霍尔电导率（anomalous Hall conductivity）和反常能斯特电导率（anomalous Nernst conductivity）等输运性质。

Result: KCrSe被确定为理想的自旋无隙外尔半金属；其纵向电导率对温度依赖性弱且赛贝克系数较小，证实了SGS性质。该材料仅含一对外尔节点（Weyl nodes）——外尔半金属中允许的最小数目，且节点紧邻费米能级（Fermi level, E_F），因而具有极其干净的体态和表面电子谱。反常霍尔电导率约为90.76 S cm⁻¹，反常能斯特电导率约为0.15 A m⁻¹ K⁻¹，且在更低能量处显著增强。

Conclusion: KCrSe结合了理想的外尔拓扑、全自旋极化的低能态以及有限的反常输运响应，因此是一种有前景的高效拓扑自旋电子学（topological spintronic）器件设计平台。

Abstract: The coexistence of topological and spin-polarized electronic states within a single material platform provides an attractive route toward emergent quantum phenomena and spintronic functionalities. However, materials simultaneously exhibiting spin-gapless semiconducting (SGS) behavior and Weyl semimetallicity remain exceedingly rare. Here, using first-principles calculations, we identify the half-Heusler compound KCrSe as an ideal spin-gapless Weyl semimetal. Transport calculations reveal a weak temperature dependence of the longitudinal conductivity and relatively small Seebeck coefficients, providing further evidence of its SGS nature. KCrSe hosts a single pair of Weyl nodes-the minimum number permitted in a Weyl semimetal-located in close proximity to the Fermi level (E$_\text{F}$), resulting in exceptionally clean bulk and surface electronic spectra. The nontrivial Berry curvature associated with these Weyl nodes gives rise to sizable anomalous transport responses, including an anomalous Hall conductivity of $σ_{xy}^{A}\sim 90.76~\mathrm{S\,cm^{-1}}$ and an anomalous Nernst conductivity of $α_{xy}^{A}\sim 0.15~\mathrm{A\,m^{-1}K^{-1}}$ at E$_\text{F}$, with substantially enhanced values at lower energies. The combination of an ideal Weyl topology, fully spin-polarized low-energy states, and finite anomalous transport establishes KCrSe as a promising platform for designing high-efficiency topological spintronic devices.

### [78] [On the Detection of Curl-Free Gauge Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02622)
*Armen Gulian,Will Benston,Vahan Nikoghosyan*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文证明，在非平衡过程中，集体量子系统可以对无旋规范场（curl-free gauge field）产生瞬态响应，无需在静态几何中包围磁通。利用超导凝聚态（superconducting condensates）作为实例，展示了宏观波函数的演化相位会产生超流和电压脉冲，其时间积分正比于矢势的开路线积分。这一机制可解释为规范轮廓（gauge contour）在时空中的动力学闭合，并通过规范不变性论证、含时Ginzburg-Landau理论建模和数值模拟支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为，在单连通（simply connected）系统中，无旋规范场不可探测，这形成了一种“拓扑盲区”（topological blindness）。本文旨在挑战这一结论的根本性，探索在非平衡条件下集体量子系统是否能够实现对无旋规范场的瞬态响应。

Method: 以超导凝聚态作为具体实例，通过含时Ginzburg-Landau理论（time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory）建模和数值模拟，分析宏观波函数相位演化产生的超流和电压脉冲。同时采用规范不变性论证（gauge-invariant arguments），将响应机制解释为规范轮廓在时空中的动力学闭合。

Result: 发现非平衡过程中，集体量子系统的演化相位可产生超流和电压脉冲，其时间积分正比于矢势（vector potential）的开路径线积分。与常规Aharonov-Bohm效应不同，该响应不受磁通量子的模限制，其幅度可能远超静态双连通几何对应的尺度。

Conclusion: 该结果建立了一个探测无旋规范场的一般原理，为在量子物质及其他系统中探测隐藏规范结构提供了新方法。

Abstract: In quantum theory, electromagnetic gauge fields enter directly into the phase evolution of the wavefunction and can even influence quantum systems in regions where the associated electric and magnetic fields vanish. The Aharonov-Bohm effect demonstrates that such gauge fields produce observable consequences when a coherent quantum system encloses magnetic flux along a doubly connected path. This has led to the widespread view that curl-free gauge fields are undetectable in simply connected systems, giving rise to a form of topological blindness. Here we show that this conclusion is not fundamental. During nonequilibrium processes, collective quantum systems can develop transient responses to curl-free gauge fields without enclosing magnetic flux in a static geometry. Using superconducting condensates as a concrete example, we demonstrate that the evolving phase of the macroscopic wavefunction generates supercurrents and voltage pulses whose time integral is proportional to the open-path line integral of the vector potential. In contrast to the conventional Aharonov-Bohm effect, the resulting response is not restricted modulo the flux quantum and may greatly exceed the scale associated with static doubly connected geometries. The mechanism can be interpreted as a dynamical closure of the gauge contour in spacetime and is supported by gauge-invariant arguments, time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory modeling, and numerical simulations. These results establish a general principle for detecting curl-free gauge fields and suggest new approaches for probing hidden gauge structures in quantum matter and beyond.

</details>


### [79] [Anharmonic lattice dynamics and superconductivity in strained bulk and surface niobium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02730)
*Mihir Ranjan Sahoo,Roman Lucrezi,Pedro Nunes Ferreira,Chia-Nien Tsai,Matthew Julian,Rohit P. Prasankumar,Mahmoud I. Hussein,Christoph Heil*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过第一性原理计算，系统分析了均匀应变与晶体表面取向对铌（Nb）的振动特性和超导性质的影响。研究揭示了应变软化声子谱、增强电子-声子耦合进而提升超导转变温度（Tc）的机制；对于低指数表面，采用机器学习势与随机自洽谐波近似（stochastic self-consistent harmonic approximation）处理非谐效应，发现Nb(001)表面具有最强的电子-声子耦合与最高的Tc（10.0 K）。同时，通过分析Eliashberg谱函数及其泛函导数，识别出对超导配对各向异性最有效的声子能量区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究均匀应变（homogeneous strain）与晶体表面取向（crystallographic surface orientation）这两种微观调控手段如何独立及协同地改变铌（Nb）的声子谱与超导转变温度，并揭示非谐晶格效应（anharmonic lattice effects）在低指数表面中的关键作用。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），结合密度泛函微扰理论（density-functional perturbation theory, DFPT）计算电子-声子耦合矩阵元；针对低指数表面，训练铌专属的机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potentials），并用于加速随机自洽谐波近似（stochastic self-consistent harmonic approximation, SSCHA）计算，从而获取非谐重整化声子模式，进而构建Eliashberg谱函数（Eliashberg spectral function）。

Result: 体相Nb在拉伸应变下声子谱显著软化，电子-声子耦合增强，Tc从平衡态的9.5 K升至约6%晶格膨胀时的14.5 K。对于无应变自由站立薄膜，Nb(001)表面的Tc最高（10.0 K），Nb(110)和Nb(111)表面配对强度依次降低。通过功能导数δTc/δα²F(ω)分析，识别出对超导配对最有效的声子能量范围。

Conclusion: 应变、表面终止（surface termination）以及非谐声子重整化（anharmonic phonon renormalization）为调控Nb的超导性提供了互补且相互关联的微观途径。

Abstract: Using first-principles calculations, we investigate how homogeneous strain and crystallographic surface orientation modify the vibrational and superconducting properties of niobium. For bulk Nb, tensile strain strongly softens the phonon spectrum and enhances the electron--phonon coupling, increasing the superconducting transition temperature from 9.5 K at equilibrium to 14.5 K at $\sim\!6\%$ lattice expansion. For the low-index Nb(001), Nb(110), and Nb(111) surfaces, harmonic phonon calculations exhibit imaginary modes, showing that anharmonic lattice effects are essential. To treat these effects efficiently, we train Nb-specific machine-learning interatomic potentials on bulk and slab first-principles configurations and use them to accelerate stochastic self-consistent harmonic approximation calculations, thereby obtaining anharmonically renormalized phonon modes that are combined with density-functional perturbation theory electron--phonon matrix elements to construct the Eliashberg spectral function. Among the clean free-standing slabs considered here, Nb(001) exhibits the strongest electron--phonon coupling and the highest calculated transition temperature of 10.0 K, while Nb(110) and Nb(111) show progressively reduced pairing strength. Finally, by analyzing the Eliashberg spectral function and the functional derivative $δT_\text{c}/δα^2F(ω)$, we identify the phonon energy ranges most effective for superconducting pairing. Our results show that strain, surface termination, and anharmonic phonon renormalization provide complementary and interrelated microscopic routes for tuning superconductivity in Nb.

</details>


### [80] [Enhanced superconductivity in atomically thin noble metals: From quantum confinement to interface-induced Lifshitz transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03663)
*Chun-Jie Zhang,Bing Zhang,Yapeng Wu,Xiao-Ping Li,Lei Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，建立了将本征量子限域效应与界面工程相结合的框架，揭示了在原本非超导的贵金属（Au、Ag、Cu）超薄薄膜中诱导超导电性的机制，并指出通过h-BN/Cu(111)异质结的界面堆叠构型调控可将超导转变温度提升至7.00 K。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在本质上非超导的贵金属（Au、Ag、Cu）中实现超导电性（superconductivity）是低维物理（low-dimensional physics）领域的基础性挑战。虽然原子级薄层中的量子限域（quantum confinement）已被发现可触发超导电性，但如何将此微弱效应放大至实验可及的温度仍是一个关键未解问题。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），建立了一个将本征限域效应与界面工程（interface engineering）相结合的统一理论框架，系统研究了贵金属薄膜的超导特性。

Result: 本征超导电性具有元素特异性：Ag因刚性声子谱（stiff phonon spectrum）被抑制，而三层Cu（TC ≈ 0.78 K）和五层Au（TC ≈ 0.63 K）分别由限域导致的态密度（density-of-states, DOS）增强和声子软化（phonon softening）驱动产生超导。在h-BN/Cu(111)异质结构中，TC由界面堆叠构型决定：热力学稳定的N键合界面可实现TC ≈ 3.23 K，而亚稳态的B键合构型通过引发Lifshitz相变（Lifshitz transition）——费米面在M点与布里渊区边界形成切线接触——将电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）增强至超越DOS效应，使TC提升至7.00 K。

Conclusion: 该工作统一了对本征二维超导电性（two-dimensional superconductivity）的理解，并将其与原子尺度的界面设计相结合，为将贵金属功能化为新兴超导体提供了蓝图。

Abstract: Unlocking superconductivity in intrinsically non-superconducting noble metals (Au, Ag, Cu) represents a fundamental challenge in low-dimensional physics. While quantum confinement in the atomically thin limit is known to trigger emergent superconductivity, strategies to amplify this marginal effect to experimentally accessible temperatures remain a key open question. Using first-principles calculations, we establish a unified framework linking intrinsic confinement effects with interface engineering in noble metal films. We reveal that intrinsic superconductivity is element-specific: it is suppressed in Ag by a stiff phonon spectrum, but emerges in trilayer Cu ($T_{\rm C} \approx 0.78$ K) and pentalayer Au ($0.63$ K) driven by confinement-induced density-of-states (DOS) enhancement and phonon softening, respectively. In h-BN/Cu(111) heterostructures, $T_{\rm C}$ is critically dictated by the interfacial stacking configuration. We identify the thermodynamically stable N-bonded interface as a reliable platform for accessible superconductivity ($T_{\rm C} \approx 3.23$ K), whereas manipulating the system into a metastable B-bonded configuration boosts $T_{\rm C}$ to $7.00$ K. This enhancement originates from a B-bonded-induced Lifshitz transition, where the Fermi surface forms a tangential contact with the Brillouin zone boundary at the M point, enhancing electron-phonon coupling beyond DOS effects. Our work unifies the understanding of intrinsic two-dimensional superconductivity with atomistic interface design, offering a blueprint for functionalizing noble metals as emergent superconductors.

</details>


### [81] [Bipolar-doped superconducting infinite-layer cuprates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03981)
*Fengzhe Wang,Yueying Li,Heng Wang,Lizhi Xu,Xianfeng Wu,Lixiang Xu,Guangdi Zhou,Jin-Feng Jia,Peng Li,Haoliang Huang,Qi-Kun Xue,Zhuoyu Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究在无限层铜氧化物（infinite-layer cuprates）单晶薄膜中实现了双极性掺杂（bipolar doping），绘制了电子相图（electronic phase diagram），并发现电子和空穴掺杂区均存在显著的电阻各向异性（resistance anisotropy）以及反铁磁能带折叠（antiferromagnetic band folding）与超导共存的现象。在空穴掺杂约0.07时，反铁磁折叠源于费米弧（Fermi arcs），超导转变温度超过60 K，重新定义了磁序与超导之间的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从电荷库层（charge-reservoir layers）的复杂性中提取超导CuO2平面的内在物理机制，是高温超导（high-temperature superconductivity）领域的关键挑战。尽管电子掺杂无限层铜氧化物已被合成，但可控且均匀的空穴掺杂长期难以实现，限制了能谱学研究的深入。

Method: 本研究在(Sr,Eu)CuO2和(Ca,Li)CuO2+δ单晶薄膜中实现了双极性掺杂（bipolar doping），通过电阻测量和角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）分别表征电子相图和电子结构。

Result: 电子和空穴掺杂薄膜均显示出显著的电阻各向异性，表明CuO2面具有准二维（quasi-two-dimensional）特性。ARPES测量在电子和空穴掺杂区域均观察到反铁磁能带折叠与超导共存。在空穴掺杂约0.07（由Luttinger体积（Luttinger volume）确定）时，反铁磁折叠从单一费米面（Fermi surface）内的费米弧中出现，超导转变温度超过60 K。

Conclusion: 这些发现重新定义了磁序（magnetic order）与超导（superconductivity）之间的相互作用，并建立了一个确凿的研究平台，用于探索高温超导铜氧化物（high-temperature superconducting cuprates）的内在机制。

Abstract: Distilling the intrinsic physics of the superconducting CuO2 plane from the complexities of charge-reservoir layers is a defining challenge in high-temperature superconductivity. While superconducting electron-doped infinite-layer cuprates have been synthesized, controllable and uniform hole doping has long remained elusive despite exploratory attempts, limiting spectroscopic insights. Here, we realize bipolar doping across infinite-layer (Sr,Eu)CuO2 and (Ca,Li)CuO2+δ single-crystalline thin films, mapping the electronic phase diagram. Both electron- and hole-doped films show pronounced electrical resistance anisotropy, indicating the quasi-two-dimensional nature of the CuO2 planes. Angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy across electron- and hole-doped regimes reveals persistent antiferromagnetic band folding coexisting with superconductivity. Remarkably, at a hole doping ~0.07 determined by Luttinger volume, the antiferromagnetic folding emerges from Fermi arcs within the film's single Fermi surface, with the onset superconducting transition temperature exceeding 60 K. These findings redefine the interplay between magnetic order and superconductivity and establish a definitive platform to investigate the intrinsic mechanism of high-temperature superconducting cuprates.

</details>

### [82] [Spatially Uniform and Defect-Tolerant Plasmonic Responses in 3D printed Gold Nanoparticle Assemblies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03285)
*Vasanthan Devaraj,Sunghyun Kwak,Hyeongjip Kim,Sang-Keun Sung,Jong-Min Lee,Thomas Zentgraf,Won-Geun Kim*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了大面积三维金纳米粒子（AuNP）组装体的光学性质，揭示了其散射光谱的鲁棒性源于有限等离激元退域长度（plasmon delocalization length）内的系综平均响应，并通过核-卫星（core-satellite）结构实现了组分依赖的光谱调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维金纳米粒子（gold nanoparticle, AuNP）组装体因结构无序和制备变异性导致光学行为复杂，缺乏对其光学可重复性和空间均匀性的系统理解。本文旨在通过可控的大规模组装方法，探究其光学响应的鲁棒性来源及组分调控机制。

Method: 采用弯月面引导组装（meniscus-guided assembly）制备大面积三维AuNP柱状结构，结合空间分辨暗场散射测量（dark-field scattering）表征光谱均匀性，并利用电磁模拟分析近场（near-field）与表面电荷分布（surface charge distribution）。进一步引入更小AuNP构建核-卫星（core-satellite）结构实现组分调制，通过波长依赖的表面增强拉曼散射（surface-enhanced Raman scattering, SERS）测量评估耦合路径变化。

Result: 高纵横比的AuNP柱体沿高度及不同柱体间展现均匀的散射光谱；电磁模拟表明鲁棒性源于有限等离激元退域长度（plasmon delocalization length）内的系综平均响应。核-卫星结构引入组分依赖的光谱重分布，产生长波长特征；633 nm与785 nm激发下的SERS响应差异反映了局域等离激元耦合路径（local plasmonic coupling pathways）的重分布。

Conclusion: 研究建立了具有系综平均与组分可调光学响应的鲁棒三维等离激元纳米粒子组装体的设计原则（design principles）。

Abstract: Three-dimensional (3D) assemblies of gold nanoparticles (AuNPs) offer a rich platform for plasmonic coupling and near-field engineering, yet their optical behavior is often complex due to structural disorder and fabrication-induced variability. Here, we present a systematic optical investigation of large-scale 3D AuNP assemblies fabricated via meniscus-guided assembly, focusing on the reproducibility and spatial uniformity. Spatially-resolved dark-field scattering measurements reveal that high-aspect-ratio AuNP pillars exhibit uniform scattering spectra along their height and across different pillars, despite variations in geometry and structure. Electromagnetic simulations suggest that this robustness arises from an ensemble-averaged plasmonic response governed by many local coupling regions within a finite plasmon delocalization length. Simulated near-field and surface charge distributions suggest that the broad ensemble response remains spatially distributed under representative structural perturbations, consistent with volumetric averaging. Building on this robust platform, we introduce compositional modulation through a core-satellite architecture by incorporating smaller AuNPs. This yields a composition-dependent spectral redistribution, including an additional long-wavelength spectral feature in the core-satellite assemblies. Wavelength-dependent surface-enhanced Raman scattering measurements reveal contrasting responses under 633 and 785 nm excitation, reflecting redistribution of local plasmonic coupling pathways. These results establish design principles for robust 3D plasmonic nanoparticle assemblies with ensemble-averaged and composition-tunable optical responses.

</details>

### [83] [Demonstration of a Spherical Penning Trap for Single Electrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03639)
*Zirui Fang,Xing Fan*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本文展示了一种球形潘宁阱（spherical Penning trap）中单电子囚禁的实验成果，并对其微波共振结构进行了表征，介绍了该几何结构的设计、单电子检测、微波模式特性及其优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 球形潘宁阱具有分离良好且清晰的微波共振模式，这使得它在电子磁矩（electron magnetic moment）精密测量以及利用囚禁电子进行暗光子（dark-photon）和轴子（axion）搜索等领域具有吸引力，因此需要对该阱型的单电子囚禁与微波特性进行实验验证。

Method: 实验上实现了球形潘宁阱中的单电子囚禁（single-electron trapping），并对其微波共振（microwave resonance）结构进行了表征，涉及阱体设计、信号检测与微波模式分析。

Result: 成功演示了单电子在球形潘宁阱中的囚禁，并明确表征了其微波共振结构。

Conclusion: 球形潘宁阱的设计与微波特性为电子磁矩精密测量及暗物质（暗光子、轴子）搜索提供了具有优势的技术方案。

Abstract: A spherical Penning trap has well-separated, clean microwave resonances, making it attractive for precision measurements of the electron magnetic moment and for dark-photon and axion searches with trapped electrons. We demonstrate single-electron trapping in a spherical Penning trap and characterize its microwave resonance structure. The design, single-electron detection, microwave mode characterization, and advantages of this geometry are presented.

</details>
