### [84] [Spacetime triple wormhole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02611)
*Vincent Herr,Aimé Fournier,Andrew J. S Hamilton*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文通过球面反演三环面（3-torus）构造了一个具有三重颈（3-neck）的时空虫洞（spacetime wormhole），并证明该度规张量（metric tensor）是爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein's field equations）的精确解，从而肯定了爱因斯坦和罗森（1935）关于多颈解存在性的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 回答爱因斯坦与罗森（1935）提出的问题：是否存在多颈（multi-neck）的虫洞解。此前未有此类解析解的明确构造。

Method: 对等半径三环面进行球面反演（spherical inversion），得到Dupin超环曲面（Dupin hypercyclide）；将其置于同步参考系（synchronous reference frame）中，并断言该度规张量为爱因斯坦场方程在全局坐标下的精确解。

Result: 所得度规生成了对角的Ricci张量与应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor），Riemann曲率张量（Riemann curvature tensor）仅有六个非零分量；类空流形为无界、渐近平坦（asymptotically flat）的三变量Dupin超环曲面；该非真空解包含负能量密度，但每个颈部的测地路径仅遇到正能量密度。

Conclusion: 成功构造了首个宇内、非薄壳、非球对称的三颈时空虫洞精确解，证实多颈虫洞解的存在性，并为后续虫洞几何的全局坐标研究提供了简化框架。

Abstract: We describe a multi-neck spacetime wormhole with a simple metric tensor and a simple injective map without coordinate patching. An intra-universe, non-thin-shell, non-spherically-symmetric 3-neck spacetime wormhole is geometrically constructed by spherically inverting a 3-torus. We place the resulting Dupin hypercyclide in a synchronous reference frame. The three necks are arranged around a central point and satisfy topological and geometric spacetime wormhole definitions. Asserting this metric tensor as an exact solution of Einstein's field equations in global coordinates generates diagonal Ricci and stress-energy tensors, and a Riemann curvature tensor with only six nonzero entries. The local inertial frame at every point of the coordinate system is comoving with the triple wormhole. This non-vacuum solution answers affirmatively the question posed by Einstein and Rosen (1935) of whether or not multi-neck solutions exist. The wormhole solution contains negative energy density as is expected to hold the necks open; however, geodesic paths through each neck exist which encounter only positive energy density. The spatial manifold is a trivariate Dupin hypercyclide. The spherically inverted equal-radii 3-torus is unbounded, asymptotically flat and admits a global isothermal coordinate system that further simplifies the curvature tensors.

</details>


### [85] [MCMC Constraints on Dyonic Kalb-Ramond Black Holes with a Cloud of Strings from Twin-Peak QPOs and EHT Shadows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02654)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Ahmad Al-Badawi,İzzet Sakallı*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个在洛伦兹破缺引力（Lorentz-violating gravity）中由背景卡尔布-拉蒙德场（Kalb–Ramond field）和宇宙弦云（cloud of strings）贯穿的双荷黑洞（dyonic black hole）。研究分析了其测地线运动、准周期振荡频率、热力学性质、霍金辐射稀疏性以及阴影半径，并通过MCMC拟合对观测数据（XTE J1550−564等）施加了约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索洛伦兹破缺引力中由卡尔布-拉蒙德场和宇宙弦云共同作用的双荷黑洞的动力学、热力学和辐射可观测特征，并利用实际天体物理观测数据对模型参数进行约束。

Method: 通过求解度规推导时间型圆轨道测地线（timelike circular geodesics），利用相对论进动模型（relativistic-precession model）和 epicyclic共振模型提取准周期振荡频率；采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法将理论频率映射到三颗微类星体的观测双峰信号上进行参数约束；基于热力学第一定律和斯马尔关系（Smarr relation）建立完整热力学词典，分析热容、自由能和霍金辐射稀疏性。

Result: 洛伦兹破缺耦合参数 ℓ、磁荷 p 和宇宙弦密度 ξ 均在动力学、热力学和辐射可观测量的特征上留下了可分辨的印记；其中 ξ 对最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）、阴影尺寸和霍金辐射稀疏性的影响最为显著。

Conclusion: 宇宙弦密度 ξ 是调控黑洞可观测特征的最强参数，洛伦兹破缺耦合和磁荷也产生可区分的效应，本模型有望通过多信使观测进行进一步检验。

Abstract: We study a dyonic black hole in a Lorentz-violating gravity that carries a background Kalb--Ramond field and is pierced by a cloud of strings. The resulting metric reduces to the recent Lin--Liu--Liu solution when the string density~$ξ$ is switched off, and to the Duan and Yang solutions in further degenerate limits. We work out the timelike circular geodesics and read off the quasi-periodic oscillation (QPO) frequencies $ν_φ$, $ν_r$ and $ν_θ$ within both the relativistic-precession and epicyclic-resonance models. We then map these frequencies onto the observed twin-peak signals of XTE~J1550$-$564, GRO~J1655$-$40 and GRS~1915$+$105, and place constraints on $(\ell, ξ)$ from a Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) fit. We extract the full thermodynamic dictionary, first law and Smarr relation included, and follow the heat capacity, free energy and sparsity of Hawking radiation through their dependence on the four parameters $(M, Q, p, \ell, ξ)$. Finally, we compute the spectral energy emission rate and look at the photon-sphere and shadow radii in the presence of the cosmic string. The Lorentz-violating coupling $\ell$, the magnetic charge $p$, and the string density $ξ$ all leave distinct fingerprints on the dynamical, thermodynamic and radiative observables, with $ξ$ exerting the strongest pull on the ISCO, the shadow size and the sparsity of Hawking emission

</details>


### [86] [Testing Exponential $f(R)$ Gravity with CMB, DESI-DR2, and Supernova Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02666)
*Saurabh Verma,Archana Dixit,Anirudh Pradhan,M. S. Barak*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过联合多个天文观测数据集（PPS、BBN、CC、DESI-DR2、CMB），对指数型f(R)引力模型进行了统计分析。结果表明该模型未能显著缓解H0 tension，但能在约1.2σ水平上部分缓解S8 tension，并在大尺度结构形成描述上提供一致改善。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了解释宇宙晚期加速膨胀现象，修改广义相对论（general relativity, GR）的模型（如f(R)引力）成为ΛCDM范式的主要竞争者之一。本文旨在检验指数型f(R)引力模型在宇宙膨胀与结构形成中的表现，并评估其对当前宇宙学张力（cosmological tensions）的缓解能力。

Method: 本研究考虑一个指数型f(R)引力模型作为广义相对论的可能扩展，持续纳入额外标量自由度（scalar degrees of freedom）及其对宇宙膨胀和结构形成的影响。通过联合PPS、BBN、CC、DESI-DR2和CMB数据集，对模型自由参数b及标准宇宙学参数施加限制，并进行详细的统计分析。

Result: 分析得到的哈勃常数H0值略低于ΛCDM模型的结果，表明对H0 tension没有显著缓解。相反，模型预测的S8值系统性偏高，在加入晚期宇宙数据集时，可在约1.2σ水平上适度缓解S8 tension。

Conclusion: 尽管所考虑的指数型f(R)引力模型无法同时解决所有的宇宙学张力，但它在大尺度结构形成的描述上提供了一致的改善，表明该模型在部分宇宙学问题上具有潜在优势。

Abstract: One of the most popular competitors to the CDM paradigm as an explanation for the late-time acceleration of the universe is the modification of general relativity (GR), with models such as $f(R)$ gravity among the main motivations. In this study, we consider an exponential $f(R)$ gravity model as a possible extensions of the GR. The extra scalar degrees of freedom and their effects on the cosmic expansion and structure formation are continuously considered in this scenario. By combining the PPS, BBN, CC, DESI-DR2, and CMB datasets, we imposed limitations on this model. We performed a detailed statistical analysis of the free model parameter $b$ together with the standard cosmological parameters. Our analysis yields values of $H_0$ that are slightly lower than those obtained in $Λ$CDM, indicating no significant relaxation of the $H_0$ tension. In contrast, the model predicts systematically higher values of $S_8$, leading to a moderate alleviation of the $S_8$ tension by up to $\sim 1.2σ$ when late-time datasets are included. Overall, these results demonstrate that although the considered $f(R)$ gravity model does not resolve all cosmological tensions simultaneously, it provides a consistent improvement in the description of large-scale structure formation.

</details>


### [87] [Quark Stars in Ricci-Determinant Gravity with an Interacting Quark Equation of State](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02681)
*Loreany F. Araújo,Krishna Pada Das*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Ricci-Determinant引力框架下，采用相互作用夸克状态方程研究静态球对称夸克星的基本性质，发现该模型导致夸克星緻密度降低、引力结合能的普适性被打破，并揭示了微扰项贡献超过广义相对论约一半时引发的不稳定条件限制了高中心密度天体的形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Ricci-Determinant引力这一扩展引力理论中自由参数对夸克星关键物理特性（尤其是质量-半径关系和稳定性判据）的影响，以揭示该理论与广义相对论（General Relativity, GR）的偏离。

Method: 采用文献中已导出的致密天体相对论性恒星结构方程（relativistic stellar structure equations），并结合相互作用的夸克状态方程（equation of state, EoS），在Ricci-Determinant引力框架下对静态球对称夸克星进行建模与分析。

Result: 与强子星情形不同，该模型预测夸克星的緻密度（compactness）降低；引力结合能（gravitational binding energy）分析表明该参数对模型敏感，所假设的普适性被打破；当微扰项的贡献超过普通GR贡献约一半时，不稳定性条件出现，从而限制了高中心密度天体的形成。

Conclusion: Ricci-Determinant引力对夸克星的结构和稳定性施加了明确的理论限制，表明该扩展引力理论在描述高密度夸克物质时存在可行的约束边界。

Abstract: In the present study, we explore the fundamental properties of static, spherically symmetric quark stars composed of quark matter with an interacting quark equation of state (EoS) within the framework of Ricci-Determinant gravity. To this end, we adopt the relativistic stellar structure equations for compact objects derived in the literature. Our primary objective is to investigate deviations from General Relativity (GR) in key physical characteristics, particularly the mass--radius relation and stability criteria, arising from the free parameters of this extended gravitational theory. We see that, unlike the hadronic case, the model predicts a reduction in the compactness of quark stars. This parameter is also sensitive to gravitational binding-energy analysis, revealing a breakdown of the assumed universality. Furthermore, the formation of objects with high central densities is restricted by the instability conditions that arise when the contribution of perturbative terms exceeds by approximately half the contribution of ordinary GR, indicating a clear limitation in the theory.

</details>


### [88] [Speed and accuracy for long signals: Frequency-domain effective-one-body waveforms for compact binary coalescences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02690)
*Marcus Haberland,Alessandra Buonanno*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种频域混合方法，将稳相近似（SPA）与快速傅里叶变换（FFT）相结合，在有效单体（effective-one-body, EOB）框架下高效且精确地实现面向双中子星（BNS）系统的SEOBNRv5THM波形模型，显著降低计算成本，使BNS信号参数估计可在数天内完成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对于来自双中子星（binary neutron-star, BNS）系统的长信号，引力波推断需要既物理可靠又计算高效的波形模型；否则，对核物质的观测推断可能产生错误结论。

Method: 采用混合频域方法：对早期旋进阶段使用稳相近似（stationary-phase approximation, SPA），对晚期旋进及旋进后阶段逐模式应用快速傅里叶变换（fast Fourier transform, FFT）。该方法保留SPA的计算效率，同时不损害靠近并合阶段（物质效应最显著）的波形精度。进一步可利用多频带（multibanding）与相对分箱（relative binning）等现代参数估计技术加速波形生成。

Result: 与基准SEOBNRv5THM模型在失配度（mismatches）以及真实与合成数据分析中均表现出高度一致性；表明波形系统误差（systematics）可能影响未来观测运行及新地面设施对BNS事件的探测。该方法显著降低计算成本，使BNS信号在数天量级的实际运行时间内即可完成可靠的参数估计。

Conclusion: 该混合频域方法可有效解决BNS长信号引力波推断中的效率与精度矛盾，并可扩展至并合双黑洞（binary black hole）系统。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave inference for long signals, like those from binary neutron-star (BNS) systems, requires waveform models that are both physically faithful and computationally efficient, otherwise, one risks drawing incorrect conclusions about nuclear matter from observations. To address this challenge, we present a frequency-domain implementation of the accurate SEOBNRv5THM waveform model for quasi-circular, spin-aligned BNS systems within the effective-one-body framework. Our approach combines the stationary-phase approximation (SPA) for the early inspiral with a fast Fourier transform treatment of the late- and post-inspiral regime, applied mode-by-mode. Our hybrid approach retains the efficiency of the SPA without affecting the waveform accuracy close to merger, where matter effects are most significant. The resulting waveform's generation speed can be further decreased using modern parameter-estimation techniques, such as multibanding and relative binning. We demonstrate excellent agreement with the baseline SEOBNRv5THM model in both mismatches and when analyzing real and synthetic data, and show how waveform systematics could affect BNS detections in upcoming observational runs and new facilities on the ground. We find that our method significantly reduces computational costs, enabling faithful parameter estimation for BNS signals within practical runtimes of order days. Our procedure can be readily extended to coalescing binary black hole systems.

</details>


### [89] [Asymptotically-FLRW$_3$ spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02722)
*Andrea Campoleoni,Arnaud Delfante,Marc Geiller,Nicolas Maindiaux*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在三维渐近FLRW时空背景下，引入并研究了一类由物质状态方程参数k控制的渐近对称群BMS₃ᵏ，详细分析了标量场物质源情形下的解空间和边界荷，识别了协变的新闻、质量和角动量方面，并在三维引力中首次给出了精确守恒的非线性Newman-Penrose荷的例子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究宇宙学背景下的渐近对称性和辐射需要一个简化的理论设置，而三维渐近FLRW时空为此提供了可控的简化模型，以便深入理解与四维情形相似的渐近对称结构。

Method: 采用三维渐近FLRW时空作为简化框架，引入BMS₃ᵏ渐近对称群（BMS₃的由物质状态方程参数k控制的单参数形变），对标量场物质源进行详细分析，通过研究真空解的有限BMS₃ᵏ变换轨道来定义协变的新闻、质量和角动量方面，并应用Wald-Zoupas方案处理荷。

Result: 完整表征了标量场物质源下的解空间与边界荷；指出对Bondi质量和角动量方面的正确识别需要进行此前尚未明确阐述的细致分析；识别了协变的新闻、质量和角动量方面；这些协变量自然地出现在与Weyl标量三维对应的Cotton标量中；在三维引力中首次给出了精确守恒的非线性Newman-Penrose荷的实例。

Conclusion: 三维渐近FLRW时空为研究宇宙学渐近对称性和辐射提供了有效的简化模型，展示了与四维情形（包括“广义BMS”对称性）相似的微妙结构，并成功构造了协变的守恒量。

Abstract: We introduce three-dimensional asymptotically-FLRW spacetimes as a simplified setting in which to study asymptotic symmetries and radiation in cosmology. Their asymptotic symmetry group is $\text{BMS}_3^k$, a one-parameter deformation of $\text{BMS}_3$ controlled by the matter equation of state with parameter $k$, in line with the four-dimensional construction of Bonga and Prabhu. We analyze in detail the case of a scalar field matter source, which allows us to fully characterize the solution space and the boundary charges. In particular, we point out that the proper identification of the Bondi mass and angular momentum aspects in the metric requires a careful analysis which had not been laid out so far, even in the existing four-dimensional literature. When superrotations are present, the model exhibits subtleties similar to those appearing when dealing with ''generalized BMS'' asymptotic symmetries in the four-dimensional case, and this requires a covariant definition of the news. We identify covariant notions of news, as well as of mass and angular momentum aspects by studying the vacuum structure, namely the orbits of the vacuum solution under finite $\text{BMS}_3^k$ transformations, and study the Wald-Zoupas prescription for the charges. We also show that these covariant aspects naturally appear in the Cotton scalars, which are the three-dimensional analogues of the Weyl scalars. Finally, we use these quantities to provide a first example of exactly conserved non-linear Newman-Penrose charges in three-dimensional gravity.

</details>


### [90] [Kerr--Schild--AdS geometries in quadratic f(R) gravity: A no-go theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02929)
*Alikram N. Aliev*

Main category: gr-qc

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 对于Kerr–Schild–AdS几何，二次f(R)引力中的黑洞解被限制在爱因斯坦分支内，确立了该几何类下的一个无存在性定理。

### [91] [Off-shell Hessian thermodynamic stability of higher-curvature black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03045)
*Chen-Hao Hao,Jieci Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于离壳吉布斯自由能（off-shell Gibbs free energy）和沃尔德熵（Wald entropy）的分支敏感热力学框架（branch-sensitive thermodynamic framework），用于分析高曲率黑洞（higher-curvature black holes）。研究发现，在一般情况下，黑洞的局部稳定性由黑塞矩阵（Hessian）$H=S'_W(r_h)T'(r_h)$ 而非单纯的温度斜率判定；该框架导出了平均场临界指数，并解释了光滑可观测量继承相同标度律的机制；同时揭示了温度斜率判据在物理上允许的黑洞分支上成立的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高曲率引力中的黑洞热力学往往偏离传统的温度斜率稳定性判据，现有框架缺乏统一且分支敏感的准则，亟需建立一种能够涵盖一般高阶曲率黑洞的通用热力学形式。

Method: 以离壳吉布斯自由能 $G_{\rm off}$ 和沃尔德熵 $S_W$ 为基础数据，在固定参数切片上将平衡态黑洞视作 $G_{\rm off}$ 的驻点，其局部稳定性由黑塞矩阵 $H=S'_W(r_h)T'(r_h)$ 决定；并在临界点附近建立了局部 $A_3$ 尖点正规型（$A_3$ cusp normal form）。

Result: 在准拓扑引力（quasi-topological gravity）的五维带电规则反德西特黑洞中，物理分支上 $S_W$ 单调，温度斜率判据被恢复为特例；临界行为给出平均场分支分离指数 $1/2$，且非退化光滑可观测量（如李雅普诺夫指数）继承相同标度。在洛甫洛克黑洞（Lovelock black holes）的非平面分支上 $S'_W$ 可变号，从而反转温度斜率的稳定性指派；但在无鬼且分支正则（ghost-free and branch-regular）的洛甫洛克外部解中 $S'_W$ 保持正定。

Conclusion: 离壳黑塞准则是温度斜率稳定性判据的严格推广；温度斜率规则仅在物理上允许的黑洞分支（即 $S'_W>0$ 的情形）上被保护，从而为高曲率黑洞热力学的分支选择提供了统一的诊断工具。

Abstract: We develop a branch-sensitive thermodynamic framework for higher-curvature black holes using the off-shell Gibbs free energy $G_{\rm off}$ and the Wald entropy$S_W$ as the basic data. On fixed-parameter slices, equilibrium black holes are stationary points of $G_{\rm off}$, and their local stability is governed by the Hessian $H=S'_W(r_h)T'(r_h)$, rather than by the temperature slope alone. For the five-dimensional charged regular AdS black hole in quasi-topological gravity, $S_W$ remains monotonic on the physical branch, so the usual temperature-slope rule is recovered only as a special consequence. The same off-shell structure also gives the local $A_3$ cusp normal form near criticality, yielding the mean-field $1/2$ branch separation exponent and explaining why smooth nondegenerate observables, such as the Lyapunov exponent, inherit the same scaling. In Lovelock black holes, $S'_W$ can change sign on non-planar branches, reversing the temperature slope stability assignment. However, on ghost-free and branch-regular Lovelock exteriors $S'_W$ remains positive. Thus the off-shell Hessian criterion also diagnoses why the ordinary slope rule is protected on physically admissible black holes branches.

### [92] [Lorentz-violating signatures in quasi-periodic oscillations from a magnetised Kalb-Ramond black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03242)
*Luiz F. G. Rodrigues,Francisco S. N. Lobo,Manuel E. Rodrigues*

TL;DR: 本文研究了Kalb-Ramond场驱动的类史瓦西黑洞周围带电粒子在均匀外磁场中的动力学，通过蒙特卡洛马尔可夫链（MCMC）分析微类星体观测数据，发现纯史瓦西模型被统计排除，而洛伦兹破缺参数$l$与磁场的联合效应可有效建模准周期振荡（QPO）频率，且$l$随天体质量增大而减小，表明洛伦兹破缺可能在强场区留下可观测印记。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索洛伦兹破缺（Lorentz violation）和磁场共同作用下黑洞周围带电粒子的轨道动力学，并利用微类星体的准周期振荡（quasi-periodic oscillation, QPO）观测数据检验该框架的统计有效性，为量子引力现象学（quantum-gravity phenomenology）提供新的测试途径。

Method: 推导了带电粒子在Kalb-Ramond场修正的类史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild-like black hole）周围的完整运动方程、有效势和准周期振荡（QPO）的基本频率；采用蒙特卡洛马尔可夫链（Monte Carlo Markov Chain, MCMC）方法，结合GRO 1655-40、XTE 1550-564和GRS 1915+105三个微类星体的观测数据进行统计分析。

Result: 纯史瓦西模型对所有三个源均被统计排除；对于GRO 1655-40和XTE 1550-564，仅磁场与洛伦兹破缺的联合效应能给出统计稳健的模型，最佳拟合值为$\mathcal{B}\sim 0.03$-$0.04$、$l\sim 0.08$--$0.10$；对于GRS 1915+105，仅洛伦兹破缺参数即可拟合QPO频率，且$ΔAIC = ΔBIC = 0$；三个源的$l$值均随天体质量增大而减小，呈现质量依赖标度（mass-dependent scaling）趋势。

Conclusion: Kalb-Ramond场与磁场的联合框架是建模微类星体QPO的可行且统计稳健的方案；洛伦兹破缺对引力的修正可能在强场区域留下可观测信号，为利用当前及下一代X射线任务检验量子引力现象学提供了新方向。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of charged particles around a Schwarzschild-like black hole sourced by a Kalb-Ramond field and immersed in a uniform external magnetic field. The Kalb-Ramond field introduces a Lorentz violation parameter $l$ that modifies the spacetime geometry, while the magnetic field profoundly influences the trajectories through the Lorentz force, leading to a rich variety of orbital behaviours including curled (epicyclic) motion and dramatic transitions between distinct energy boundary configurations. We derive the full equations of motion, the effective potential, and the fundamental frequencies of quasi-periodic oscillations, and perform a comprehensive Monte Carlo Markov Chain (MCMC) analysis using observational data from the microquasars GRO 1655-40, XTE 1550-564, and GRS 1915+105. The pure Schwarzschild model is statistically ruled out for all three sources. For GRO 1655-40 and XTE 1550-564, only the combined effect of the magnetic field and Lorentz violation yields statistically robust models, with best-fit values $\mathcal{B}\sim 0.03$-$0.04$ and $l\sim 0.08$--$0.10$. Remarkably, for GRS 1915+105, the most massive object in our sample, the Lorentz violation parameter alone is sufficient to model the QPO frequencies, yielding an optimal fit with $ΔAIC = ΔBIC = 0$. Across all three objects, a clear trend emerges: the required value of $l$ decreases as the mass of the astrophysical object increases, suggesting a mass-dependent scaling of the Kalb-Ramond parameter. These findings establish the combined KR and magnetic field framework as a viable and statistically robust scenario for modeling QPOs in microquasars, and indicate that Lorentz-violating modifications to gravity may leave observable imprints in the strong-field regime, offering new avenues for testing quantum-gravity phenomenology with current and next-generation X-ray missions.

Abstract: Echo models phenomenologically encode possible near-horizon structure by replacing the purely ingoing horizon-side condition with an effective reflecting inner boundary near the would-be horizon. ### [94] [Model-Independent Search Discards Faint Lensed-Pairs of Gravitational Wave Events in the Sub-Threshold Candidates of GWTC-4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03346)
*Aniruddha Chakraborty,Suvodip Mukherjee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究首次对GWTC-4全部应变数据（含约90个超级事件和约800个次阈值事件，共约11,000个事件对）执行了基于互相关的模型无关引力波透镜搜索（GLANCE方法）。尽管发现四对候选事件具有≥2σ的交叉相关显著性，但在两个LIGO探测器中均未超过3σ，从而强有力地排除了GWTC-4中存在统计上显著的次阈值透镜引力波事件。该零结果将透镜探测率上界约束为≤1.5/年。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在当前理解下，透镜事件发生率约为千分之几，而地面探测器网络仅探测到数百次引力波事件；若纳入次阈值（sub-threshold）事件，总检测数可跨越数千量级，从而显著提高透镜探测几率。因此，有必要开展包含两类事件的系统性透镜搜索。

Method: 采用基于互相关（cross-correlation）的模型无关透镜搜索技术GLANCE，覆盖GWTC-4全部应变数据，包含约90个超级事件（super-events）和约800个次阈值事件，形成约11,000个事件对；采用较高的虚警率（False Alarm Rate, FAR）阈值以深入噪声主导区域进行搜索，并进一步对感兴趣的事件对进行频谱图（spectrogram）数据质量检查、天图（sky-map）重叠检查以及次阈值事件的贝叶斯参数（Bayesian parameter）探索。

Result: 搜索发现四对潜在地的事件对具有≥2σ的交叉相关显著性，但在LIGO-Hanford和LIGO-Livingston两个探测器中均未超过3σ，因此强有力地排除了GWTC-4中任何统计显著的次阈值透镜引力波事件。该零结果将透镜探测率上界约束为≤1.5/年（含次阈值事件候选体）。

Conclusion: GWTC-4中不存在统计显著的次阈值透镜引力波事件，透镜探测率上界为≤1.5/年。未来随着观测时间增加，当前一代引力波探测器有望实现透镜引力波的直接探测。

Abstract: Gravitational lensing of gravitational waves (GWs) can produce multiple images in the geometric optics limit. These lensed GW images arrive at different times, are amplified by different magnification factors, and are shifted by constant phases. With current understanding, the occurrence of lensed events stands at a few per thousand events, and the number of GW detections is a few hundred with the ground-based detector network. However, with the inclusion of the sub-threshold events, the total number of detections crosses a few thousand. Therefore, a search that includes both types of events yields a higher chance of lensing detection. In this work, we carry out the first model-independent lensing search using a cross-correlation-based technique GLANCE over the entire volume of the GWTC-4 strain data, containing $\sim 90$ super-events $\sim 800$ sub-events forming a total of $\sim 11,000$ event pairs with a higher False Alarm Rate (FAR) event rate allowing to search deep in the noise dominated regime. We further conduct their spectrogram checks to inspect data quality, sky-map overlap of the interesting pairs, and a Bayesian parameter exploration of the sub-event to make a robust lensing detection. Although the search indicated four pairs of potential events with cross-correlation significance $\geq 2σ$, none were above $3σ$ at both the LIGO-Hanford and LIGO-Livingston detectors. This makes it possible to strongly rule out the presence of any statistically significant sub-threshold lensed GW event in GWTC-4. The null detection translates to an upper bound on the lensing detection rate to be $\leq$ 1.5/yr with inclusion of the sub-threshold event candidates. In the future, with more observation time, the detection of lensed GW can be possible from the current generation of GW detectors.

### [95] [Quantum Matter Makes Lightcones Quantum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03671)
*Tomohiro Fujita,Misao Sasaki*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明，当决定光锥的物质本身处于量子态时，时空的因果结构（causal structure）也会变得量子化：光锥位置成为非对易算符，因果关系可处于类时与类空的叠加态，且Wightman函数的光锥奇点被抹平，产生有效紫外截断（UV cutoff）。这一结论在非相对论性量子粒子产生的牛顿引力势背景中严格推导，无需引入量子化引力子（quantized gravitons）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在引力物理中，物质不仅存在于时空之中，还决定了定义因果关系的因果结构（causal structure）。当这种决定光锥的物质本身处于量子态时，因果结构会如何变化，是一个尚未被充分理解的基本问题。本文在一个可控的低能框架下严格回答这一问题。

Method: 考虑一个无质量标量场（massless scalar field）在由非相对论性量子粒子产生的牛顿引力势（Newtonian gravitational potential）背景中传播。通过分析算符取值的Shapiro延迟（operator-valued Shapiro delay），研究量子物质对光锥结构的影响。

Result: 得到三个主要结果：(i) 因果边界（causal-boundary）的位移被提升为非对易算符（noncommuting observables），给因果结构带来不可约的量子不确定性；(ii) 两点之间的因果关系可以处于类时（timelike）与类空（spacelike）的量子叠加态；(iii) 当对源自由度求迹后，Wightman函数的光锥奇点（light-cone singularity）被抹平，产生一个有效紫外截断。

Conclusion: 量子物质不仅会在时空内涨落，还会使因果结构本身变得量子化——这一效应在无需量子化引力子的低能设置中即可出现。

Abstract: In gravitational physics, matter does not merely move within spacetime; it also determines the light cones that define causal relations. What happens when the matter that determines these light cones is itself in a quantum state? We address this question in a controlled low-energy setting: a massless scalar field propagating in the spacetime with the Newtonian gravitational potential sourced by a non-relativistic quantum particle. We show that the light cones are affected by an operator-valued Shapiro delay, with the three consequences: (i) causal-boundary shifts are promoted to noncommuting observables, giving the causal structure an irreducible quantum uncertainty; (ii) the causal relation between two fixed spacetime points can become a superposition of timelike and spacelike configurations; and (iii) tracing out the source smears the Wightman light-cone singularity, producing an effective UV cutoff. Thus, quantum matter does not merely fluctuate within spacetime; it makes the causal structure itself quantum, even without quantized gravitons.

### [96] [Critical collapse of a self-interacting scalar field in asymptotically anti-de Sitter spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03751)
*Li-Jie Xin,Xiangdong Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究渐近反德西特（anti-de Sitter, AdS）时空中球对称无质量标量场的临界引力坍缩行为，特别是验证标量场势能形式是否会影响临界现象。

Method: 采用极坐标（polar coordinates）和双零坐标（double null coordinates）两种坐标系进行数值计算并交叉验证；通过精细调节不同AdS半径ℓ下标量场的初始振幅，研究临界坍缩行为。

Result: 在ℓ=8时确认发生II型临界坍缩（type II critical collapse），回声周期和临界指数与Choptuik经典结果高度一致；对于所有测试的ℓ值，回声周期Δ≈3.4和临界指数γ≈0.37基本保持不变。

Conclusion: 所采用的势能形式不会以任何有意义的方式改变引力坍缩的临界行为，表明该临界现象具有鲁棒性（robustness）。

Abstract: We study the critical gravitational collapse of a spherically symmetric massless scalar field in asymptotically anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetime. The scalar field potential adopted here is inversely proportional to the square of the AdS curvature radius $\ell$, and the system admits a well-known exact static solution. Working in polar coordinates, we first confirm that type II critical collapse occurs for a range of distinct initial configurations when $\ell=8$, where the measured echoing period and critical exponent are in excellent agreement with Choptuik's classic results. We then fine-tune the initial amplitude of the scalar field for a series of AdS radii $\ell$, performing calculations in both polar coordinates and double null coordinates to cross-validate our results. We find that the form of the potential does not alter the critical behavior of gravitational collapse in any meaningful way: in particular, both the echoing period ($Δ\approx 3.4$) and critical exponent ($γ\approx 0.37$) remain essentially unchanged across all tested values of $\ell$.

### [97] [A master equation for Carter-separable stationary axisymmetric spacetimes and compatible sources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03758)
*Hyeong-Chan Kim*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明，在稳态轴对称时空（stationary axisymmetric spacetimes）的Carter-射影（Carter-projective）扇区中，剩余的对角爱因斯坦方程等价于一个带源的主方程（sourced master equation）。射影结构由非对角爱因斯坦方程固定作为输入。在反指指数分支（anti-aligned exponential branch）中（包含Kerr–Carter和Plebański–Demiański实截面），剩余的对角爱因斯坦系统可简化为一个关于径向结构函数Δ(r)和角向结构函数Y(x)的主方程。该约化伴随两个爱因斯坦张量的几何对角恒等式，它们成为可允许物质源的代数相容性条件。在齐次极限下，真空-Λ Kerr–Carter和Plebański–Demiański族作为同一主算子的解被恢复。此外还展示了该构造的射影协变性（projective covariance），并讨论了兼容的物质源，包括对齐的麦克斯韦场（aligned Maxwell field）和可分离的各向异性例子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 简化稳态轴对称时空中剩余对角爱因斯坦方程的处理，揭示其与射影结构和物质源之间的内在代数与几何关系。

Method: 利用Carter-射影扇区结构，以非对角爱因斯坦方程固定射影输入，将剩余对角爱因斯坦系统约化为单一主方程；通过两个几何对角恒等式建立物质源的代数相容性条件。

Result: 在反指指数分支中，对角爱因斯坦系统简化为关于Δ(r)和Y(x)的带源主方程；真空-Λ Kerr–Carter和Plebański–Demiański族作为同一主算子的齐次解被恢复；构造具有射影协变性。

Conclusion: 该主方程框架统一描述了稳态轴对称时空的对角扇区，并自然兼容对齐麦克斯韦场等物质源，为可分离各向异性源的分析提供了基础。

Abstract: We show that the remaining diagonal Einstein equations in the Carter-projective sector of stationary axisymmetric spacetimes are equivalent to a single sourced master equation. The projective structure is taken as the input fixed by the off-diagonal Einstein equations. In the anti-aligned exponential branch, which contains the Kerr--Carter and Plebański--Demiański real section, the remaining diagonal Einstein system reduces to \[
  \mathcal L_{\rm CP}[Δ,Y]
  =16πΣ\left( T_{\hat0\hat0}+T_{\hat3\hat3} \right), \] where \(Δ(r)\) and \(Y(x)\) are the radial and angular structure functions. The reduction is accompanied by two geometric diagonal identities of the Einstein tensor, which become algebraic compatibility conditions on admissible matter sources. In the homogeneous limit, the vacuum--\(Λ\) Kerr--Carter and Plebański--Demiański families are recovered as solutions of the same master operator. We also show the projective covariance of the construction and discuss compatible sources, including the aligned Maxwell field and separable anisotropic examples.

</details>


### [98] [Geodesic completeness of singularity free gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03944)
*Vasil Todorinov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类广义相对论框架下无奇点（singularity free）的引力理论，通过推广一个已有的引力势，导出了在大尺度上退化为平坦时空的相对论性引力理论。这些理论中的黑洞解通常具有双视界（two horizon）结构，且存在一个子类能实现测地完备性（geodesic completeness）穿过原点。研究还表明，此类黑洞解存在一个最小允许质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决广义相对论中黑洞奇点（singularity）问题，构造在经典框架内无奇点的引力理论，避免时空曲率和引力势在原点处发散。

Method: 通过推广文献[1]中提出的引力势，构造一类相对论性无奇点引力理论，并验证其在大尺度上退化为平坦时空；分析其引力势、时空曲率、视界结构以及测地完备性等几何性质。

Result: 所选引力势能消除奇点，且力和时空曲率在大距离处趋于零；这类无奇点黑洞解普遍具有双视界结构；存在一个子类可实现穿过原点的测地完备性；黑洞解存在一个最小允许质量。

Conclusion: 所构造的一类无奇点引力理论能在经典层面避免奇点问题，双视界结构和最小质量预言为黑洞物理提供了新的理论约束和可检验的后果。

Abstract: Generalizing the gravitational potential first proposed in [1] we derive a large class of relativistic singularity free theories of gravity, which reduce to flat spacetime at large distances. We verify that for the chosen gravitational potential the force and the space-time curvature resolve the singularity and vanish at large distances. We show that those singularity free black hole solutions generically have a two horizon structure. Furthermore, we show that there is a subclass of potentials which produce a geometries geodesically complete through the origin. We discuss the implications of the effects resulting from such theories and show that black holes solutions are predicted to have minimum allowed mass.

### [99] [Entropy Production and the Gravitational Origin of the Second Law](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02727)
*Simone Antonini,Antonino Marciano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在非平衡框架下研究引力动力学与热力学第二定律的关系，通过引入时空度规的随机几何流（stochastic geometric flow）并定义熵产生（entropy production），证明爱因斯坦场方程对应熵产生为零的可逆极限，而热力学第二定律源自非平衡演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Jacobson关于爱因斯坦方程的热力学推导推广至非平衡框架，以阐明引力动力学与热力学第二定律之间的深层联系。

Method: 引入时空度规的随机几何流（stochastic geometric flow），并将熵产生定义为正向与时间反演轨迹的比值（ratio between forward and time-reversed trajectories）。

Result: 熵产生由曲率（curvature）和物质贡献（matter contributions）控制；熵产生为零时，系统满足爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein field equations）。

Conclusion: 经典广义相对论（classical general relativity）作为底层随机几何动力学（stochastic geometro-dynamics）的可逆极限（reversible limit）出现，热力学第二定律则源于其非平衡演化（non-equilibrium evolution）。

Abstract: We investigate the relation between gravitational dynamics and the second law of thermodynamics in a non-equilibrium framework. Extending Jacobson's thermodynamic derivation of the Einstein equations, we introduce a stochastic geometric flow for the spacetime metric and define entropy production as the ratio between forward and time-reversed trajectories. We show that entropy production is governed by curvature and matter contributions, and that its vanishing selects configurations satisfying the Einstein field equations. Classical general relativity thus emerges as the reversible limit of an underlying stochastic geometro-dynamics, while the second law arises from its non-equilibrium evolution.

</details>


### [100] [Testing the ${\rm ER=EPR}$ conjecture with entangled photons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02943)
*Kimet Jusufi,Francisco S. N. Lobo,Douglas Singleton*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过弦启发长度尺度对Aichelburg-Sexl冲击波度规进行正则化，得到无奇点的引力势，揭示了其横向几何为零喉爱因斯坦-罗森虫洞，为纠缠光子的ER=EPR猜想提供了显式几何实现；同时发现引力自能依赖于光子纵向尺度，并建立了纠缠熵解释，表明极端相对论量子受到显著的量子引力效应抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证纠缠光子对是否可以通过爱因斯坦-罗森虫洞（Einstein-Rosen wormhole）几何实现ER=EPR猜想，并探究无质量粒子（massless particles）在弦尺度下的引力自能（gravitational self-energy）行为及其对波函数坍缩的可能影响。

Method: 采用弦启发长度尺度 $l_0$ 对无质量粒子的 Aichelburg-Sexl 冲击波度规（shock-wave metric）进行正则化，消除点源奇点；通过坐标变换揭示横向几何为零喉（zero-throat）爱因斯坦-罗森虫洞；计算引力自能并引入有效纠缠温度（entanglement temperature）$k_B T_{\rm ent}\sim\hbar c/(2πL)$ 建立纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）解释。

Result: 正则化后得到无奇点引力势；对横向分离的光子对，引力自能正比于 $4G(\hbarω)^2/(c^4 L)\ln(d^2/l_0^2)$，被系数 $1/L$ 强烈抑制；对 $e^{+} e^{-}\to2γ$ 产生的背对背光子对，虫洞无额外束缚能，对数相互作用能仅在光子分离后才出现；对光学光子，坍缩时间超过 $10^{30}$ 年。

Conclusion: 该工作为检验ER=EPR猜想提供了严谨的理论框架，并揭示了极端相对论性量子（ultra-relativistic quanta）的量子引力效应受到深度抑制。

Abstract: We regularize the Aichelburg-Sexl shock-wave metric for massless particles by smearing the point-like source over a string-inspired length scale $l_0$, obtaining a singularity-free gravitational potential. A coordinate transformation reveals that the transverse geometry is a zero-throat Einstein-Rosen wormhole, providing an explicit geometric realization of the ER=EPR conjecture for entangled photons. Crucially, we show that the gravitational self-energy depends on the photon's longitudinal extent $L$ (its wavelength) and, for a transversely separated photon pair, is suppressed by a factor $1/L$, giving $E^{\rm GSE}\sim 4G(\hbarω)^2/(c^4 L)\ln(d^2/l_0^2)$. For the coincident back-to-back pair created in $e^{+} e^{-}\to2γ$, the wormhole carries no additional binding energy; the logarithmic interaction energy emerges only after the entangled photons separate to a distance $d$, stretching the ER bridge. We further provide an entanglement-entropy interpretation: by computing the entanglement entropy of null intervals in the shock-wave geometry and introducing an effective entanglement temperature $k_B T_{\rm ent}\sim\hbar c/(2πL)$, we recover the same scaling and normalization of the gravitational self-energy. For optical photons the corresponding collapse time exceeds $10^{30}$ years, making isolated photons immune to gravity-induced wave-function collapse. These findings establish a rigorous playground for testing ER=EPR and reveal a deep suppression of quantum-gravity effects for ultra-relativistic quanta.

</details>

### [101] [Negative temperature coefficient of Gilbert damping in magnetic bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02858)
*Lulu Cao,Yuting Gong,Xianyang Lu,Yongbing Xu,Ya Zhai,Jing Wu,Roy W. Chantrell,Richard F. L. Evans*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过原子模拟和实验测量发现，在Py/Nd双层膜中，吉尔伯特阻尼（Gilbert damping）随温度升高而降低，这与简单金属中阻尼随温度升高而增大的传统行为相反。该效应源于界面自旋泵浦（spin pumping）导致的增强阻尼，高温引起弛豫过程中界面与体磁化的动态分离，且阻尼的温度依赖性可通过调节Nd覆盖层厚度来控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 吉尔伯特阻尼是决定自旋电子学器件（spintronic devices）开关速度和能耗的关键磁学参数。简单金属中本征吉尔伯特阻尼随温度升高而增大，并在居里温度（Curie temperature）附近因自旋涨落（spin fluctuations）发散。本研究旨在探索Py/Nd双层膜中可能存在的反常温度依赖行为。

Method: 采用原子模拟（atomistic simulations）和实验测量相结合的方法，系统研究了Py/Nd双层膜中吉尔伯特阻尼随温度的变化规律，并通过改变Nd覆盖层厚度来调控阻尼的温度依赖性。

Result: 在Py/Nd双层膜中观察到吉尔伯特阻尼随温度升高而降低的反常行为，与简单金属中的传统趋势相反。该效应归因于界面处自旋泵浦引起的增强阻尼，高温导致弛豫过程中界面磁化与体磁化发生动态分离。此外，通过调节Nd覆盖层厚度可控制阻尼的温度依赖性。

Conclusion: 这一发现揭示了一种新的自旋电子学效应（spintronic effect），可用于调控纳米材料和器件的动态磁学性质，从而实现更高的能量效率或改进的开关动力学特性。

Abstract: The Gilbert damping of magnetic materials is an important magnetic parameter that determines the switching speed and energy dissipation of spintronic devices. In simple metals, the intrinsic Gilbert damping increases with temperature and diverges near the Curie temperature as a result of spin fluctuations. Here we present atomistic simulations and experimental measurements showing surprising and opposite behavior in Py/Nd bilayers, where the Gilbert damping decreases with increasing temperature. The effect arises because of the enhanced damping at the interface as a result of spin pumping, where elevated temperatures cause a dynamic separation of the interfacial and bulk magnetization during relaxation. Furthermore, the temperature dependence of the damping can be controlled by varying the thickness of the Nd capping layer. Our findings present a new spintronic effect that can be used to modify the dynamic properties of nanoscale materials and devices for enhanced energy efficiency or with improved switching dynamics.

</details>


### [102] [Second-Order Synaptic Memory using Inherent Plasticity of Moiré Superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02931)
*Tanweer Ahmed,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Fèlix Casanova,Luis E. Hueso*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明，纯碳组成的扭曲双层石墨烯（twisted double bilayer graphene, tDBLG）莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice）在存在转角无序（twist-angle disorder）时，可以展现电子迟滞（electronic hysteresis）与可塑性（plasticity），并利用电子可塑性与二阶非线性（second-order nonlinearity）的共存实现了二阶突触存储器件（second-order synaptic memory device），为单元素材料中的神经形态计算（neuromorphic computing）提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的电子突触功能实现依赖于引入外禀电荷陷阱（extrinsic charge-traps）或极性组分（polar components），而寻找在单元素量子材料中直接实现突触功能的方法是一个基本挑战。

Method: 利用纯碳组成的扭曲双层石墨烯（tDBLG）莫尔超晶格，通过引入转角无序打破莫尔尺度上的反演对称性（inversion symmetry breaking），从而产生电子迟滞、可塑性以及无序介导的外禀二阶非线性电响应（second-order nonlinear electrical response）。

Result: 二阶非线性的符号和大小均可通过改变载流子浓度（carrier concentration）和垂直位移场（vertical displacement field）进行高度调控。利用电子可塑性与二阶非线性的共存，成功实现了二阶突触存储器件。

Conclusion: 应变莫尔碳基系统（strained moiré carbon systems）为低能耗神经形态计算提供了一个强大的新平台，表明仅凭单元素材料中的对称性破缺物理即可涌现出复杂的电子功能。

Abstract: Achieving synaptic functionality electronically in a single-element quantum material is a fundamental challenge, as conventional methods rely on the introduction of extrinsic charge-traps or polar components. Here, we demonstrate that twisted double bilayer graphene (tDBLG) moiré superlattices, composed purely of carbon, exhibit electronic hysteresis and plasticity in presence of twist-angle disorder. Inversion symmetry breaking at the moiré length scales also gives rise to second-order nonlinear electrical response via disorder-mediated extrinsic mechanisms. Such second-order nonlinearity is highly tunable in both sign and magnitude by varying carrier concentration and vertical displacement field. We harness the coexistence of electronic plasticity and second-order nonlinearity to realize a second-order synaptic memory device. Our findings establish strained moiré carbon systems as a powerful new platform for energy-efficient neuromorphic computing, demonstrating that complex electronic functionality can emerge purely from symmetry breaking physics in a single-element material.

### [103] [Geometric aspects of spin transport in magnetic multilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03041)
*Valentin Fadeev*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从几何角度讨论了自旋依赖的转移矩阵形式体系在磁性多层膜中的应用，通过路径有序指数、Iwasawa分解和Weyl室变量等几何工具，揭示了自旋过滤到自旋-轨道混合的过渡机制，并指出该方法可推广至轨道输运等更高维内禀空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自旋依赖转移矩阵（spin-dependent transfer matrix）形式体系在磁性多层膜研究中缺乏统一的几何解释，难以揭示输运过程中的内在结构约束和对称性。本文旨在建立该形式体系的几何基础，以更自然地理解自旋输运中的不变量和拓扑结构。

Method: 将定态薛定谔方程（stationary Schrödinger equation）改写为一阶空间演化问题，将转移矩阵解释为路径有序指数（path-ordered exponential）；利用Iwasawa分解（Iwasawa decomposition）将反射矩阵上的Möbius作用（Möbius action）与非紧致群约束（noncompact group constraint）联系起来；识别Weyl室变量（Weyl-chamber variables）为最小非紧致输运不变量，并分析扭矩相关自旋结构来自紧致部分（compact-sector）和对易子（commutator）贡献。

Result: 通过一系列多层膜示例，展示了从纯自旋过滤（pure spin filtering）到可控自旋-轨道混合（controlled spin-orbit mixing）的过渡，以及由此导致的Weyl室轨迹（Weyl-chamber trajectories）的形变。

Conclusion: 该几何形式体系为磁性多层膜中自旋输运提供了统一框架，并可扩展至与轨道输运（orbital transport）相关的更高维内禀空间及实际计算。

Abstract: We discuss spin-dependent transfer-matrix formalism applied to magnetic multilayers in geometric terms. Starting from the stationary Schrödinger equation rewritten as a first-order spatial evolution problem, we interpret the transfer matrix as a path-ordered exponential and relate its matching-matrix construction to a noncompact group constraint. We thenconnect the induced Möbius action on reflection matrices to an Iwasawa decomposition, identify Weyl-chamber variables as the minimal noncompact transport invariants, and show how torque-related spin structures arise from compact-sector and commutator contributions. A sequence of multilayer examples illustrates the transition from pure spin filtering to controlled spin-orbit mixing and the resulting deformation of Weyl-chamber trajectories. We finally comment on the extension to higher-dimensional internal spaces relevant to orbital transport and realistic calculations.

</details>


### [104] [Generation and time evolution of anomalous Floquet Majorana flat edge modes in two-dimensional noncolinear magnet-superconductor heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03193)
*Kamalesh Bera,Priyanka Mohan,Arijit Saha*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从理论上研究了在化学势谐波驱动下，二维磁体-超导体异质结构（Shiba晶格）中实现无间隙Floquet拓扑超导相，获得了0模和π模Floquet Majorana平坦边缘模（FMFEMs），并通过卷绕数、布里渊-维格纳（BW）与Floquet微扰理论（FPT）进行了拓扑表征与分析验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在周期性驱动（化学势谐波驱动）下，二维磁体-超导体异质结构（2D Shiba晶格）中能否实现无间隙Floquet拓扑超导相，并理解其边缘态的拓扑性质。

Method: 采用实空间紧束缚模型（real-space tight-binding model）获得准能量谱；利用卷绕数（winding number）基于等效体有效动量空间哈密顿量的手征对称性进行拓扑表征；结合布里渊-维格纳（Brillouin-Wigner, BW）理论和Floquet微扰理论（Floquet perturbation theory, FPT）进行解析分析，并与精确数值结果对比。

Result: 在准能量谱中观测到常规的0模和反常的π模Floquet Majorana平坦边缘模（FMFEMs）；在高频高幅值区域，尤其是接近0-准能量模时，精确数值、BW和FPT结果之间具有良好的一致性。

Conclusion: 周期性驱动可在二维Shiba晶格中实现Floquet拓扑超导相，产生FMFEMs；卷绕数可有效表征其拓扑性质；BW与FPT在高频高幅值区域能较好地描述该体系。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the realization of gapless Floquet topological superconducting phases in a two-dimensional magnet-superconductor heterostructure (2D Shiba lattice) in the presence of a harmonic drive implemented in the chemical potential. Employing a real-space tight-binding model, we obtain both the regular $0$- and anomalous $π$-Floquet Majorana flat edge modes (FMFEMs) in the quasi-energy spectrum. We also study the real-time evolution of the FMFEMs and analyze their local density of states in the presence of such a periodic drive. The topological characterization is performed using the winding number, exploiting the chiral symmetry of the equivalent bulk effective momentum-space Hamiltonian. This is also supported by the corresponding edge state spectra. Furthermore, we employ the Brillouin-Wigner (BW) and Floquet perturbation theory (FPT) to gain analytical insight into the problem. We compare our exact (numerical), BW, and FPT results in terms of the quasi-energy spectra obtained across different frequency regimes. We find good agreement between the exact numerical, BW, and FPT results in the higher-frequency and high-amplitude domain, particularly close to the $0$-quasi-energy modes.

</details>


### [105] [Tailoring pure valley-Zeeman spin-orbit coupling in WSe$_2$-encapsulated monolayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03278)
*Yaqing Han,Siqi Jiang,Jingkuan Xiao,Jiawei Jiang,Yulu Liu,Jiabei Huang,Yu Du,Di Zhang,Fuzhuo Lian,Wanting Xu,Siqin Wang,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Xiaoxiang Xi,Alexander S. Mayorov,Renjun Du,Kai Chang,Hongxin Yang,Lei Wang,Geliang Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 通过将单层石墨烯封装在两块平行扭转的WSe₂单层之间，实现了纯谷-塞曼自旋-轨道耦合（valley-Zeeman spin-orbit coupling），观察到由谷-塞曼能量与回旋能量竞争驱动的朗道能级（Landau levels）对称性强制重排，以及通过封装几何调控可完全猝灭邻近自旋-轨道耦合（proximity spin-orbit coupling）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管过渡金属硫族化合物（transition metal dichalcogenide, TMD）封装石墨烯在理论上可选择性调控自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）分量，但实验实现一直未能达成。

Method: 将单层石墨烯封装在两块平行扭转的WSe₂单层之间，构建扭转范德华异质结（twisted van der Waals heterostructures），并通过改变封装几何来调控邻近效应。

Result: 在单层石墨烯中实现了纯谷-塞曼自旋-轨道耦合；观测到由固定谷-塞曼能量与磁场依赖的回旋能量（cyclotron energy）竞争所驱动的朗道能级对称性强制重排，表现为量子霍尔效应（quantum Hall effect）中从对称性破缺态向四重简并整数或半整数量子霍尔序列的转变；并展示了通过调整封装几何完全猝灭邻近自旋-轨道耦合的能力。

Conclusion: 扭转范德华异质结中工程化邻近效应是一种有效设计电子特性的平台；本工作实现了纯谷-塞曼型自旋-轨道耦合并实验证实了相应的量子霍尔态转变，为自旋电子学应用提供了新的调控手段。

Abstract: Engineering proximity effects in twisted van der Waals heterostructures offers a powerful platform for designing electronic properties. While theoretical predictions of quantum interference in transition metal dichalcogenide-encapsulated graphene can selectively control the spin-orbit coupling component, experimental realizations have remained elusive. Here, we report pure valley-Zeeman spin-orbit coupling in monolayer graphene, achieved by encapsulation between two parallel twisted WSe$_2$ monolayers. We observed a symmetry-enforced reordering of Landau levels, which is driven by the competition between the fixed valley-Zeeman energy and the magnetic-field-dependent cyclotron energy. This reordering is characterized by a transition from symmetry-broken states in the quantum Hall effect to a restored fourfold degeneracy with integer or half-integer quantum Hall sequences. We also demonstrate the ability to completely quench the proximity spin-orbit coupling by tuning the encapsulated geometry.

</details>


### [106] [Spin-wave phase modulation using magnetic domain walls in dipolarly coupled structures for non-volatile magnonic computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03336)
*Hanadi Mortada,Philipp Pirro,Alexandre Abbass Hamadeh*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于畴壁位置控制的自旋波移相器（spin-wave phase shifter），利用两个紧密波导间的偶极耦合（dipolar coupling）实现接近360°的连续相位调谐，同时保持自旋波振幅不变。微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulation）验证了由具有强垂直磁各向异性的掺铋钇铁石榴石（bismuth-doped YIG）制成的混合结构，通过半环中的畴壁位移改变直波导中的色散关系（dispersion relation），从而提供紧凑且可动态重构的移相机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可控移相器是自旋波逻辑与信息处理器件中的关键组件，现有方案在连续相位调谐范围和振幅稳定性方面存在局限。

Method: 采用微磁模拟的方法，构建了一个由纳米级波导与半环形结构组成的无偏置混合系统，两者均由具有强垂直磁各向异性的掺铋钇铁石榴石制成，并通过静磁耦合实现相互作用。

Result: 移动半环中的畴壁位置可改变相邻直波导的色散关系，从而在保持自旋波振幅恒定的条件下实现接近360°的连续相位调谐。

Conclusion: 该方案提供了一种精确且非易失（non-volatile）的自旋波传播控制方式，并与节能型磁子逻辑架构（magnonic logic architectures）兼容。

Abstract: A controllable phase shifter is a key component for spin-wave-based logic and information processing devices. Here, we propose a domain-wall-position-controlled spin-wave phase shifter that exploits dipolar coupling between two closely spaced waveguides to enable continuous phase tuning over a range approaching 360degrees while keeping the spin-wave amplitude constant. Using micromagnetic simulations, we model a bias-free hybrid structure composed of a nanoscale waveguide magnetostatically coupled to a half-ring-shaped structure both made from bismuth-doped yttrium iron garnet with strong perpendicular magnetic anisotropy. Displacing a domain wall in the half-ring modulates the dispersion relation in the adjacent straight waveguide due to the changed magnetostatic interaction, providing a compact and dynamically reconfigurable phase-shifting mechanism. This approach offers precise and non-volatile control over spin-wave propagation and is compatible with energy-efficient magnonic logic architectures.

### [107] [Epitaxial $\mathrm{Co_2MnSi}$ with intrinsic magnetocrystalline anisotropy as a route to bias-field-free nonlinear half-metal magnonics at the nanoscale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03431)

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了具有完美晶格有序性的半金属Heusler化合物Co₂MnSi波导中的线性和非线性自旋波动力学，揭示了其固有的立方磁晶各向异性可有效抑制非线性不稳定性，并在零偏置场下实现稳定的Damon-Eshbach几何构型，确立了Co₂MnSi作为偏置场自由非线性半金属磁子学（half-metal magnonics）的稳健可扩展平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半金属Heusler化合物（如Co₂MnSi）兼具100%自旋极化与超低Gilbert阻尼（Gilbert damping, α ≤ 10⁻³），为混合非传统计算架构提供了理想材料基础；然而其优异物性对晶格有序度高度敏感，纳米器件的结构完整性制备仍具挑战，导致材料参数对非线性自旋波动力学的影响迄今尚未被充分探索。

Method: 研究采用具有外延L2₁有序结构的Co₂MnSi波导，在横向磁化条件下系统测量线性和非线性自旋波（spin-wave）动力学，通过分析磁晶各向异性（magnetocrystalline anisotropy）对自旋波色散关系的重塑效应，评估其对非线性不稳定性抑制及器件几何构型的影响。

Result: 证实了外延L2₁有序Co₂MnSi存在包含一阶和二阶贡献的本征立方各向异性（cubic anisotropy），使磁化沿⟨110⟩晶向稳定排列；图案化结构中的晶体完整性得以保持，磁性未受破坏；磁晶各向异性重塑了自旋波色散，产生覆盖数GHz的一阶非线性不稳定性抑制区间，即使在零偏置场下仍有效；该各向异性可抵消形状退磁（shape demagnetization）效应，在Damon-Eshbach几何中实现低偏置场稳定操作，兼具高群速度和长衰减长度。

Conclusion: 结合已证实的半金属性与超低Gilbert阻尼，该研究确立了Co₂MnSi作为一种稳健、可扩展的平台，适用于偏置场自由的非线性半金属磁子学（bias-field-free nonlinear half-metal magnonics），为磁子学与自旋电子学混合非传统计算开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Half-metallic Heusler compounds like $\mathrm{Co_2MnSi}$ allow to bridge magnonic and spintronic functionality for hybrid unconventional computing approaches with sought-after properties like 100% spin polarization and associated low Gilbert damping $α\leq 10^{-3}$. However, the desirable material parameters are inherently tied to the crystal lattice with a particularly critical dependence on structural order in $\mathrm{Co_2MnSi}$. To date, the successful fabrication of nanoscale devices with robust structural integrity remains yet a challenge, and consequently the impact of the material parameters on the resulting nonlinear spin-wave dynamics remains largely unexplored. Here, we report on a study of linear and nonlinear spin-wave dynamics in transversally magnetized $\mathrm{Co_2MnSi}$ waveguides with impeccable crystalline ordering. We show that epitaxial, $\mathrm{L2}_1$-ordered $\mathrm{Co_2MnSi}$ exhibits an intrinsic cubic anisotropy with first- and second-order contributions, stabilizing a magnetization alignment along the crystal $\langle110\rangle$ directions. We confirm the implication of an unaffected crystal structure resulting in preserved magnetic properties in the patterned structures. Herein, the persistent magnetocrystalline anisotropy reshapes the spin-wave dispersion which yields a first-order nonlinear instability suppression range extending over several GHz - even for vanishing bias fields. Moreover, the intrinsic magnetocrystalline anisotropy can be exploited to counteract shape demagnetization for a stabilized low bias field operation in the favourable Damon-Eshbach geometry with high group velocities and decay lengths. Together with the proven half-metallicity and ultralow Gilbert damping, this research establishes $\mathrm{Co_2MnSi}$ as a robust, scalable platform towards bias-field-free nonlinear half-metal magnonics.

### [108] [Ferroelectric-tunable quantum nonlinearity of chiral Bloch electrons in a moiré system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03497)
*Zitian Pan,Jundong Zhu,Yu Hong,Jingwei Dong,Dongxia Shi,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Luojun Du,Wei Yang,Guangyu Zhang*

TL;DR: 本文在六方氮化硼（hBN）封装的扭曲双层石墨烯莫尔异质结中，展示了滑动铁电性对量子非线性输运的铁电控制，发现极化强度在1.7-200 K范围内与温度无关，而成核时间呈热激活行为，并实现了铁电可切换的非线性霍尔效应，建立了滑动铁电体与量子几何属性（Berry曲率）之间的直接耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管范德华材料中的滑动铁电性（sliding ferroelectricity）在鲁棒存储器件设计中展现出巨大潜力，但其热力学行为以及与某些量子效应的耦合仍未被充分探索。

Method: 采用hBN封装的扭曲双层石墨烯莫尔异质结（twisted double-bilayer graphene moiré heterostructure），通过电输运和光学二次谐波产生（second harmonic generation, SHG）测量确认铁电性源于顶部hBN中的菱方堆垛（rhombohedral stacking）。

Conclusion: 研究结果确立了滑动铁电体作为研究电可编程Berry曲率物理的平台，展示了滑动铁电性与量子几何属性之间的直接耦合。

Abstract: Sliding ferroelectricity in van der Waals materials shows great potential for designing robust memory devices. However, its thermodynamic behaviors and the coupling with certain quantum effects remain largely unexplored. Here, we demonstrate ferroelectric control over quantum nonlinear transport in a hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) encapsulated twisted double-bilayer graphene moiré heterostructure. The ferroelectricity is attributed to the presence of rhombohedral stacking in the top hBN, confirmed by both electrical transport and optical second harmonic generation (SHG) measurements. Remarkably, the polarization magnitude remains temperature-independent across 1.7-200 K, while nucleation time exhibits thermally activated behavior, decreasing with increasing temperature. Furthermore, we demonstrate a ferroelectric-switchable nonlinear Hall effect, attributed to the chiral scattering induced by Berry curvature, with outstanding fatigue-resistant and nonvolatility, demonstrating direct coupling between sliding ferroelectricity and quantum geometric properties. Our results establish sliding ferroelectrics as a platform for exploring electrically programmable Berry curvature physics.

### [109] [Mechanochemical Nano-Writing of an Atomically Thin Metal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03710)
*Shuai Zhang,Yanyu Jia,Atanu Samanta,Yutian Bao,Haosen Guan,Zhaoyi Joy Zheng,Guangming Cheng,Ting Liu,Cangyu Qu,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Nan Yao,Ashlie Martini,Leslie Schoop,Andrew M. Rappe,Sanfeng Wu,Robert W. Carpick*

TL;DR: 本研究展示了一种利用原子力显微镜（AFM）针尖施加的局部机械力，在二维范德华（vdW）异质结中实现材料合成与纳米级图案化，并成功制备出原子级超薄超导体 Pd7MoTe2。机械力可指数级加速反应动力学，将合成温度从约200°C降低至近室温，并通过有限元模拟与第一性原理计算揭示了应力辅助的化学吸附机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用原子力显微镜（atomic force microscope, AFM）针尖对二维双层 MoTe2 与邻近 Pd 源构成的范德华（van der Waals, vdW）封装堆叠结构施加局部机械力，实现 2D Pd7MoTe2 的生长与纳米图案化，横向分辨率达 50 nm。结合有限元模拟（finite element simulations）、密度泛函理论（DFT）与从头算巨正则蒙特卡洛（ab-initio grand canonical Monte Carlo）计算分析机制。

Result: 机械力按照 Eyring 应力辅助热激活模型（Eyring's stress-assisted thermal activation model）指数级加速反应动力学，将合成温度从约200°C降至近室温。计算表明，针尖诱导的压缩力促进了 Pd 在拉伸应力作用下的 MoTe2 表面的化学吸附，最终转化为均匀的 Pd7MoTe2。

Abstract: Mechanical energy accelerates many physicochemical processes, including materials syntheses that are hard to produce with thermal energy alone. However, physical understanding connecting applied mechanical forces with internal stresses and ensuing reaction mechanisms is lacking. Here we demonstrate mechanical force-enabled synthesis and nanoscale patterning to metallize a two-dimensional (2D) material, producing an atomically-thin superconducting material. Localized force applied by atomic force microscope tips to van der Waals (vdW) encapsulated stacks of 2D bilayer MoTe2 and adjacent source Pd guides 2D Pd7MoTe2 growth with 50 nm lateral resolution. Force accelerates reaction kinetics exponentially per Eyring's stress-assisted thermal activation model, reducing synthesis temperatures from ~200 °C to near-room temperature. Finite element simulations, density functional theory, and ab-initio grand canonical Monte Carlo calculations show that tip-induced compression facilitates Pd chemisorption to tensile-strained MoTe2 that converts to uniform Pd7MoTe2. This demonstrates a new, generalizable paradigm for nanoscale synthesis of quantum materials, and high-precision engineering of superconductivity.

Winkler,David J. van Woerkom,Brian Paquelet Wuetz,Cécile X. Yu,Emrah Yucelen,Jesús Herranz Zamorano,Roland Zeisel,Guoji Zheng,A. M. Zimmerman*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过实验验证了拓扑量子计算中激发隙（excitation gap）越大器件性能越好的原理。在InAs-Pb tetron器件中，用高能隙超导体铅替代铝提升了拓扑相的鲁棒性，并开发了射频测量技术实现微电子伏特（μeV）精度的低能态能量分裂测量。实验观察到h/2e周期性双峰量子电容位移，特征宇称切换时间约20秒，远超典型量子比特操作时间（微秒量级），讨论了其对泡利测量（Pauli measurements）保真度的潜在影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑量子计算（topological quantum computing）的核心承诺是增大激发隙可以显著提升器件性能，但该原理此前缺乏直接的实验验证。本工作旨在通过在超导体-半导体混合器件中用更高能隙的超导体铅替代铝，实验检验这一原理，并开发适用于规模化调测的精密测量技术。

Method: 基于InAs-Pb tetron器件，采用干涉式单次宇称测量（interferometric single-shot parity measurements）；开发射频（rf）测量技术，以微电子伏特精度分辨低能线端态（low-energy wire-end states）并直接测量其能量分裂；在多tetron阵列中通过可控切换线宇称（wire parity），测量耦合于干涉环路中混合纳米线（hybrid nanowire）的量子点（quantum dot）上的量子电容（quantum capacitance）变化。

Result: 观察到h/2e周期性的双峰（bimodal）量子电容位移；特征宇称切换时间约20秒，部分实例达到分钟量级，远长于典型量子比特操作时间（微秒量级）。

Conclusion: 高能隙超导体铅替代铝确实提升了拓扑相的鲁棒性，验证了增大激发隙改善器件性能的原理；极长的宇称寿命对泡利测量保真度（fidelity of Pauli measurements）具有潜在积极意义。

Abstract: A central promise of topological quantum computing is that increasing the excitation gap improves device performance significantly. Here, we experimentally validate this principle in an InAs--Pb tetron device via interferometric single-shot parity measurements. By replacing aluminum with the higher-gap superconductor lead in our superconductor-semiconductor hybrid devices, we have improved the robustness of our topological phase. In addition, to enable fast and precise bring-up at scale, we have developed an rf measurement technique that resolves low-energy wire-end states and directly measures their energy splitting with $μ\text{eV}$ precision. We employ this technique to bring up a device in a multi-tetron array and perform parity measurements of one of the tetron's hybrid nanowires (NWs). By controllably switching the wire parity, we observe $h/2e$-periodic bimodal shifts in the quantum capacitance of a quantum dot coupled to the hybrid nanowire in an interference loop. Further time-resolved measurements reveal a characteristic parity switching time of $\sim 20$ s with some instances reaching minute-scale. Such extremely long parity lifetimes are orders of magnitude longer than typical qubit operation times, which are on the order of $μ\text{s}$. Finally, we discuss potential implications for the fidelity of Pauli measurements.

### [111] [Emergent Hall viscosity in the integer quantum Hall phases of graphene-like systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03932)
*M. Selch,M. A. Zubkov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文明确区分了两种霍尔粘度（Hall viscosity）：一种对应应变场，另一种对应涌现的维拜因/度规场（vielbein/metric field），并统一为“涌现霍尔粘度”（emergent Hall viscosity）。以石墨烯体系为例，作者在整数量子霍尔态（integer quantum Hall states）下计算了半金属相与Semenoff半导体相的涌现霍尔粘度，利用格林函数（Green function）与Wigner-Weyl演算（Wigner-Weyl calculus）推导了平移与旋转对称性下的拓扑不变量（topological invariants），并讨论了实验提取的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献中广泛讨论的是基于引力/维拜因-度规框架下的“几何”霍尔粘度（geometric Hall viscosity），但作者指出还存在一项与霍尔电导率（Hall conductivity）成正比的“电子”霍尔粘度（electronic Hall viscosity），源于涌现应变诱导规范场（emergent strain induced gauge field）。因此需要将两者统一处理，并明确其在不同体系中的区分与贡献。

Method: 论文通过格林函数表示与Wigner-Weyl演算方法，在平移与旋转对称性条件下导出涌现霍尔粘度中的拓扑不变量；针对石墨烯体系，在半金属（semimetal）与Semenoff半导体相中分别计算了整数量子霍尔态下的涌现霍尔粘度，并在半导体相中与非相对论极限（non-relativistic limit）进行比较。

Result: 成功将几何霍尔粘度与电子霍尔粘度统一为涌现霍尔粘度；在石墨烯半金属相和Semenoff半导体相的整数量子霍尔态下给出了明确表达式；发现两种拓扑不变量参与了涌现霍尔粘度的构成；在半导体相中给出了与非相对论极限的对比结果。

Conclusion: 论文为涌现霍尔粘度提供了统一的定义与计算框架，指出该物理量在石墨烯类体系中可由两种拓扑不变量刻画，并展望了在实验中提取涌现霍尔粘度的可行途径。

Abstract: We explicitly distinguish Hall viscosity as defined relative to the strain field vs. relative to an emergent vielbein or metric field and discuss it for graphene-like systems. Aside from the gravitational or vielbein/metric related ``geometric'' Hall viscosity prevailing throughout the literature, a contribution proportional to the Hall conductivity, the ``electronic'' Hall viscosity, due to the emergent strain induced gauge field exists. We unify both contributions within the ``emergent'' Hall viscosity, determine it explicitly for graphene in the semimetal and Semenoff semiconducting phases for integer quantum Hall states and in the latter case compare it to its non-relativistic limit. Under these circumstances two topological invariants enter the emergent Hall viscosity in the presence of translational and rotational symmetry which we derive in the Green function representation of Wigner-Weyl calculus. We discuss experimental perspectives for extracting the emergent Hall viscosity.

</details>

### [112] [20 ps Non-Destructive Read and 1 ns Write Operations at <5 V in Ferroelectric HfO2/ZrO2 Non-Volatile Memories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03677)

Method: 将HfO₂/ZrO₂铁电纳米层同时集成于CMOS的后道工序（BEOL）以及SiO₂/Si衬底上；利用铁电的部分翻转（partial ferroelectric switching）增强耐久性；引入一种基于20 ps电脉冲的非破坏性读出方法，通过测量极化依赖泄漏电流（polarization-dependent leakage current）实现超快读出。

Conclusion: 实验发现读出频率高于1 MHz时MC窗口会塌缩，但通过提出的基于20 ps脉冲的极化依赖泄漏电流测量方法，可克服这一速度限制，为铁电存储器在高速、低能耗存内计算中的应用提供新途径。

Abstract: Achieving low-voltage, nanosecond multi-level programming and non-destructive read-out of ferroelectric non-volatile memories (NVM) is critical for analog in-memory computing architectures relying on ferroelectric capacitive devices (FeCap). We integrate HfO2/ZrO2 ferroelectric nanolayers concurrently in the BEOL of CMOS and on SiO2/Si, achieving nanosecond multilevel switching with programming voltages below 5 V. Partial ferroelectric switching enhances FeCap endurance above 1011 cycles, leading to MemCapacitance (MC) states with non-destructive read-out and 10-year retention. However, experiments reveal the collapse of the MC window for read frequencies above 1 MHz. To overcome this speed limit, we introduce a novel, non-destructive readout methodology. Using electrical pulses with widths down to 20 ps, below the RC time constant of the FeCaps, we enable measurement of the polarization-dependent leakage current, providing ultrafast and non-destructive read operations at only 14 fJ.

### [113] [The Inverted Dirac-Moshinsky Oscillator in $(1+1)$ Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02637)
*Kevin Hernández,Marcos Orellana-Iraheta,William Larín-Escobar*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文推导并分析了(1+1)维反演狄拉克-莫辛斯基振子（IDMO）的精确解，得到了连续谱和复能量Gamow共振，并揭示了其真空不稳定性与Schwinger效应的类比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在(1+1)维时空下，通过规范替代 $p \to p + imωβx$ 从标准狄拉克模型构造反演狄拉克-莫辛斯基振子（IDMO），并研究其精确可解性及物理性质。

Method: 利用解析求解方法，将上旋量分量化为含有复谱参数 $λ= (E^2-m^2)/(2mω)+i/2$ 的Weber方程，解为复数阶 $ν= λ- 1/2$ 的抛物柱函数 $D_ν(ξ)$；并发展了三种归一化方案。

Result: 物理谱为纯连续谱（$|E|>m$），无离散束缚态；识别出离散Gamow共振 $E_n^\pm = \pm\sqrt{m^2+(2n+1)mω-imω}$ 作为预解式的极点；负能区描述虚部为正的反粒子反共振，标志真空不稳定性与自发对产生。

Conclusion: IDMO的代数结构由 $SU(1,1)$ 的主系列支配，哈密顿量满足 $\mathcal{PT}$ 对称性且在 $|E|>m$ 区间对称性未破缺；负能共振现象与Schwinger效应类似。

Abstract: We derive and analyze the exact solutions of the inverted Dirac-Moshinsky oscillator (IDMO) in $(1+1)$ dimensions, obtained from the standard model via the substitution $p \to p + imωβx$. The upper spinor component satisfies a Weber equation with complex spectral parameter $λ= (E^2-m^2)/(2mω)+i/2$, whose solutions are parabolic cylinder functions $D_ν(ξ)$ with complex order $ν= λ- 1/2$. The physical spectrum is purely continuous ($|E|>m$), with no discrete bound states. Three normalization schemes are developed, and the discrete Gamow resonances at $E_n^\pm = \pm\sqrt{m^2+(2n+1)mω-imω}$ are identified as poles of the resolvent. The negative-energy sector describes antiparticle anti-resonances whose positive imaginary part signals vacuum instability and spontaneous pair production, analogous to the Schwinger effect. The algebraic structure is governed by the principal series of $SU(1,1)$, and the Hamiltonian is $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetric with unbroken symmetry for $|E|>m$.

</details>


### [114] [Resonant delay in a stationary quantum clock: Lifting the threshold mask](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02718)
*Paul C. W. Davies,Damien A. Easson*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了Salecker-Wigner-Peres（SWP）稳态量子钟，证明其原始形式在连续谱边缘存在一个由低能散射数据决定的普适性 \(1/\sqrt{E}\) 发散项。通过引入阈值相减（threshold-subtracted）的钟观测量，可分离出普适的阈值运动学贡献与共振延迟贡献，从而在传输共振附近得到预期的局部洛伦兹（Lorentzian）线形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子穿越时间（quantum transit time）长期以来存在多种不等价定义（如相位时间、驻留时间、量子钟构造），亟需厘清不同观测量之间的物理关系，特别是稳态量子钟在连续谱边缘的奇异行为及其与共振延迟的区分。

Method: 以Salecker-Wigner-Peres稳态量子钟为散射观测量，基于一维实紧支撑势（real compactly supported one-dimensional potentials）推导钟时间表达式；采用阈值相减（threshold-subtracted）方法构造新观测量；通过方势阱、对称势垒-势阱-势垒腔体及非对称两步吸引势阱进行解析和数值验证。

Result: 原始稳态Peres钟在连续谱边缘存在普适的 \(1/\sqrt{E}\) 项，系数由低能散射数据固定。阈值相减后，共振峰仅以 \(\varepsilon^{-1/2}\) 增长，而未相减的阈值本底以 \(\varepsilon^{-3/2}\) 增长。与驻留时间（dwell time）和Wigner相位延迟（Wigner phase delay）的比较表明，相减后的钟具有预期的洛伦兹（Lorentzian）线形。

Conclusion: 阈值相减后的稳态量子钟可有效分离普适的阈值运动学效应与极依赖共振结构的延迟效应，为量子穿越时间的定义和共振分析提供了新的可靠观测量。

Abstract: Quantum transit times have a long history of inequivalent definitions, including phase times, dwell times, and quantum-clock constructions. In this context we revisit the Salecker--Wigner--Peres stationary quantum clock as a phase-sensitive scattering observable, with clock time defined by the energy derivative of the transmission phase shift across the interaction region. For real compactly supported one-dimensional potentials, we show that the raw stationary Peres clock generically contains a universal \(1/\sqrt{E}\) continuum-edge term whose coefficient is fixed by low-energy scattering data. For the attractive square well, this threshold singularity is inherited from the vanishing exterior momentum and the associated scattering matching, rather than from resonant delay itself. We derive the exact stationary clock time for the square well and introduce a new threshold-subtracted clock observable. Away from exceptional zero-energy tuning, the subtraction removes the universal low-energy term and isolates the resonant contribution. Comparison with the dwell time and the transmission Wigner phase delay shows that the threshold-subtracted clock acquires the expected local Lorentzian form near isolated transmission resonances. Near the continuum edge, if \(\varepsilon\) denotes the detuning from threshold, the resonant peak grows only as \(\varepsilon^{-1/2}\), whereas the unsubtracted threshold background grows as \(\varepsilon^{-3/2}\). A symmetric barrier--well--barrier cavity and a numerical asymmetric two-step attractive well provide complementary controls. The result is a new threshold-subtracted stationary-clock candidate that separates universal threshold kinematics from pole-sensitive resonant delay.

</details>


### [115] [Triple exceptional point with unitary paths of unfolding in a three-site fermionic Swanson-like model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03789)
*Bijan Bagchi,Aritra Ghosh,Miloslav Znojil*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种费米子三-site推广的Swanson模型（bosonic Swanson model的费米子类比），作为精确可解的五参数量子力学幺正演化（unitary evolution）实例，该演化最终导致可观测性丧失并落入三阶例外点（exceptional-point singularity, EP3）。简并时刻具有显式单参数形式，其幺正相容邻域（即通往EP3的通道）同样以闭合形式给出。精确、数值误差无关的可解性至关重要，因为另一个被避免的虚假能级交叉（avoided false energy-level crossing）恰好发生在真实EP3奇点附近。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索费米子版本的三-site Swanson模型作为精确可解实例，研究量子幺正演化过程中可观测性丧失并落入三阶例外点（EP3）的机制。

Method: 采用费米子三-site推广的Swanson模型，基于五参数可解框架，通过闭合形式推导简并时刻及其幺正相容邻域（corridor of access to EP3）。

Result: 发现EP3简并时刻具有显式单参数形式；通往EP3的通道（即幺正相容邻域）以闭合形式给出；在真实EP3奇点附近存在一个被避免的虚假能级交叉（avoided false energy-level crossing）。

Conclusion: 精确的、不依赖数值误差的可解性对于正确识别真实EP3与虚假能级交叉至关重要，该模型为研究例外点奇点（exceptional-point singularity）提供了清晰的理论实例。

Abstract: A fermionic three-site generalization of the popular bosonic Swanson model is studied as providing an exactly solvable five-parametric example of the quantum-mechanical unitary-evolution process leading to an ultimate loss of the observability and fall in an exceptional-point singularity (EP3). The instant of degeneracy is found to have an explicit one-parametric form. Its unitarity-compatible vicinity (i.e., the corridor of access to EP3) is also specified in closed form. The exact, numerical-error-independent solvability is found essential due to another, avoided, false energy-level crossing which is found to occur not too far from the true EP3 singularity.

</details>


### [116] [The bulk spectral gap is semi-decidable: a convergent family of certified upper bounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03836)
*Xiangling Xu,Matthias Schötz,Jie Wang,Victor Magron,Igor Klep,Omar Fawzi,Marc-Olivier Renou*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一族通过求解半定规划（semidefinite programs）获得的体谱隙（bulk spectral gap）的可证上界（certified upper bounds），证明了体谱隙的半可判定性（semi-decidability），并将其应用于自旋-1/2 kagome晶格海森堡反铁磁体，得到了首个非平凡的可证上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下体谱隙的确定是量子多体物理（quantum many-body physics）的核心难题：现有严格方法局限于特殊情形，而变分数值方法通常只提供估计值而非可证界（certified bounds）。因此需要一种能提供严格上界且可任意收紧的方法。

Method: 通过求解一系列半定规划（semidefinite programs）来构造体谱隙的可证上界族；随着计算资源的增加，这些上界可以任意紧密（arbitrarily tight）。

Result: 证明了体谱隙是半可判定的（semi-decidable），这与基于给定边界条件的有限系统序列的谱隙不可判定性（undecidability）结果形成对比。在对自旋-1/2 kagome晶格海森堡反铁磁体的应用中获得首个非平凡的可证上界。

Conclusion: 该方法为量子多体系统的体谱隙提供了严格且可计算的上界框架，证明了体谱隙在计算复杂性上属于半可判定问题，并在具体物理模型中展示了可行性。

Abstract: Determining spectral gaps in the thermodynamic limit is a central challenge in quantum many-body physics. Existing rigorous methods are largely limited to special settings, while variational numerical approaches typically provide estimates rather than certified bounds. Here we introduce a complete family of certified upper bounds on the bulk spectral gap of quantum many-body systems. These upper bounds are obtained by solving a series of semidefinite programs and they become arbitrarily tight at the cost of more computational resources. This shows that the bulk spectral gap is semi-decidable, in contrast to undecidability results for alternative notions of spectral gap based on sequences of finite systems with prescribed boundary conditions. As a proof of principle, we apply our algorithm to the spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ kagome lattice Heisenberg antiferromagnet and obtain, to our knowledge, the first nontrivial certified upper bounds on its bulk spectral gap.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文将上述实验方案构建为量子-引力模拟游戏（quantum-gravitational imitation games），重点分析机械振子（mechanical oscillators）之间的引力相互作用如何实现任意量子态的隐形传态。

Abstract: Gravity is the most apparent force in our everyday existence. Yet its fundamental nature remains the most opaque of the known interactions. This gap in our understanding is, in large part, due to the weakness of the gravitational interaction, which makes its empirical probing exceedingly hard. Nevertheless, on the backdrop of rapid advances in quantum technologies, hope has mounted that tests of the quantum nature of gravity could be realized in tabletop experiments. In this essay, we frame these recently proposed tests as quantum-gravitational imitation games. In particular, we examine how gravitational interactions among mechanical oscillators enable the teleportation of arbitrary quantum states and how this can inform fundamental tests of gravity.

### [118] [Fracton Topological Holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03582)
*Yu-Tao Hu,Jie-Yu Zhang,Peng Ye*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了分形子拓扑全息术（fracton topological holography, FTH），将拓扑全息术（topological holography, TH）从液体的拓扑序推广到分形子稳定子码（fracton stabilizer codes），构建了一个四阶段框架，并通过X-cube模型和Haah立方码两个典型例子展示了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将拓扑全息术（topological holography, TH）从液体的拓扑序扩展至分形子拓扑序（fracton topological orders），以统一理解和组织这类具有亚广泛激发（sub-extensive excitations）的量子系统的对称性与对偶性（dualities）。

Method: 构建了一个通用的四阶段框架：(1) 制备体态模型并计算其激发；(2) 确定边界数据及允许的有隙拓扑边界（gapped top boundaries）；(3) 识别低能保持算子代数及其对称性、关系与扭转数据（twist data）；(4) 在不同拓扑边界之间切换以比较诱导的边界描述。X-cube模型和Haah立方码分别作为类型-I和类型-II的例子进行了具体构造。

Result: 对于X-cube模型，平滑与粗糙拓扑边界均诱导出横向场plaquette Ising模型，但子系统的对称性与扭转数据互换，边界切换通过线性深度的局域酉顺序量子电路（sequential quantum circuit, SQC）实现。对于Haah立方码，利用Laurent-多项式稳定子形式体系分析了自然(Z)和(X)拓扑边界，诱导出两个二维量子比特系统，局域上互换广义plaquette Ising项与横向场项，非局域上呈现对称性–关系对偶（symmetry–relation duality）。

Conclusion: FTH是TH到类型-I和类型-II分形子序的真正推广，为组织和理解对偶性提供了具体的框架，并有望为发现新对偶性提供系统性途径。

Abstract: Topological holography (TH), or SymTFT, realizes symmetries and dualities of a quantum system as boundary data of a topological bulk in one higher dimension. We formulate fracton topological holography (FTH), extending this mechanism from liquid topological orders to fracton stabilizer codes. The construction is organized as a general four-stage framework: prepare the bulk model and compute its excitations, determine boundary data and admissible gapped top boundaries, identify the low-energy preserving operator algebra together with its symmetry, relation, and twist data, and then switch among top boundaries to compare the induced boundary descriptions. As a type-I example, we develop FTH for the X-cube model with smooth and rough top boundaries; for a minimal effective Hamiltonian, both yield transverse-field plaquette Ising models, with exchanged subsystem symmetry and twist data, and the boundary switch is implemented by a linear-depth local unitary sequential quantum circuit (SQC). As a type-II example, we formulate FTH for Haah's cubic code in the Laurent-polynomial stabilizer formalism and analyze the natural $(Z)$ and $(X)$ top boundaries, which induce two two-dimensional qubit systems related locally by exchanging generalized plaquette Ising and transverse-field terms and nonlocally by a symmetry--relation duality. These results show that FTH is a genuine extension of TH to both type-I and type-II fracton orders. FTH therefore provides a concrete framework for organizing and understanding duality, with the prospect of offering a systematic route to new dualities.

</details>


### [119] [Subspace-selective unitary manipulation based on the Hilbert-space symmetric structures in the multiple-quantum operator algebra spaces in the quantum-computing speedup theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03859)
*Xijia Miao*

Abstract: The quantum-computing speedup theory considers the symmetric structures and properties of quantum systems as the fundamental Quantum-Computing-Speedup (QCS) resources which are responsible for exponentially speeding up quantum computing and simulating. At present a large and important problem is how to make use of the fundamental QCS resources to speed up essentially quantum computing and simulating. Here the author makes a great effort toward solving this important problem. The theoretical research work in this paper is mainly divided into the two Parts I and II. The Part I investigates mainly the multiple-quantum operator algebra spaces. And the relationships are analyzed among the multiple-quantum operator algebra spaces, quantum simulating for the unitary time-evolutional processes, and the fundamental QCS resources which exist in the different kinds of basic quantum spaces: the multiple-quantum operator algebra space, the density operator space, and the Hilbert space. It concludes that the multiple-quantum operator algebra space must be positioned as the central place where the QCS resources are exploited to speed up quantum computing and simulating. The Part II investigates mainly the subspace-selective unitary manipulation based on the Hilbert-space symmetric structures. Recognize that the multiple-quantum operator algebra space is the central place. Then those QCS resources original from the Hilbert space (a quantum-state space) must be explicitly taken into account in the multiple-quantum operator algebra space (a linear operator space). This is an important problem. The subspace-selective unitary manipulation is able to solve this problem. It aims to harness the fundamental QCS resources original from the Hilbert space to speed up quantum computing and simulating in the multiple-quantum operator algebra space.

</details>


### [120] [Probing information theoretic measures of nonlinear ultracold quantum gases using phase-space distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02656)
*Mariyah Ughradar,Ramkumar Radhakrishnan,Siddharth Kumar Tiwari,Vikash Kumar Ojha*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文利用维格纳（Wigner）和胡西米（Husimi）准概率分布，研究了由Gross-Pitaevskii方程描述的谐波囚禁玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）的相空间信息论特性，发现更强的排斥相互作用导致相空间离域化增强，且Wigner与Husimi表示在强相互作用下趋于经典化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将相空间分布（phase space distributions）与信息论度量（information theoretic measures）相结合，系统研究谐波囚禁玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体的量子-经典过渡行为，特别是相互作用强度对相空间结构的影响。

Method: 从平均场基态波函数（mean field ground state wavefunction）出发，构建Wigner和Husimi准概率分布及其位置和动量空间边缘分布，据此计算Shannon熵、Wehrl熵、Rényi熵、Fisher信息（Fisher information）、累积与交叉累积剩余熵、互信息（mutual information）以及Kullback-Leibler、Jeffreys、Cauchy-Schwarz和Rényi散度等一整套信息论度量。

Result: 更强的排斥相互作用导致相空间离域化（delocalization）增加，表现为Shannon熵和Wehrl熵单调增长；Fisher信息呈现互补趋势——位置空间增加而动量空间减少，符合全局Fisher不确定界（Fisher uncertainty bound）；Rényi熵和散度度量显示，从Wigner表示过渡到Husimi表示时，非经典干涉被系统性抑制，相空间结构趋于经典化；基于Wigner和Husimi的互信息在强相互作用下收敛。

Conclusion: Gross-Pitaevskii框架处理多体态为平均场乘积形式，因此该工作中计算的互信息衡量的是有效单体分布中相空间共轭变量之间的统计依赖关系，而非真正的粒子-粒子纠缠（particle-particle entanglement）。

Abstract: We use phase space distributions, specifically the Wigner and Husimi quasi probability distributions, to study harmonically trapped Bose--Einstein condensate described by the Gross Pitaevskii equation. From the mean field ground state wavefunction we construct both distributions and their position and momentum space marginals and we use these to compute a comprehensive set of information theoretic measures: Shannon, Wehrl, and Rényi entropies; Fisher information; cumulative and cross cumulative residual entropies; mutual information; and Kullback--Leibler, Jeffreys, Cauchy Schwarz, and Rényi divergences. Studying these quantities as a function of the $s$-wave scattering length for a representative Rb-85 condensate, we find that stronger repulsive interactions drive increased phase space delocalization, seen by a monotonic growth of Shannon and Wehrl entropies, while the Fisher information shows the complementary trend -- increasing in position space and decreasing in momentum space in a manner consistent with the global Fisher uncertainty bound. Rényi entropies and divergence measures further reveal a systematic suppression of non classical interference and a shift toward more classical phase space structure in moving from the Wigner to the Husimi representation, with Wigner and Husimi based mutual informations converging at larger interaction strength. We note that, because the Gross Pitaevskii framework treats the many body state as a mean field product, the mutual information computed here quantifies statistical dependence between the conjugate phase space variables of the effective one body distribution rather than genuine particle particle entanglement.

</details>


### [121] [Trapping 11,000 Atoms in a Tweezer Array Generated by a Single Metasurface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02715)
*Yuqing Wang,Zhongchi Zhang,Tao Zhang,Yuxuan Liao,Hanteng Wang,Ye Tian,Binjie Ji,Yujia Wu,Luming Ma,Chen Qing,Chengshu Li,Wei Zhang,Yidong Huang,Wenjun Zhang,Xue Feng,Wenlan Chen,Hui Zhai*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用单个超表面（metasurface）在直径约2厘米的区域内生成整个光镊阵列，实现了11,000个独立原子的鲁棒囚禁，首次将量子计算平台的可用量子比特（qubit）资源提升至数万规模，并通过逾渗相变（percolation phase transition）的统计理论表征了随机加载的原子阵列。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用容错量子计算机（universal fault-tolerant quantum computer）面临的核心挑战是物理量子比特数的可扩展性（scalability）。原子阵列量子计算机因原子量子比特的同一性而具有内在可扩展性，但其可用量子比特资源主要受限于可被囚禁和操控的原子数目。

Method: 采用一个直径约2厘米的单个超表面（metasurface）生成整个光镊阵列，无需使用显微物镜（microscope objective），从而最大化激光功率效率（laser-power efficiency）。大孔径提供了约1.5厘米的工作距离（working distance），使超表面可置于真空腔外，避免了真空内操作的技术复杂性。

Result: 成功实现了11,000个独立原子在光镊阵列（tweezer array）中的鲁棒囚禁，使可用量子比特资源首次在所有量子计算平台中达到数万规模。此外，利用逾渗相变（percolation phase transition）的统计理论对随机加载的原子阵列进行了表征。

Conclusion: 该工作为迈向万量子比特（10,000-qubit）规模的量子计算机迈出了重要的第一步。

Abstract: The scalability of physical qubit numbers is a central challenge toward a universal fault-tolerant quantum computer. The inherent scalability of atom array quantum computers stems from the identical nature of atomic qubits, so the available qubit resource is primarily limited by the number of atoms that can be trapped and controlled. Here, we robustly trap 11,000 individual atoms in a tweezer array, thereby enabling the available qubit resource to reach the tens-of-thousands scale for the first time among all quantum computation platforms. This advance is enabled by a single metasurface, approximately 2 cm in diameter, that generates the entire tweezer array without the need for microscope objectives, thereby maximizing laser-power efficiency. The large aperture ensures a working distance of about 1.5 cm, allowing the metasurface to be placed outside the vacuum cell and avoiding the technical complications of in-vacuum operation. We further characterize the randomly loaded atom array using the statistical theory of percolation phase transitions. This work takes an important first step toward a quantum computer at the 10,000-qubit scale.
